Likewise the wayfarer (ibn al-sabil): he is the traveler passing through a land who has nothing with him to help him continue his journey. He is given from the charitable funds what suffices him to reach his homeland, even if he has wealth elsewhere. The same ruling applies to one who intends to set out on a journey from his own land and has nothing with him: he is given from the zakat funds what suffices for his going and returning. The evidence for this is the verse itself, and what was narrated by Imam Abu Dawud and Ibn Majah from the hadith of Ma'mar, from Zayd ibn Aslam, from Ata' ibn Yasar, from Abu Sa'id, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Charity (sadaqah) is not permissible for a wealthy person except for five: the one employed to collect it, or a man who purchased it with his own wealth, or a debtor, or one fighting in the path of Allah, or a poor person to whom charity was given and who then gives a gift from it to a wealthy person."

This was narrated by the two Sufyans, from Zayd ibn Aslam, from Ata', as a mursal (report missing a link in the chain). And Abu Dawud has it from Atiyyah al-Awfi, from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Charity is not permissible for a wealthy person except in the path of Allah, or for the wayfarer, or for a poor neighbor who gives you a gift or invites you."

His saying, {an obligation from Allah}, means: a ruling determined by Allah's determination, His ordaining, and His apportioning. {And Allah is Knowing, Wise}, meaning: Knowing of the outward and inward aspects of matters and of the true interests of His servants; Wise in what He does, says, legislates, and rules by. There is no god but He, and no lord besides Him.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى اعْتِرَاضَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ الْجَهَلَةِ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ وَلَمْزَهُمْ إِيَّاهُ فِي قَسْم الصَّدَقَاتِ، بَيَّنَ تَعَالَى أَنَّهُ هُوَ الَّذِي قَسَمَهَا وَبَيَّنَ حُكْمَهَا، وَتَوَلَّى أَمْرَهَا بِنَفْسِهِ، وَلَمْ يَكلْ قَسْمها إِلَى أَحَدٍ غَيْرِهِ، فَجَزَّأَهَا لِهَؤُلَاءِ الْمَذْكُورِينَ، كَمَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ فِي سُنَنِهِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ زِيَادِ بْنِ أَنْعَمَ -وَفِيهِ ضَعْفٌ -عَنْ زِيَادِ بْنِ نُعَيْمٍ، عَنْ زِيَادِ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ الصُدَائي، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: أَتَيْتُ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ فَبَايَعْتُهُ، فَأَتَى رَجُلٌ فَقَالَ: أَعْطِنِي مِنَ الصَّدَقَةِ فَقَالَ لَهُ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَمْ يَرْضَ بِحُكْمِ نَبِيٍّ وَلَا غَيْرِهِ فِي الصَّدَقَاتِ حَتَّى حَكَمَ فِيهَا هُوَ، فَجَزَّأَهَا ثَمَانِيَةَ أَصْنَافٍ، فَإِنْ كُنْتَ مِنْ تِلْكَ الْأَجْزَاءِ أَعْطَيْتُكَ" وَقَدِ اخْتَلَفَ الْعُلَمَاءُ فِي هَذِهِ الْأَصْنَافِ الثَّمَانِيَةِ: هَلْ يَجِبُ اسْتِيعَابُ الدَّفْعِ إِلَيْهَا أَوْ إِلَى مَا أَمْكَنَ مِنْهَا؟ عَلَى قَوْلَيْنِ:

أَحَدُهُمَا: أَنَّهُ يَجِبُ ذَلِكَ، وَهُوَ قَوْلُ الشَّافِعِيِّ وَجَمَاعَةٍ.

وَالثَّانِي: أَنَّهُ لَا يَجِبُ اسْتِيعَابُهَا، بَلْ يَجُوزُ الدَّفْعُ إِلَى وَاحِدٍ مِنْهَا، وَيُعْطَى جميعَ الصَّدَقَةِ مَعَ وُجُودِ الْبَاقِينَ. وَهُوَ قَوْلُ مَالِكٍ وَجَمَاعَةٍ مِنَ السَّلَفِ وَالْخَلَفِ، مِنْهُمْ: عُمَرُ، وَحُذَيْفَةُ، وَابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَأَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَير، وَمَيْمُونُ بْنُ مِهْران.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَهُوَ قَوْلُ عَامَّةِ أَهْلِ الْعِلْمِ، وَعَلَى هَذَا فَإِنَّمَا ذَكَرْتُ الْأَصْنَافَ هَاهُنَا لِبَيَانِ الْمَصْرَفِ لَا لِوُجُوبِ اسْتِيعَابِ الْإِعْطَاءِ.

وَلِوُجُوهِ الْحِجَاجِ وَالْمَآخِذِ مَكَانٌ غَيْرُ هَذَا، واللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَإِنَّمَا قَدَّمَ الْفُقَرَاءَ هَاهُنَا لِأَنَّهُمْ أَحْوَجُ مِنَ الْبَقِيَّةِ عَلَى الْمَشْهُورِ، لِشِدَّةِ فَاقَتِهِمْ وَحَاجَتِهِمْ، وَعِنْدَ أَبِي حَنِيفَةَ أَنَّ الْمِسْكِينَ أَسْوَأُ حَالًا مِنَ الْفَقِيرِ، وَهُوَ كَمَا قَالَ، قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي يَعْقُوبُ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عُلَيَّة، أَنْبَأَنَا ابْنُ عَوْن، عَنْ مُحَمَّدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ عُمَرُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: الْفَقِيرُ لَيْسَ بِالَّذِي لَا مَالَ لَهُ، وَلَكِنَّ الْفَقِيرَ الْأَخْلَقُ الْكَسْبِ. قَالَ ابْنُ عُلَيَّةَ: الْأَخْلَقُ: المحارَفُ عِنْدَنَا 

وَالْجُمْهُورُ عَلَى خِلَافِهِ. ورُوي عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وَالْحَسَنِ الْبَصْرِيِّ، وَابْنِ زَيْدٍ. وَاخْتَارَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ أَنَّ الْفَقِيرَ: هُوَ الْمُتَعَفِّفُ الَّذِي لَا يَسْأَلُ النَّاسَ شَيْئًا، وَالْمِسْكِينَ: هُوَ الَّذِي يَسْأَلُ وَيَطُوفُ وَيَتَّبِعُ النَّاسَ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: الْفَقِيرُ: مَنْ بِهِ زَمَانَةٌ، وَالْمِسْكِينُ: الصَّحِيحُ الْجِسْمِ.

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ: هُمْ فُقَرَاءُ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ. قَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ: يَعْنِي: وَلَا يُعْطَى الأعرابُ مِنْهَا شَيْئًا.

وَكَذَا رُوِيَ عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَير، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ أبْزَى.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمة: لَا تَقُولُوا لِفُقَرَاءِ الْمُسْلِمِينَ مَسَاكِينَ، وَإِنَّمَا الْمَسَاكِينُ مَسَاكِينُ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ.

وَلْنَذْكُرْ أَحَادِيثَ تَتَعَلَّقُ بِكُلٍّ مِنَ الْأَصْنَافِ الثَّمَانِيَةِ.

فَأَمَّا "الْفُقَرَاءُ"، فَعَنِ ابْنِ عَمْرٍو قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم: "لَا تَحِلُّ الصَّدَقَةُ لغَنِيٍّ وَلَا لِذِي مِرَّة سَويّ". رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ 

وَلِأَحْمَدَ أَيْضًا، وَالنَّسَائِيِّ، وَابْنِ مَاجَهْ عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، مِثْلَهُ 

وَعَنْ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَدِيِّ بْنِ الْخِيَارِ: أَنَّ رَجُلَيْنِ أَخْبَرَاهُ: أَنَّهُمَا أَتَيَا النَّبِيَّ ﷺ يَسْأَلَانِهِ مِنَ الصَّدَقَةِ، فَقَلَّبَ إِلَيْهِمَا الْبَصَرَ، فَرَآهُمَا جَلْدين، فَقَالَ: "إِنْ شِئْتُمَا أَعْطَيْتُكُمَا، وَلَا حَظَّ فِيهَا لِغَنِيٍّ وَلَا لِقَوِيٍّ مُكْتَسِبٍ".

رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ، وَأَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ بِإِسْنَادٍ جَيِّدٍ قَوِيٍّ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ فِي كِتَابِ الْجَرْحِ [وَالتَّعْدِيلِ: أَبُو بَكْرٍ الْعَبْسِيُّ قَالَ: قَرَأَ عُمَرُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: ﴿إِنَّمَا الصَّدَقَاتُ لِلْفُقَرَاءِ﴾ قَالَ: هُمْ أَهْلُ الْكِتَابِ] رَوَى عَنْهُ عُمَرُ بْنُ نَافِعٍ، سَمِعْتُ أَبِي يَقُولُ ذَلِكَ 

قُلْتُ: وَهَذَا قَوْلٌ غَرِيبٌ جِدًّا بِتَقْدِيرِ صِحَّةِ الْإِسْنَادِ، فَإِنَّ أَبَا بَكْرٍ هَذَا، وَإِنْ لَمْ يَنُصَّ أَبُو حَاتِمٍ عَلَى جَهَالَتِهِ، لَكِنَّهُ فِي حُكْمِ الْمَجْهُولِ.

وَأَمَّا الْمَسَاكِينُ: فَعَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "لَيْسَ الْمِسْكِينُ بِهَذَا الطَّوَّافِ الَّذِي يَطُوفُ عَلَى النَّاسِ، فتردُّه اللُّقْمَةُ وَاللُّقْمَتَانِ، وَالتَّمْرَةُ وَالتَّمْرَتَانِ". قَالُوا: فَمَا الْمِسْكِينُ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ قَالَ: "الَّذِي لَا يجدُ غِنًى يُغْنِيهِ، وَلَا يُفْطَن لَهُ فَيُتَصَدَّقُ عَلَيْهِ، وَلَا يَسْأَلُ النَّاسُ شَيْئًا".

رَوَاهُ الشَّيْخَانِ: الْبُخَارِيُّ وَمُسْلِمٌ وَأَمَّا الْعَامِلُونَ عَلَيْهَا: فَهُمُ الْجُبَاةُ وَالسُّعَاةُ يَسْتَحِقُّونَ مِنْهَا قِسْطًا عَلَى ذَلِكَ، وَلَا يَجُوزُ أَنْ يَكُونُوا مِنْ أَقْرِبَاءِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ الَّذِينَ تَحْرُمُ عَلَيْهِمُ الصَّدَقَةُ، لِمَا ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ عَنْ عَبْدِ الْمُطَّلِبِ بْنِ رَبِيعَةَ بْنِ الْحَارِثِ: أَنَّهُ انْطَلَقَ هُوَ وَالْفَضْلُ بْنُ عَبَّاسٍ يَسْأَلَانِ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ لِيَسْتَعْمِلَهُمَا عَلَى الصَّدَقَةِ، فَقَالَ: "إِنَّ الصَّدَقَةَ لَا تَحِلُّ لِمُحَمَّدٍ وَلَا لِآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ، إِنَّمَا هِيَ أَوْسَاخُ النَّاسِ" 

وَأَمَّا الْمُؤَلَّفَةُ قُلُوبُهُمْ: فَأَقْسَامٌ: مِنْهُمْ مَنْ يُعْطَى ليُسلم، كَمَا أَعْطَى النَّبِيُّ ﷺ صَفْوَانَ بْنَ أُمَيَّةَ مِنْ غَنَائِمِ حُنَيْنٍ، وَقَدْ كَانَ شَهِدَهَا مُشْرِكًا. قَالَ: فَلَمْ يَزَلْ يُعْطِينِي حَتَّى صَارَ أحبَّ النَّاسِ إليَّ بَعْدَ أَنْ كَانَ أَبْغَضَ النَّاسِ إِلَيَّ، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا زَكَرِيَّا بْنُ عَدِيٍّ، أنا ابْنُ الْمُبَارَكِ، عَنْ يُونُسَ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ الْمُسَيَّبِ، عَنْ صَفْوَانَ بْنِ أُمَيَّةَ قَالَ: أَعْطَانِي رسول الله صلى الله عليه وسلم يوم حُنَيْنٍ، وَإِنَّهُ لَأَبْغَضُ النَّاسِ إِلَيَّ، فَمَا زَالَ يُعْطِينِي حَتَّى صَارَ وَإِنَّهُ لَأَحَبُّ النَّاسِ إِلَيَّ.

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ يُونُسَ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، بِهِ 

وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يُعْطَى ليحسُن إِسْلَامُهُ، وَيَثْبُتَ قَلْبُهُ، كَمَا أَعْطَى يَوْمَ حُنَيْنٍ أَيْضًا جَمَاعَةً مِنْ

صَنَادِيدِ الطُّلَقَاءِ وَأَشْرَافِهِمْ: مِائَةً مِنَ الْإِبِلِ، مِائَةً مِنَ الْإِبِلِ وَقَالَ: "إِنِّي لَأُعْطِي الرَّجُلَ وَغَيْرُهُ أَحَبُّ إِلَيَّ مِنْهُ، مَخَافَةَ أَنْ يَكُبَّه اللَّهُ عَلَى وَجْهِهِ فِي نَارِ جَهَنَّمَ" 

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ: أَنَّ عَلِيًّا بَعَثَ إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ بذُهَيبة فِي تُرْبَتِهَا مِنَ الْيَمَنِ فَقَسَمَهَا بَيْنَ أَرْبَعَةِ نَفَرٍ: الْأَقْرَعِ بْنِ حَابِسٍ، وعُيَينة بْنِ بَدْرٍ، وَعَلْقَمَةَ بْنِ عُلاثة، وَزَيْدِ الْخَيْرِ، وَقَالَ: "أَتَأَلَّفُهُمْ" 

وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يُعطَى لِمَا يُرْجَى مِنْ إِسْلَامِ نُظَرَائِهِ. وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ يُعطَى لِيَجْبِيَ الصَّدَقَاتِ مِمَّنْ يَلِيهِ، أَوْ لِيَدْفَعَ عَنْ حَوزة الْمُسْلِمِينَ الضَّرَرَ مِنْ أَطْرَافِ الْبِلَادِ. وَمَحَلُّ تَفْصِيلِ هَذَا فِي كُتُبِ الْفُرُوعِ، واللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَهَلْ تُعْطَى الْمُؤَلَّفَةُ عَلَى الْإِسْلَامِ بَعْدَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ؟ فِيهِ خِلَافٌ، فرُوي عَنْ عُمَرَ، وَعَامِرٍ الشَّعْبِيِّ وَجَمَاعَةٍ: أَنَّهُمْ لَا يُعطَون بَعْدَهُ؛ لِأَنَّ اللَّهَ قَدْ أَعَزَّ الْإِسْلَامَ وَأَهْلَهُ، ومَكَّن لَهُمْ فِي الْبِلَادِ، وَأَذَلَّ لَهُمْ رِقَابَ الْعِبَادِ.

وَقَالَ آخَرُونَ: بَلْ يُعطَون؛ لِأَنَّهُ عَلَيْهِ الصَّلَاةُ وَالسَّلَامُ قَدْ أَعْطَاهُمْ بَعْدَ فَتْحِ مَكَّةَ وَكَسْرِ هَوازن، وَهَذَا أَمْرٌ قَدْ يَحْتَاجُ إِلَيْهِ فَيُصْرَفُ إِلَيْهِمْ.

وَأَمَّا الرِّقَابُ: فرُوي عَنِ الْحَسَنِ الْبَصْرِيِّ، وَمُقَاتِلِ بْنِ حَيَّانَ، وَعُمَرَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَير، والنَّخعي، والزُّهْرِيِّ، وَابْنِ زَيْدٍ: أَنَّهُمُ المكاتَبون، وَرُوِيَ عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيِّ نَحْوَهُ، وَهُوَ قَوْلُ الشَّافِعِيِّ وَاللَّيْثِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ، وَالْحَسَنُ: لَا بَأْسَ أَنْ تُعْتَقَ الرَّقَبَةُ مِنَ الزَّكَاةِ، وَهُوَ مَذْهَبُ الْإِمَامِ أَحْمَدَ بْنِ حَنْبَلٍ، وَمَالِكٍ، وَإِسْحَاقَ، أَيْ: إِنَّ الرِّقَابَ أَعَمُّ مِنْ أَنْ يُعْطَى الْمُكَاتَبُ، أَوْ يَشْتَرِيَ رَقَبَةً فَيُعْتِقَهَا اسْتِقْلَالًا. وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي ثَوَابِ الْإِعْتَاقِ وَفَكِّ الرَّقَبَةِ أَحَادِيثُ كَثِيرَةٌ، وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ يُعْتِقُ بِكُلِّ عُضْوٍ مِنْهَا عُضْوًا مِنْ مُعتقها حَتَّى الفَرْج بِالْفَرْجِ، وَمَا ذَاكَ إِلَّا لِأَنَّ الْجَزَاءَ مِنْ جِنْسِ الْعَمَلِ، ﴿وَمَا تُجْزَوْنَ إِلا مَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ:٣٩]

وَعَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ قَالَ: "ثَلَاثَةٌ حَقٌّ عَلَى اللَّهِ عونُهم: الْغَازِي فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، وَالْمُكَاتَبُ الَّذِي يُرِيدُ الْأَدَاءَ، وَالنَّاكِحُ الَّذِي يُرِيدُ الْعَفَافَ".

رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ وَأَهْلُ السُّنَنِ إِلَّا أَبَا دَاوُدَ 

وَفِي الْمُسْنَدِ عَنِ الْبَرَاءِ بْنِ عَازِبٍ قَالَ: جَاءَ رَجُلٌ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، دُلَّني عَلَى عَمَلٍ يُقَرِّبُنِي مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ وَيُبَاعِدُنِي مِنَ النَّارِ. فَقَالَ: "أَعْتِقِ النسَمة وَفُكَّ الرَّقَبَةَ". فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ الله، أو ليسا وَاحِدًا؟ قَالَ: "لَا عِتْقُ النَّسَمَةِ أَنْ تُفرد بِعِتْقِهَا، وَفَكُّ الرَّقَبَةِ أَنْ تُعِينَ فِي ثَمَنِهَا" 

وَأَمَّا الْغَارِمُونَ: فَهُمْ أَقْسَامٌ: فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ تَحَمَّلَ حَمَالَةً أَوْ ضَمِنَ دَيْنًا فَلَزِمَهُ فَأَجْحَفَ بِمَالِهِ، أَوْ غَرِمَ فِي أَدَاءِ دَيْنِهِ أَوْ فِي مَعْصِيَةٍ ثُمَّ تَابَ، فَهَؤُلَاءِ يُدْفَعُ إِلَيْهِمْ. وَالْأَصْلُ فِي هَذَا الْبَابِ حَدِيثُ قَبِيصة بْنِ مُخَارِقٍ الْهِلَالِيِّ قَالَ: تَحَمَّلْتُ حَمَالَةً فَأَتَيْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَسْأَلُهُ فِيهَا، فَقَالَ: "أَقِمْ حَتَّى تَأْتِيَنَا الصَّدَقَةُ، فَنَأْمُرَ لَكَ بِهَا". قَالَ: ثُمَّ قَالَ: "يَا قَبِيصة، إِنَّ الْمَسْأَلَةَ لَا تَحِلُّ إِلَّا لِأَحَدِ ثَلَاثَةٍ: رَجُلٍ تحمَّل حَمَالَةً فَحَلَّتْ لَهُ الْمَسْأَلَةُ حَتَّى يُصِيبَهَا، ثُمَّ يُمْسِكَ. وَرَجُلٍ أَصَابَتْهُ جَائِحَةٌ اجْتَاحَتْ مَالَهُ، فَحَلَّتْ لَهُ الْمَسْأَلَةُ حَتَّى يُصِيبَ قِوَامًا مِنْ عَيْشٍ: أَوْ قَالَ: سِدَادًا مِنْ عَيْشٍ -وَرَجُلٍ أَصَابَتْهُ فَاقَةٌ حَتَّى يَقُومَ ثَلَاثَةٌ مِنْ ذَوِي الْحِجَا مِنْ قَوْمِهِ، فَيَقُولُونَ: لَقَدْ أَصَابَتْ فُلَانًا فَاقَةٌ فَحَلَّتْ لَهُ الْمَسْأَلَةُ، حَتَّى يُصِيبَ قِوَامًا مِنْ عَيْشٍ -أَوْ قَالَ سِدَادًا مِنْ عَيْشٍ -فَمَا سِوَاهُنَّ مِنَ الْمَسْأَلَةِ سُحْتٌ، يَأْكُلُهَا صَاحِبُهَا سُحْتًا". رواه مسلم وَعَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ قَالَ: أُصِيبَ رَجُلٌ فِي عَهْدِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فِي ثِمَارٍ ابْتَاعَهَا، فَكَثُرَ دَيْنُهُ، فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ تَصَدَّقُوا عَلَيْهِ". فَتَصَدَّقَ النَّاسُ فَلَمْ يَبْلُغْ ذَلِكَ وَفَاءَ دَيْنِهِ، فَقَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ لِغُرَمَائِهِ: "خُذُوا مَا وَجَدْتُمْ، وَلَيْسَ لَكُمْ إِلَّا ذَلِكَ". رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الصَّمَدِ، أَنْبَأَنَا صَدَقَةُ بْنُ مُوسَى، عَنْ أَبِي عِمْرَانَ الجَوْني، عَنْ قَيْسِ بْنِ زَيْدٍ عَنْ قَاضِي الْمِصْرَيْنِ عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ أَبِي بَكْرٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "يَدْعُو اللَّهُ بِصَاحِبِ الدَّيْنِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ حتى يوقف بين يديه، فيقول: يا بن آدَمَ، فِيمَ أَخَذْتَ هَذَا الدَّيْنَ؟ وَفِيمَ ضَيَّعْتَ حُقُوقَ النَّاسِ؟ فَيَقُولُ: يَا رَبِّ، إِنَّكَ تَعْلَمُ أَنِّي أَخَذْتُهُ فَلَمْ آكُلْ وَلَمْ أَشْرَبْ وَلَمْ أُضَيِّعْ، وَلَكِنْ أَتَى عَلَى يَدَيَّ إِمَّا حَرْقٌ وَإِمَّا سَرَقٌ وَإِمَّا وَضِيعَةٌ. فَيَقُولُ اللَّهُ: صَدَقَ عَبْدِي، أَنَا أَحَقُّ مَنْ قَضَى عَنْكَ الْيَوْمَ. فَيَدْعُو اللَّهُ بِشَيْءٍ فَيَضَعُهُ فِي كِفَّةِ مِيزَانِهِ، فَتَرْجَحُ حَسَنَاتُهُ عَلَى سَيِّئَاتِهِ، فَيَدْخُلُ الْجَنَّةَ بِفَضْلِ اللَّهِ وَرَحْمَتِهِ" 

وَأَمَّا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ: فَمِنْهُمُ الْغُزَاةُ الَّذِينَ لَا حَقَّ لَهُمْ فِي الدِّيوَانِ، وَعِنْدَ الْإِمَامِ أَحْمَدَ، وَالْحَسَنِ، وَإِسْحَاقَ: وَالْحَجُّ مِنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، لِلْحَدِيثِ.

وَكَذَلِكَ ابْنُ السَّبِيلِ: وَهُوَ الْمُسَافِرُ الْمُجْتَازُ فِي بَلَدٍ لَيْسَ مَعَهُ شَيْءٌ يَسْتَعِينُ بِهِ عَلَى سَفَرِهِ، فَيُعْطَى مِنَ الصَّدَقَاتِ مَا يَكْفِيهِ إِلَى بَلَدِهِ وَإِنْ كَانَ لَهُ مَالٌ. وَهَكَذَا الْحُكْمُ فِيمَنْ أَرَادَ إِنْشَاءَ سَفَرٍ مِنْ بَلَدِهِ وَلَيْسَ مَعَهُ شَيْءٌ، فَيُعْطَى مِنْ مَالِ الزَّكَاةِ كِفَايَتَهُ فِي ذَهَابِهِ وَإِيَابِهِ. وَالدَّلِيلُ عَلَى ذَلِكَ الْآيَةُ، وَمَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ مِنْ حَدِيثِ مَعْمَر، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ يَسَار، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا تَحِلُّ الصَّدَقَةُ لِغَنِيٍّ إِلَّا لِخَمْسَةٍ: الْعَامِلِ عَلَيْهَا، أَوْ رَجُلٍ اشْتَرَاهَا بِمَالِهِ، أَوْ غَارِمٍ، أَوْ غَازٍ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، أَوْ مِسْكِينٍ تُصُدِّقَ عَلَيْهِ مِنْهَا فَأَهْدَى لِغَنِيٍّ" 

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ السُّفْيَانَانِ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، عَنْ عَطَاءٍ مُرْسَلًا. وَلِأَبِي دَاوُدَ عَنْ عَطِيَّةَ الْعَوْفِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيِّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَا تَحِلُّ الصَّدَقَةُ لِغَنِيٍّ إِلَّا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، وَابْنِ السَّبِيلِ، أَوْ جَارٍ فَقِيرٍ فيُهدي لَكَ أَوْ يَدْعُوكَ" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَرِيضَةً مِنَ اللَّهِ﴾ أَيْ حُكْمًا مُقَدَّرًا بِتَقْدِيرِ اللَّهِ وفَرْضِه وقَسْمه ﴿وَاللَّهُ عَلِيمٌ حَكِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: عَلِيمٌ بِظَوَاهِرِ الْأُمُورِ وَبَوَاطِنِهَا وَبِمَصَالِحِ عِبَادِهِ، ﴿حَكِيمٌ﴾ فِيمَا يَفْعَلُهُ وَيَقُولُهُ وَيَشْرَعُهُ وَيَحْكُمُ بِهِ، لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا هُوَ، وَلَا رَبَّ سِوَاهُ.

---

## 9:61 — verse 61

### Translation

The Exalted says: among the hypocrites there is a group who harm the Messenger of Allah ﷺ through speech about him, saying: {He is an ear}, meaning: whoever says something to him, he believes it, and whoever speaks to him about us, he believes it, but if we come and swear to him, he believes us. Its meaning has been related from Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, and Qatadah.

Allah the Exalted says: {Say: an ear of good for you}, meaning: he is an ear of good, he recognizes the truthful from the liar. {He believes in Allah and believes the believers}, meaning: and he accepts the believers as truthful. {And a mercy for those among you who have believed}, meaning: and he is a proof against the disbelievers. For this reason He said: {And those who harm the Messenger of Allah, for them is a painful punishment}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: وَمِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ قَوْمٌ يُؤذون رسولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِالْكَلَامِ فِيهِ وَيَقُولُونَ: ﴿هُوَ أُذُنٌ﴾ أَيْ: مَنْ قَالَ لَهُ شَيْئًا صَدَّقَهُ، وَمَنْ حَدَّثَهُ فِينَا صَدَّقَهُ، فَإِذَا جِئْنَا وَحَلَفْنَا لَهُ صَدَّقَنَا. رُوِيَ مَعْنَاهُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَمُجَاهِدٍ، وقَتَادَةَ. قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿قُلْ أُذُنُ خَيْرٍ لَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: هُوَ أُذُنُ خَيْرٍ، يَعْرِفُ الصَّادِقَ مِنَ الْكَاذِبِ، ﴿يُؤْمِنُ بِاللَّهِ وَيُؤْمِنُ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ﴾ أَيْ: وَيُصَدِّقُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، ﴿وَرَحْمَةٌ لِلَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مِنْكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: وَهُوَ حُجَّةٌ عَلَى الْكَافِرِينَ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ يُؤْذُونَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ لَهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ﴾ .

---

## 9:62-63 — verses 62-63 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Qatadah said concerning the words of the Most High, {They swear by Allah to you in order to please you} the verse: he said, "It was mentioned to us that a man among the hypocrites said: 'By Allah, these people are indeed our best and our nobles, and even if what Muhammad says is true, they are worse than donkeys.'" He said: "A man among the Muslims heard this and said: 'By Allah, what Muhammad says is indeed true, and you are worse than a donkey.'" He said: "The man went and reported this to the Prophet ﷺ, informing him. So the Prophet sent for the man and summoned him and said: 'What led you to say what you said?' The man began cursing himself and swearing by Allah that he had not said that. Meanwhile the Muslim man kept saying: 'O Allah, confirm the truthful one and belie the liar.'" So Allah, Mighty and Majestic, sent down: {They swear by Allah to you in order to please you, but Allah and His Messenger are more deserving that they should please Him, if they are believers}.

Regarding the words of the Most High, {Do they not know that whoever opposes Allah and His Messenger, for him is the fire of Hell, abiding therein}, meaning: have they not verified and come to know that whoever opposes Allah, that is, contends against Him, wars against Him, and defies Him, thereby placing himself in one camp while Allah and His Messenger are in another camp, {for him is the fire of Hell, abiding therein}, meaning: humiliated and tormented, {that is the great disgrace}, meaning: this is the immense degradation and the great wretchedness.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَحْلِفُونَ بِاللَّهِ لَكُمْ لِيُرْضُوكُمْ﴾ الْآيَةَ، قَالَ: ذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّ رَجُلًا مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ قَالَ: وَاللَّهِ إِنَّ هَؤُلَاءِ لَخِيَارُنَا وَأَشْرَافُنَا، وَإِنْ كَانَ مَا يَقُولُ مُحَمَّدٌ حَقًّا، لَهُمْ شَرٌّ مِنَ الْحَمِيرِ. قَالَ: فَسَمِعَهَا رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ فَقَالَ: وَاللَّهِ إِنَّ مَا يَقُولُ مُحَمَّدٌ لَحَقٌّ، وَلَأَنْتَ أَشَرُّ مِنَ الْحِمَارِ. قَالَ: فَسَعَى بِهَا الرَّجُلُ إِلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ فَأَخْبَرَهُ، فَأَرْسَلَ إِلَى الرَّجُلِ فَدَعَاهُ فَقَالَ: "مَا حَمَلَكَ عَلَى الَّذِي قُلْتَ؟ " فَجَعَلَ يَلْتَعِنُ، وَيَحْلِفُ بِاللَّهِ مَا قَالَ ذَلِكَ. وَجَعَلَ الرَّجُلُ الْمُسْلِمُ يَقُولُ: اللَّهُمَّ صَدِّقِ الصَّادِقَ وَكَذِّبِ الْكَاذِبَ. فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿يَحْلِفُونَ بِاللَّهِ لَكُمْ لِيُرْضُوكُمْ وَاللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ أَحَقُّ أَنْ يُرْضُوهُ إِنْ كَانُوا مُؤْمِنِينَ﴾

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿أَلَمْ يَعْلَمُوا أَنَّهُ مَنْ يُحَادِدِ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ فَأَنَّ لَهُ نَارَ جَهَنَّمَ خَالِدًا فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: أَلَمْ يَتَحَقَّقُوا وَيَعْلَمُوا أَنَّهُ مَنْ حَادَّ اللَّهَ، أَيْ: شَاقَّهُ وَحَارَبَهُ وَخَالَفَهُ، وَكَانَ فِي حَدٍّ وَاللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ فِي حدٍّ ﴿فَأَنَّ لَهُ نَارَ جَهَنَّمَ خَالِدًا فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: مُهَانًا مُعَذَّبًا، ﴿ذَلِكَ الْخِزْيُ الْعَظِيمُ﴾ أَيْ: وَهَذَا هُوَ الذُّلُّ الْعَظِيمُ، وَالشَّقَاءُ الْكَبِيرُ.

---

## 9:64 — verse 64

### Translation

Mujahid said: They speak among themselves, then say, "Perhaps Allah will not disclose this secret of ours."

This verse resembles His saying, the Most High: {And when they come to you, they greet you with that which Allah has not greeted you with, and they say within themselves, "Why does Allah not punish us for what we say?" Sufficient for them is Hell, which they will burn in, and what an evil destination it is} [al-Mujadilah: 8]. And He said in this verse: {Say: "Mock on. Indeed Allah will bring forth what you are wary of"}, meaning: Allah will send down upon His Messenger that which will expose you and make your affair clear to him, just as He said: {Or do those in whose hearts is a disease think that Allah will never bring forth their malice?} up to His saying: {And you will surely know them by the tone of their speech. And Allah knows your deeds} [Muhammad: 29, 30]. For this reason Qatadah said: This surah used to be called "al-Fadihah" (the Exposer), the exposer of the hypocrites.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: يَقُولُونَ الْقَوْلَ بَيْنَهُمْ، ثُمَّ يَقُولُونَ: عَسَى اللَّهُ أَلَّا يُفْشِيَ عَلَيْنَا سِرَّنَا هَذَا.

وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ شَبِيهَةٌ بِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِذَا جَاءُوكَ حَيَّوْكَ بِمَا لَمْ يُحَيِّكَ بِهِ اللَّهُ وَيَقُولُونَ فِي أَنْفُسِهِمْ لَوْلا يُعَذِّبُنَا اللَّهُ بِمَا نَقُولُ حَسْبُهُمْ جَهَنَّمُ يَصْلَوْنَهَا فَبِئْسَ الْمَصِيرُ﴾ [المجادلة: ٨] وَقَالَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: ﴿قُلِ اسْتَهْزِءُوا إِنَّ اللَّهَ مُخْرِجٌ مَا تَحْذَرُونَ﴾ أَيْ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ سَيُنْزِلُ عَلَى رَسُولِهِ مَا يَفْضَحُكُمْ بِهِ، وَيُبَيِّنُ لَهُ أَمْرَكُمْ كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿أَمْ حَسِبَ الَّذِينَ فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ مَرَضٌ أَنْ لَنْ يُخْرِجَ اللَّهُ أَضْغَانَهُمْ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَتَعْرِفَنَّهُمْ فِي لَحْنِ الْقَوْلِ وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ أَعْمَالَكُمْ﴾ [مُحَمَّدٍ: ٢٩، ٣٠] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ قَتَادَةُ: كَانَتْ تُسَمَّى هَذِهِ السُّورَةُ "الْفَاضِحَةُ"، فَاضِحَةُ الْمُنَافِقِينَ.

---

## 9:65-66 — verses 65-66 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Abu Ma'shar al-Madini said, on the authority of Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi and others: they said, a man among the hypocrites said, "I see nothing in these Qur'an-reciters of ours except that they are the greediest of us in the belly, the most lying of us in the tongue, and the most cowardly of us at the moment of battle." This was reported to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, so he came to the Messenger of Allah after he had already set out and mounted his she-camel, and said, "O Messenger of Allah, we were only engaging in idle talk and playing." So he said, {"Was it Allah, His signs, and His Messenger that you were mocking?"} up to His saying, {"criminals"}, while the man's feet were kicking up stones and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ would not even turn to look at him, though he was clinging to the strap of the Messenger of Allah's ﷺ saddle.

Abdullah ibn Wahb said: Hisham ibn Sa'd informed me, from Zayd ibn Aslam, from Abdullah ibn Umar, who said: a man said during the expedition of Tabuk, in a gathering, "I have not seen the like of these Qur'an-reciters of ours: greedier in the belly, more lying in tongue, nor more cowardly at the moment of battle." A man in the gathering said, "You have lied, rather you are a hypocrite. I will surely inform the Messenger of Allah ﷺ." That reached the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and the Qur'an came down. Abdullah ibn Umar said: I saw him clinging to the strap beneath the belly of the she-camel of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, with stones striking him, while he was saying, "O Messenger of Allah, we were only engaging in idle talk and playing." And the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was saying, {"Was it Allah, His signs, and His Messenger that you were mocking? Make no excuse; you have disbelieved after your belief."}

Al-Layth also related it from Hisham ibn Sa'd in a similar manner.

Ibn Ishaq said: there was a group among the hypocrites, among them Wadi'ah ibn Thabit, a brother of Banu Umayyah ibn Zayd from Banu Amr ibn Awf, and a man from Ashja', an ally of Banu Salamah called Mukhashshin ibn Humayyir, who used to make gestures about the Messenger of Allah ﷺ while he was on his way to Tabuk. Some of them said to others, "Do you think fighting the Banu al-Asfar (the Byzantines) is like the Arabs fighting one another? By Allah, it is as though we can already see you tomorrow bound together in ropes," spreading alarm and instilling fear among the believers. Mukhashshin ibn Humayyir said, "By Allah, I would wish that I could be judged on the condition that each of us be struck one hundred lashes, rather than that Qur'an be sent down concerning us because of this statement of yours." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, as has reached me, to Ammar ibn Yasir: "Catch up with the people, for they have been burned up; ask them about what they said, and if they deny it, say: Yes indeed, you said such and such." So Ammar went to them and said that to them, and they came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ making excuses to him. Wadi'ah ibn Thabit spoke while the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was standing upon his mount, and he kept saying, holding the strap beneath its belly, "O Messenger of Allah, we were only engaging in idle talk and playing." [Then Allah, mighty and majestic, sent down: {"And if you ask them, they will surely say, 'We were only engaging in idle talk and playing.'"}] Mukhashshin ibn Humayyir said, "O Messenger of Allah, my name and my father's name have brought this upon me." The one who was pardoned in this verse was Mukhashshin ibn Humayyir; he then named himself Abd al-Rahman, and asked Allah that he be killed as a martyr in a place where his whereabouts would not be known. He was killed on the day of Yamamah, and no trace of him was ever found.

Qatadah said, concerning {"And if you ask them, they will surely say, 'We were only engaging in idle talk and playing'"}: while the Prophet ﷺ was on the expedition of Tabuk, a group of hypocrites riding ahead of him said, "Does this man suppose that he will conquer the palaces and fortresses of the Romans? Far from it, far from it!" Allah then informed His Prophet ﷺ of what they had said, so he said, "Bring these men to me." He summoned them and said, "You said such and such." They swore, "We were only engaging in idle talk and playing."

Ikrimah said, in explaining this verse: there was a man, among those whom, if Allah willed, He pardoned, who used to say, "O Allah, I hear a verse that I know is meant for me, one that makes the skin shiver and the hearts respond. O Allah, make my death a killing in Your path, such that no one will say: I washed him, I shrouded him, I buried him." He said: that man was struck down on the day of Yamamah, and every single Muslim killed there had someone found of him except him.

His saying, {"Make no excuse; you have disbelieved after your belief,"} means: because of this statement with which you mocked. {"If We pardon one party of you, We will punish another party,"} means: not all of you will be pardoned; some of you must inevitably be punished. {"Because they were criminals,"} means: criminals for this wicked, sinful statement.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ أَبُو مَعْشَرٍ الْمَدِينِيُّ عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ كَعْبٍ القُرَظي وَغَيْرِهِ قَالُوا: قَالَ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ: مَا أَرَى قُرّاءنا هَؤُلَاءِ إِلَّا أَرْغَبَنَا بُطُونًا، وَأَكْذَبَنَا أَلْسِنَةً، وَأَجْبَنَنَا عِنْدَ اللِّقَاءِ. فرُفع ذَلِكَ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَجَاءَ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ وَقَدِ ارْتَحَلَ وَرَكِبَ نَاقَتَهُ، فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّمَا كُنَّا نَخُوضُ وَنَلْعَبُ. فَقَالَ: ﴿أَبِاللَّهِ وَآيَاتِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ كُنْتُمْ تَسْتَهْزِئُونَ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ: ﴿مُجْرِمِينَ﴾ وَإِنَّ رِجْلَيْهِ لَتَنْسِفَانِ الْحِجَارَةَ وَمَا يَلْتَفِتُ إِلَيْهِ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَهُوَ مُتَعَلِّقٌ بِنِسْعَةِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ وَهْبٍ: أَخْبَرَنِي هِشَامُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أسلم، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عُمَرَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَجُلٌ في غزوة تبوك في مجلس مَا رَأَيْتُ مِثْلَ قُرائنا هَؤُلَاءِ، أرغبَ بُطُونًا، وَلَا أكذبَ أَلْسُنًا، وَلَا أَجْبَنَ عِنْدَ اللِّقَاءِ. فَقَالَ رَجُلٌ فِي الْمَسْجِدِ: كذبتَ، وَلَكِنَّكَ مُنَافِقٌ. لَأُخْبِرَنَّ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَبَلَغَ ذَلِكَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَنَزَلَ الْقُرْآنُ. قَالَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عُمَرَ: وَأَنَا رَأَيْتُهُ مُتَعَلِّقًا بحَقَب نَاقَةِ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ تَنكُبُه الْحِجَارَةُ وَهُوَ يَقُولُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّمَا كُنَّا نَخُوضُ وَنَلْعَبُ. وَرَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: ﴿أَبِاللَّهِ وَآيَاتِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ كُنْتُمْ تَسْتَهْزِئُونَ لَا تَعْتَذِرُوا قَدْ كَفَرْتُمْ بَعْدَ إِيمَانِكُمْ﴾ .

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ اللَّيْثُ، عَنْ هِشَامِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، بِنَحْوٍ مِنْ هَذَا 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: وَقَدْ كَانَ جَمَاعَةٌ مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ مِنْهُمْ وَديعة بْنُ ثَابِتٍ، أَخُو بَنِي أُمَيَّةَ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، مِنْ بَنِي عَمْرِو بْنِ عَوْفٍ، وَرَجُلٌ مِنْ أَشْجَعَ حَلِيفٌ لِبَنِي سَلَمَةَ يُقَالُ لَهُ: مُخَشّن بْنُ حُميّر يُشِيرُونَ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهُوَ مُنْطَلِقٌ إِلَى تَبُوكَ، فَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ لِبَعْضٍ: أَتَحْسَبُونَ جِلادَ بَنِي الْأَصْفَرِ كَقِتَالِ الْعَرَبِ بَعْضِهِمْ بَعْضًا؟ وَاللَّهِ لَكَأَنَّا بِكُمْ غَدًا مُقَرّنين فِي الْحِبَالِ، إِرْجَافًا وَتَرْهِيبًا لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ، فَقَالَ مُخَشّن بْنُ حُمَيّر: وَاللَّهِ لوددتُ أَنِّي أُقَاضَى عَلَى أَنْ يُضْرَبَ كُلُّ رَجُلٍ مِنَّا مِائَةَ جَلْدَةٍ، وإما نَنْفَلتُ أَنْ يُنَزَّلَ فِينَا قُرْآنٌ لِمَقَالَتِكُمْ هَذِهِ. وَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ -فِيمَا بَلَغَنِي -لِعَمَّارِ بْنِ يَاسِرٍ: "أَدْرِكِ الْقَوْمَ، فَإِنَّهُمْ قَدِ احْتَرَقُوا، فَسَلْهُمْ عَمَّا قَالُوا، فَإِنْ أَنْكَرُوا فَقُلْ: بَلَى، قُلْتُمْ كَذَا وَكَذَا". فَانْطَلَقَ إِلَيْهِمْ عَمَّارٌ، فَقَالَ ذَلِكَ لَهُمْ، فَأَتَوْا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَعْتَذِرُونَ إِلَيْهِ، فَقَالَ وَدِيعَةُ بْنُ ثَابِتٍ، وَرَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَاقِفٌ عَلَى رَاحِلَتِهِ، فَجَعَلَ يَقُولُ وَهُوَ آخِذٌ بحَقَبها: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّمَا كُنَّا نَخُوضُ وَنَلْعَبُ، [فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَلَئِنْ سَأَلْتَهُمْ لَيَقُولُنَّ إِنَّمَا كُنَّا نَخُوضُ وَنَلْعَبُ﴾ ] فَقَالَ مُخَشّن بْنُ حُمّير: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، قَعَدَ بِيَ اسْمِي وَاسْمُ أَبِي. فَكَانَ الَّذِي عُفِيَ عَنْهُ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ مُخَشّن بْنُ حُمّير، فَتَسَمَّى عَبْدَ الرَّحْمَنِ، وَسَأَلَ اللَّهَ أَنْ يُقْتَلَ شَهِيدًا لَا يُعْلَمُ بِمَكَانِهِ، فَقُتِلَ يَوْمَ الْيَمَامَةِ، فَلَمْ يُوجَدْ لَهُ أَثَرٌ 

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: ﴿وَلَئِنْ سَأَلْتَهُمْ لَيَقُولُنَّ إِنَّمَا كُنَّا نَخُوضُ وَنَلْعَبُ﴾ قَالَ: فَبَيْنَمَا النَّبِيُّ ﷺ فِي غَزْوَةِ تَبُوكَ، وَرَكْبٌ مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ يَسِيرُونَ بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ، فَقَالُوا: يَظُنُّ هَذَا أَنْ يَفْتَحَ قُصُورَ الرُّومِ وَحُصُونَهَا. هَيْهَاتَ هَيْهَاتَ. فَأَطْلَعَ اللَّهُ نَبِيَّهُ ﷺ عَلَى مَا قَالُوا، فَقَالَ: "عَليَّ بِهَؤُلَاءِ النَّفَرِ". فَدَعَاهُمْ، فَقَالَ: "قُلْتُمْ كَذَا وَكَذَا". فَحَلَفُوا مَا كُنَّا إِلَّا نَخُوضُ وَنَلْعَبُ.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمة فِي تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: كَانَ رَجُلٌ مِمَّنْ إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ عَفَا عَنْهُ يَقُولُ: اللَّهُمَّ، إِنِّي أَسْمَعُ آيَةً أَنَا أعنَى بِهَا، تَقْشَعِرُّ مِنْهَا الْجُلُودُ، وتجيب مِنْهَا الْقُلُوبُ، اللَّهُمَّ، فَاجْعَلْ وَفَاتِي قَتْلًا فِي سَبِيلِكَ، لَا يَقُولُ أَحَدٌ: أَنَا غُسِّلْتُ، أَنَا كُفِّنْتُ، أَنَا دُفِنْتُ، قَالَ: فَأُصِيبَ يَوْمَ الْيَمَامَةِ، فَمَا أَحَدٌ مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ إِلَّا وَقَدْ وُجِدَ غَيْرُهُ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَا تَعْتَذِرُوا قَدْ كَفَرْتُمْ بَعْدَ إِيمَانِكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: بِهَذَا الْمَقَالِ الَّذِي اسْتَهْزَأْتُمْ بِهِ ﴿إِنْ نَعْفُ عَنْ طَائِفَةٍ مِنْكُمْ نُعَذِّبْ طَائِفَةً﴾ أَيْ: لَا يُعْفى عَنْ جَمِيعِكُمْ، وَلَا بُدَّ مِنْ عَذَابِ بَعْضِكُمْ، ﴿بِأَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا مُجْرِمِينَ﴾ أَيْ: مُجْرِمِينَ بِهَذِهِ الْمَقَالَةِ الْفَاجِرَةِ الْخَاطِئَةِ.

---

## 9:67-68 — verses 67-68 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted speaks, denouncing the hypocrites who are contrary in their qualities to the believers. Since the believers command what is right and forbid what is wrong, these people {command what is wrong and forbid what is right and withhold their hands}, meaning: from spending in the way of Allah. {They have forgotten Allah}, meaning: they have forgotten the remembrance of Allah, {so He has forgotten them}, meaning: He treats them as one treats those who are forgotten, as in His saying, the Exalted: {And it will be said, "Today We forget you as you forgot the meeting of this Day of yours"} [al-Jathiyah: 34]. {Indeed, the hypocrites are the fasiqun (transgressors)}, meaning: those who have departed from the path of truth and entered upon the path of misguidance.

As for His saying: {Allah has promised the hypocrite men and hypocrite women and the disbelievers the fire of Jahannam}, meaning: for this conduct mentioned about them, {abiding therein eternally}, meaning: remaining in it forever, they and the disbelievers together, {it is sufficient for them}, meaning: it suffices them as punishment, {and Allah has cursed them}, meaning: He has driven them away and cast them far off, {and for them is an enduring punishment}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُنْكِرًا عَلَى الْمُنَافِقِينَ الَّذِينَ هُمْ عَلَى خِلَافِ صِفَاتِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَلَمَّا كَانَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ يَأْمُرُونَ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَيَنْهَوْنَ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ، كَانَ هَؤُلَاءِ ﴿يَأْمُرُونَ بِالْمُنْكَرِ وَيَنْهَوْنَ عَنِ الْمَعْرُوفِ وَيَقْبِضُونَ أَيْدِيَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: عَنِ الْإِنْفَاقِ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، ﴿نَسُوا اللَّهَ﴾ أَيْ: نسوا ذكر الله، ﴿فَنَسِيَهُمْ﴾ أي: عاملهم مُعَامَلَةَ مَنْ نَسِيَهُمْ، كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَقِيلَ الْيَوْمَ نَنْسَاكُمْ كَمَا نَسِيتُمْ لِقَاءَ يَوْمِكُمْ هَذَا﴾ [الْجَاثِيَةِ:٣٤] ﴿إِنَّ الْمُنَافِقِينَ هُمُ الْفَاسِقُونَ﴾ أَيْ: الْخَارِجُونَ عَنْ طَرِيقِ الْحَقِّ، الدَّاخِلُونَ فِي طَرِيقِ الضَّلَالَةِ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَعَدَ اللَّهُ الْمُنَافِقِينَ وَالْمُنَافِقَاتِ وَالْكُفَّارَ نَارَ جَهَنَّمَ﴾ أَيْ: عَلَى هَذَا الصَّنِيعِ الَّذِي ذُكِرَ عَنْهُمْ، ﴿خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: مَاكِثِينَ فِيهَا مُخَلَّدِينَ، هُمْ وَالْكُفَّارُ، ﴿هِيَ حَسْبُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: كِفَايَتُهُمْ فِي الْعَذَابِ، ﴿وَلَعَنَهُمُ اللَّهُ﴾ أَيْ: طَرَدَهُمْ وَأَبْعَدَهُمْ، ﴿وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ مُقِيمٌ﴾ .

---

## 9:69 — verse 69

### Translation

The Almighty says: these people were struck by God's punishment in this world and the next just as those before them were struck, and those before them had been greater than them in strength and more abundant in wealth and children. {So they enjoyed their portion} al-Hasan al-Basri said: their portion of religion. {just as those before you enjoyed their portion, and you plunged in as they plunged in}, meaning: into falsehood and vanity. {Those are the ones whose deeds have come to nothing}, meaning: their efforts became void, so there is no reward for them because these deeds are corrupt, {in this world and the next, and those, they are the losers}, because they obtained no reward for them.

Ibn Jurayj said, from Umar ibn Ata', from Ikrimah, from Ibn Abbas, concerning His saying: {like those before you}, the verse. Ibn Abbas said: how similar tonight is to last night. {Like those before you}, these are the Children of Israel, we have been likened to them. I know of nothing else except that he said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, you will surely follow them, so that even if one of them entered the hole of a lizard, you would enter it too."

Ibn Jurayj said: Ziyad ibn Sa'd informed me, from Muhammad ibn Zayd ibn Muhajir, from Sa'id ibn Abi Sa'id al-Maqburi, from Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with him, who said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "By the One in whose hand is my soul, you will surely follow the paths of those before you, span for span, cubit for cubit, armspan for armspan, so that even if they entered the hole of a lizard, you would enter it too." They said: and who are they, O Messenger of God? The People of the Book? He said: "Then who else?"

And likewise it was narrated by Abu Ma'shar, from Sa'id al-Maqburi, from Abu Hurayrah, from the Prophet ﷺ, and he mentioned it and added: Abu Hurayrah said: recite, if you wish, the Qur'an: {like those before you, they were greater than you in strength and more abundant in wealth and children; they enjoyed their portion, and you enjoyed your portion just as those before you enjoyed their portion}. Abu Hurayrah said: al-khalaq (the portion) means religion. {and you plunged in as they plunged in}. They said: O Messenger of God, as Persia and Rome did? He said: "Are people other than them?" This hadith has a corroborating report in the Sahih.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: أَصَابَ هَؤُلَاءِ مِنْ عَذَابِ اللَّهِ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ كَمَا أَصَابَ مَنْ قَبْلَهُمْ، وَقَدْ كَانُوا أَشَدَّ مِنْهُمْ قُوَّةً وَأَكْثَرَ أَمْوَالًا وَأَوْلَادًا، ﴿فَاسْتَمْتَعُوا بِخَلاقِهِمْ﴾ قَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: بِدِينِهِمْ، ﴿كَمَا اسْتَمْتَعَ الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ بِخَلاقِهِمْ وَخُضْتُمْ كَالَّذِي خَاضُوا﴾ أَيْ: فِي الْكَذِبِ وَالْبَاطِلِ، ﴿أُولَئِكَ حَبِطَتْ أَعْمَالُهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: بَطَلَتْ مَسَاعِيهِمْ، فَلَا ثَوَابَ لَهُمْ عَلَيْهَا لِأَنَّهَا فَاسِدَةٌ ﴿فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالآخِرَةِ وَأُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْخَاسِرُونَ﴾ ؛ لِأَنَّهُمْ لَمْ يَحْصُلْ لَهُمْ عَلَيْهَا ثَوَابٌ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج عَنْ عُمَر بْنُ عَطَاء، عَنْ عِكْرِمة، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿كَالَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ﴾ الْآيَةَ، قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: مَا أَشْبَهَ اللَّيْلَةَ بِالْبَارِحَةِ، ﴿كَالَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ﴾ هَؤُلَاءِ بَنُو إِسْرَائِيلَ، شُبِّهْنَا بِهِمْ، لَا أَعْلَمُ إِلَّا أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَتَتَّبِعُنَّهُمْ حَتَّى لَوْ دَخَلَ الرَّجُلُ مِنْهُمْ جُحر ضَبٍّ لَدَخَلْتُمُوهُ".

قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج: وَأَخْبَرَنِي زِيَادُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ زَيْدِ بْنِ مُهَاجِرٍ، عَنْ سَعِيدُ بْنُ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ المَقْبُري، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "وَالَّذِي نَفْسِي بِيَدِهِ، لَتَتَّبِعُنَّ سَنَن الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ، شِبْرًا بِشِبْرٍ، وَذِرَاعًا بِذِرَاعٍ، وَبَاعًا بِبَاعٍ، حَتَّى لَوْ دَخَلُوا جُحْر ضَبٍّ لَدَخَلْتُمُوهُ". قَالُوا: وَمَنْ هُمْ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ؟ أَهْلُ الْكِتَابِ؟ قَالَ: "فَمَه" 

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ أَبُو مَعْشَر، عَنْ سَعِيدٍ الْمَقْبُرِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، فَذَكَرَهُ وَزَادَ: قَالَ أَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ: اقْرَءُوا إِنْ شِئْتُمُ الْقُرْآنَ. ﴿كَالَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ كَانُوا أَشَدَّ مِنْكُمْ قُوَّةً وَأَكْثَرَ أَمْوَالا وَأَوْلادًا فَاسْتَمْتَعُوا بِخَلاقِهِمْ فَاسْتَمْتَعْتُمْ بِخَلاقِكُمْ كَمَا اسْتَمْتَعَ الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ بِخَلاقِهِمْ﴾ قَالَ أَبُو هُرَيْرَةَ: الْخَلَاقُ: الدِّينُ. ﴿وَخُضْتُمْ كَالَّذِي خَاضُوا﴾ قَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، كَمَا صَنَعَتْ فَارِسُ وَالرُّومُ؟ قَالَ: "فَهَلِ الناس إلا هم" وَهَذَا الْحَدِيثُ لَهُ شَاهِدٌ فِي الصَّحِيحِ

---

## 9:70 — verse 70

### Translation

The Exalted says, admonishing these hypocrites who deny the messengers: {Has there not come to them the report of those before them} that is, have you not been informed of the report of those nations before you who denied the messengers: {the people of Nuh} and what befell them of the universal flood which engulfed all the people of the earth, except those who believed in His servant and messenger Nuh (peace be upon him); {and 'Ad}, how they were destroyed by the barren wind when they denied Hud (peace be upon him); {and Thamud}, how the Blast seized them when they denied Salih (peace be upon him) and hamstrung the she-camel; {and the people of Ibrahim}, how Allah granted him victory over them and supported him with manifest miracles against them, and destroyed their king, Namrud ibn Kan'an ibn Kush the Canaanite, may Allah curse him; {and the companions of Madyan}, who were the people of Shu'ayb (peace be upon him), and how the earthquake, the Blast, and the punishment of the Day of the Shadow struck them; {and the overturned cities}, the people of Lut, who used to dwell in cities. In another verse He says: {and the overturned cities He cast down} [al-Najm: 53], meaning the overturned nation. It is also said that it refers to the mother of their cities, which was "Sodom". The point is that Allah, the Exalted, destroyed them entirely because they denied the prophet of Allah, Lut (peace be upon him), and committed the abomination which no one among the worlds had ever committed before them.

{Their messengers came to them with clear proofs}, that is, with decisive arguments and evidences. {So it was not Allah who wronged them}, that is, by destroying them, for He had established the proof against them by sending the messengers and removing all excuses. {But it was they who wronged themselves}, that is, by denying the messengers and opposing the truth, and so they ended up in the punishment and destruction that befell them.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى وَاعِظًا لِهَؤُلَاءِ الْمُنَافِقِينَ الْمُكَذِّبِينَ لِلرُّسُلِ: ﴿أَلَمْ يَأْتِهِمْ نَبَأُ الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَلَمْ تُخْبَرُوا خَبَرَ مَنْ كَانَ قَبْلَكُمْ مِنَ الْأُمَمِ الْمُكَذِّبَةِ لِلرُّسُلِ ﴿قَوْمِ نُوحٍ﴾ وَمَا أَصَابَهُمْ مِنَ الْغَرَقِ الْعَامِّ لِجَمِيعِ أَهْلِ الْأَرْضِ، إِلَّا مَنْ آمَنَ بِعَبْدِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ نُوحٍ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، ﴿وَعَادٍ﴾ كَيْفَ أُهْلِكُوا بِالرِّيحِ الْعَقِيمِ، لَمَّا كَذَّبُوا هُودًا، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، ﴿وَثَمُودَ﴾ كَيْفَ أَخَذَتْهُمُ الصَّيْحَةُ لَمَّا كَذَّبُوا صَالِحًا، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَعَقَرُوا النَّاقَةَ، ﴿وَقَوْمِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ﴾ كَيْفَ نَصَرَهُ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ وَأَيَّدَهُ بِالْمُعْجِزَاتِ الظَّاهِرَةِ عَلَيْهِمْ، وَأَهْلَكَ مَلِكَهُمُ النَّمْرُوذَ بْنَ كَنْعَانَ بْنِ كُوشَ الْكَنْعَانِيَّ لَعَنَهُ اللَّهُ، ﴿وَأَصْحَابِ مَدْيَنَ﴾ وَهُمْ قَوْمُ شُعَيْبٍ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَكَيْفَ أَصَابَتْهُمُ الرَّجْفَةُ وَالصَّيْحَةُ وَعَذَابُ يَوْمِ الظُّلَّةِ، ﴿وَالْمُؤْتَفِكَاتِ﴾ قَوْمِ لُوطٍ، وَقَدْ كَانُوا يَسْكُنُونَ فِي مَدَائِنَ، وَقَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَالْمُؤْتَفِكَةَ أَهْوَى﴾ [النَّجْمِ: ٥٣،] أَي: الْأُمَّةَ الْمُؤْتَفِكَةَ، وَقِيلَ: أُمُّ قُرَاهُمْ، وَهِيَ "سَدُومُ". وَالْغَرَضُ: أَنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى أَهْلَكَهُمْ عَنْ آخِرِهِمْ بِتَكْذِيبِهِمْ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ لُوطًا، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَإِتْيَانِهِمُ الْفَاحِشَةَ الَّتِي لَمْ يَسْبِقْهُمْ بِهَا أَحَدٌ مِنَ الْعَالَمِينَ.

﴿أَتَتْهُمْ رُسُلُهُمْ بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ﴾ أَيْ: بِالْحُجَجِ وَالدَّلَائِلِ الْقَاطِعَاتِ، ﴿فَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيَظْلِمَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: بِإِهْلَاكِهِ إِيَّاهُمْ؛ لِأَنَّهُ أَقَامَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْحُجَّةَ بِإِرْسَالِ الرُّسُلِ وَإِزَاحَةِ الْعِلَلِ ﴿وَلَكِنْ كَانُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ يَظْلِمُونَ﴾ أَيْ: بِتَكْذِيبِهِمُ الرُّسُلَ وَمُخَالَفَتِهِمُ الْحَقَّ، فَصَارُوا إِلَى مَا صَارُوا إِلَيْهِ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ وَالدَّمَارِ.

---

## 9:71 — verse 71

### Translation

When Allah, exalted is He, mentioned the blameworthy attributes of the hypocrites, He followed this by mentioning the praiseworthy attributes of the believers, saying: {Some of them are the allies of others}, meaning: they support one another and aid one another, as has come in the sahih (authentic hadith): "The believer is to the believer like a structure, part of it strengthening the other," and he interlaced his fingers. And in the sahih also: "The parable of the believers in their mutual love and mercy is like the parable of a single body: when one part of it complains of ailment, the rest of the body responds to it with fever and sleeplessness."

His saying: {They enjoin what is right and forbid what is wrong} is like His saying, exalted is He: {And let there be among you a community calling to good, enjoining what is right and forbidding what is wrong, and those are the successful} [Al Imran: 104].

His saying, exalted is He: {And they establish prayer and give zakat}, meaning: they obey Allah and do good to His creation. {And they obey Allah and His Messenger}, meaning: in what He has commanded and by refraining from what He has forbidden. {Those, Allah will have mercy upon them}, meaning: Allah will have mercy upon whoever is characterized by these attributes. {Indeed, Allah is Mighty, Wise}, meaning: Mighty, whoever obeys Him, He grants him might, for might belongs to Allah and to His Messenger and to the believers. {Wise} in His apportioning of these attributes to these people, and in singling out the hypocrites with their aforementioned attributes, for He has wisdom in everything He does, blessed and exalted is He.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ [اللَّهُ] تَعَالَى صِفَاتِ الْمُنَافِقِينَ الذَّمِيمَةَ، عَطَفَ بِذِكْرِ صِفَاتِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ الْمَحْمُودَةِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿بَعْضُهُمْ أَوْلِيَاءُ بَعْضٍ﴾ أَيْ: يَتَنَاصَرُونَ وَيَتَعَاضَدُونَ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الصحيح: "المؤمن للمؤمن كالبنان يَشُدُّ بَعْضُهُ بَعْضًا" وَشَبَّكَ بَيْنَ أَصَابِعِهِ وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ أَيْضًا: "مَثَلُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ فِي تَوَادِّهِمْ وَتَرَاحُمِهِمْ، كَمَثَلِ الْجَسَدِ الْوَاحِدِ، إِذَا اشْتَكَى مِنْهُ عُضْوٌ تَدَاعَى لَهُ سائر الجسد بالحمى والسهر" وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿يَأْمُرُونَ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَيَنْهَوْنَ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ﴾ كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلْتَكُنْ مِنْكُمْ أُمَّةٌ يَدْعُونَ إِلَى الْخَيْرِ وَيَأْمُرُونَ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَيَنْهَوْنَ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ وَأُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْمُفْلِحُونَ﴾ [آلِ عِمْرَانَ:١٠٤]

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَيُقِيمُونَ الصَّلاةَ وَيُؤْتُونَ الزَّكَاةَ﴾ أَيْ: يُطِيعُونَ اللَّهَ وَيُحْسِنُونَ إِلَى خَلْقِهِ، ﴿وَيُطِيعُونَ اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ﴾ أَيْ: فِيمَا أَمَرَ، وَتَرْكِ مَا عَنْهُ زَجَرَ، ﴿أُولَئِكَ سَيَرْحَمُهُمُ اللَّهُ﴾ أَيْ: سَيَرْحَمُ اللَّهُ مَنِ اتَّصَفَ بِهَذِهِ الصِّفَاتِ، ﴿إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَزِيزٌ حَكِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: عَزِيزٌ، مَنْ أَطَاعَهُ أَعَزَّهُ، فَإِنَّ الْعِزَّةَ لِلَّهِ وَلِرَسُولِهِ وَلِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ، ﴿حَكِيمٌ﴾ فِي قِسْمَتِهِ هَذِهِ الصِّفَاتِ لِهَؤُلَاءِ، وَتَخْصِيصِهِ الْمُنَافِقِينَ بِصِفَاتِهِمُ الْمُتَقَدِّمَةِ، فَإِنَّ لَهُ الْحِكْمَةَ فِي جَمِيعِ مَا يَفْعَلُهُ، تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى.

---

## 9:72 — verse 72

### Translation

The Almighty informs of what He has prepared for the believing men and believing women, of goodness and abiding bliss in {gardens beneath which rivers flow, abiding therein forever}, that is: remaining in them eternally, {and good dwellings}, that is: excellent in construction, good in their settledness, as has come in the two Sahihs, in the hadith of Abu Imran al-Jawni, from Abu Bakr ibn Abi Musa Abdullah ibn Qays al-Ashari, from his father, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Two gardens of gold, whose vessels and what is in them are of gold, and two gardens of silver, whose vessels and what is in them are of silver, and there is nothing between the people and their looking upon their Lord except the veil of grandeur upon His face, in the Garden of Eden."

And with the same chain he said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The believer will indeed have in Paradise a tent made from a single hollowed-out pearl, sixty miles in height reaching into the sky, in which the believer will have families whom he visits, none of them seeing the others." Both [Bukhari and Muslim] transmitted it.

And in the two Sahihs also, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever believes in Allah and His Messenger, establishes the prayer, and fasts Ramadan, then it is a right due upon Allah that He admit him into Paradise, whether he emigrated for the sake of Allah or remained in the land in which he was born." They said: O Messenger of Allah, shall we not inform the people? He said: "In Paradise there are a hundred levels which Allah has prepared for those who strive in His cause, between every two levels being like the distance between the heaven and the earth. So when you ask Allah, ask Him for al-Firdaws, for it is the highest part of Paradise and its middle, and from it the rivers of Paradise burst forth, and above it is the Throne of the Most Merciful."

And with al-Tabarani, al-Tirmidhi, and Ibn Majah, by the narration of Zayd ibn Aslam, from Ata ibn Yasar, from Mu'adh ibn Jabal, may Allah be pleased with him: I heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ saying... and he mentioned the like of it.

And al-Tirmidhi transmitted, from Ubadah ibn al-Samit, the like of it. And from Abu Hazim, from Sahl ibn Sa'd, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The people of Paradise will indeed see the upper chamber in Paradise just as you see a star in the sky." Both [Bukhari and Muslim] transmitted it in the two Sahihs.

Then let it be known that the highest rank in Paradise is a place called "al-Wasilah" (the means), due to its nearness to the Throne, and it is the dwelling place of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ in Paradise, as the Imam Ahmad [ibn Hanbal] said:

[chain] Abd al-Razzaq told us, Sufyan informed us, from Layth, from Ka'b, from Abu Hurayrah, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When you invoke blessings upon me, ask Allah for al-Wasilah for me." It was said: O Messenger of Allah, what is al-Wasilah? He said: "The highest level in Paradise, which none attains except a single man, and I hope that I am he."

And in the Sahih of Muslim, from the hadith of Ka'b ibn Alqamah, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Jubayr, from Abdullah ibn Amr ibn al-As, that he heard the Prophet ﷺ say: "When you hear the caller to prayer, say the like of what he says, then invoke blessings upon me, for whoever invokes blessings upon me once, Allah invokes blessings upon him tenfold because of it. Then ask for al-Wasilah for me, for it is a rank in Paradise fitting for none but a servant among Allah's servants, and I hope that I am he. So whoever asks for al-Wasilah for me, intercession becomes permissible for him on the Day of Resurrection."

[And in the Sahih of al-Bukhari, from the hadith of Muhammad ibn al-Munkadir, from Jabir, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Whoever says, upon hearing the call to prayer: O Allah, Lord of this complete call and of the established prayer, grant Muhammad al-Wasilah and superiority, and raise him to the praised station which You have promised him, then intercession becomes permissible for him on the Day of Resurrection."]

And the Hafiz Abu al-Qasim al-Tabarani said: [chain] Ahmad ibn Ali al-Abbar told us, al-Walid ibn Abd al-Malik al-Harrani told us, Musa ibn A'yan told us, from Ibn Abi Dhi'b, from Muhammad ibn Amr ibn Ata, from Ibn Abbas, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Ask Allah for al-Wasilah for me, for no servant asks for it for me in this world except that I will be a witness for him, or an intercessor, on the Day of Resurrection."

And in the Musnad of Imam Ahmad, from the hadith of Sa'd Abu Mujahid al-Ta'i, from Abu al-Mudalla, from Abu Hurayrah, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: We said: O Messenger of Allah, tell us about Paradise, what is its construction? He said: "A brick of gold and a brick of silver, its mortar is musk, its pebbles are pearls and rubies, its soil is saffron. Whoever enters it lives in bliss without misery, abides forever without dying, his garments never wear out, and his youth never fades."

And it is narrated from Ibn Umar, as a raised report, something similar. And with al-Tirmidhi, from the hadith of Abd al-Rahman ibn Ishaq, from al-Nu'man ibn Sa'd, from Ali, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "In Paradise there are indeed chambers whose exteriors are seen from their interiors, and whose interiors are seen from their exteriors." A bedouin stood and said: O Messenger of Allah, for whom are they? He said: "For whoever makes his speech good, feeds others, continually fasts, and prays at night while people are asleep."

Then he said: This is a gharib (singular) hadith.

And al-Tabarani transmitted it, from the hadith of Abdullah ibn Amr and Abu Malik al-Ashari, each of them from the Prophet ﷺ, with similar wording. Each of the two chains is good and sound (hasan), and according to him the questioner was "Abu Malik," but Allah knows best.

And from Usamah ibn Zayd, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Is there one who girds himself up for Paradise? For Paradise has no equal in value. It is, by the Lord of the Ka'bah, a light that gleams, a fragrant herb that sways, a lofty palace, a flowing river, ripe fruit, a beautiful and lovely spouse, abundant garments, and an abode in eternity, in a sound dwelling, with fruit, greenery, joy, and blessing, in an elevated and radiant abode." They said: Yes, O Messenger of Allah, we are the ones who gird ourselves up for it. He said: "Say: if Allah wills." So the people said: If Allah wills. Ibn Majah transmitted it.

And the Almighty's saying, {and approval from Allah, which is greater}, that is: Allah's approval of them is greater, more majestic, and more magnificent than what they are in of bliss, as Imam Malik, may Allah have mercy on him, said, from Zayd ibn Aslam, from Ata ibn Yasar, from Abu Sa'id al-Khudri, may Allah be pleased with him, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Allah, Mighty and Majestic, will say to the people of Paradise: O people of Paradise! They will say: At Your service, our Lord, and at Your beck and call, and all good is in Your hand. He will say: Are you pleased? They will say: How could we not be pleased, O Lord, when You have given us what You have not given to any other of Your creation? He will say: Shall I not give you something better than that? They will say: O Lord, what could be better than that? He will say: I bestow upon you My approval, and I shall never be angry with you after it, ever." Both [Bukhari and Muslim] transmitted it from the hadith of Malik.

And Abu Abdullah al-Husayn ibn Isma'il al-Mahamili said: [chain] al-Fadl al-Rukhami told us, al-Firyabi told us, from Sufyan, from Muhammad ibn al-Munkadir, from Jabir ibn Abdullah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "When the people of Paradise enter Paradise, Allah, Mighty and Majestic, will say: Do you desire anything that I may increase you with? They will say: O our Lord, what is better than what You have already given us? He will say: My approval is greater."

And al-Bazzar transmitted it in his Musnad, from the hadith of al-Thawri. And the Hafiz al-Diya al-Maqdisi said in his book "The Description of Paradise": This, in my view, meets the conditions of a sound (sahih) hadith, and Allah knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى بِمَا أَعَدَّهُ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ بِهِ وَالْمُؤْمِنَاتِ مِنَ الْخَيْرَاتِ وَالنَّعِيمِ الْمُقِيمِ فِي ﴿جَنَّاتٍ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الأنْهَارُ خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا﴾ أَيْ: مَاكِثِينَ فِيهَا أَبَدًا، ﴿وَمَسَاكِنَ طَيِّبَةً﴾ أَيْ: حَسَنَةَ الْبِنَاءِ، طَيِّبَةَ الْقَرَارِ، كَمَا جَاءَ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي عِمْرَانَ الْجَوْنِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ أَبِي مُوسَى عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ قَيْسٍ الْأَشْعَرِيِّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "جَنَّتَانِ مِنْ ذَهَبٍ آنِيَتُهُمَا وَمَا فِيهِمَا، وَجَنَّتَانِ مِنْ فِضَّةٍ آنِيَتُهُمَا وَمَا فِيهِمَا، وَمَا بَيْنَ الْقَوْمِ وَبَيْنَ أَنْ يَنْظُرُوا إِلَى رَبِّهِمْ إِلَّا رِدَاءُ الْكِبْرِيَاءِ عَلَى وَجْهِهِ فِي جَنَّةِ عَدْنٍ" 

وَبِهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ لِلْمُؤْمِنِ فِي الْجَنَّةِ لَخَيْمَة مِنْ لُؤْلُؤَةٍ وَاحِدَةٍ مُجَوَّفة، طُولُهَا سِتُّونَ مِيلًا فِي السَّمَاءِ، لِلْمُؤْمِنِ فِيهَا أَهْلُونَ يَطُوفُ عَلَيْهِمْ، لَا يَرَى بَعْضُهُمْ بَعْضًا" أَخْرَجَاهُ 

وَفِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ أَيْضًا، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ آمَنَ بِاللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ، وَأَقَامَ الصَّلَاةَ وَصَامَ رَمَضَانَ، فَإِنَّ حَقًّا عَلَى اللَّهِ أَنْ يُدْخِلَهُ الْجَنَّةَ، هَاجَرَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، أَوْ جَلَسَ فِي أَرْضِهِ الَّتِي وُلِدَ فِيهَا". قَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، أَفَلَا نُخْبِرُ النَّاسَ؟ قَالَ: "إِنَّ فِي الْجَنَّةِ مِائَةَ دَرَجَةٍ، أَعَدَّهَا اللَّهُ لِلْمُجَاهِدِينَ فِي سَبِيلِهِ، بَيْنَ كُلِّ دَرَجَتَيْنِ كَمَا بَيْنَ السَّمَاءِ وَالْأَرْضِ، فَإِذَا سَأَلْتُمُ اللَّهَ فَاسْأَلُوهُ الْفِرْدَوْسَ، فَإِنَّهُ أَعْلَى الْجَنَّةِ وَأَوْسَطُ الْجَنَّةِ، وَمِنْهُ تَفَجَّر أَنْهَارُ الْجَنَّةِ، وَفَوْقَهُ عَرْشُ الرَّحْمَنِ" 

وَعِنْدَ الطَّبَرَانِيِّ وَالتِّرْمِذِيِّ وَابْنِ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ رِوَايَةِ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ يَسَار، عَنْ مُعَاذِ بْنِ جَبَلٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ. . . فَذَكَرَ مِثْلَهُ 

وَلِلتِّرْمِذِيِّ عَنْ عبادة بن الصامت، مثله وَعَنْ أَبِي حَازِمٍ، عَنْ سَهْلِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ لَيَتَرَاءَوْنَ الغُرفة فِي الْجَنَّةِ، كما تراؤون الْكَوْكَبَ فِي السَّمَاءِ". أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ 

ثُمَّ لِيُعْلَمَ أَنَّ أَعْلَى مَنْزِلَةٍ فِي الْجَنَّةِ مكانٌ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "الْوَسِيلَةُ" لِقُرْبِهِ مِنَ الْعَرْشِ، وَهُوَ مَسْكَنُ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ [بْنُ حَنْبَلٍ] 

حَدَّثَنَا عبد الرازق، أخبرنا سفيان، عَنْ لَيْثٍ، عَنْ كَعْبٍ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِذَا صَلَّيْتُمْ عَلَيَّ فَسَلُوا اللَّهَ لِيَ الْوَسِيلَةَ" قِيلَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، وَمَا الْوَسِيلَةُ؟ قَالَ: "أَعْلَى دَرَجَةٍ فِي الْجَنَّةِ، لَا يَنَالُهَا إِلَّا رَجُلٌ وَاحِدٌ، وَأَرْجُو أَنْ أَكُونَ أَنَا هُوَ" 

وَفِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ كَعْبِ بْنِ عَلْقَمَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ جُبَير، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ الْعَاصِ؛ أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "إِذَا سَمِعْتُمُ الْمُؤَذِّنَ فَقُولُوا مِثْلَ مَا يَقُولُ، ثُمَّ صلُّوا عليَّ، فَإِنَّهُ مَنْ صَلَّى عَلَيَّ صَلَاةً صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ بِهَا عَشْرًا، ثُمَّ سَلُوا لِيَ الْوَسِيلَةَ، فَإِنَّهَا مَنْزِلَةٌ فِي الْجَنَّةِ لَا تَنْبَغِي إِلَّا لِعَبْدٍ مِنْ عِبَادِ اللَّهِ، وَأَرْجُو أَنِّي أَكُونُ أَنَا هُوَ، فَمَنْ سَأَلَ لِيَ الْوَسِيلَةَ حلت عليه الشَّفَاعَةُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ" 

[وَفِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ الْمُنْكَدِرِ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "مَنْ قَالَ حِينَ يَسْمَعُ النِّدَاءَ: اللَّهُمَّ رَبَّ هَذِهِ الدَّعْوَةِ التَّامَّةِ وَالصَّلَاةِ الْقَائِمَةِ، آتِ مُحَمَّدًا الْوَسِيلَةَ وَالْفَضِيلَةَ، وَابْعَثْهُ مَقَامًا مَحْمُودًا الَّذِي وَعَدْتَهُ، إِلَّا حَلَتْ لَهُ الشَّفَاعَةُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ"] 

وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو الْقَاسِمِ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَلِيٍّ الْأَبَّارُ، حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ الْحَرَّانِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا مُوسَى بْنُ أَعْيَنَ، عَنِ ابْنِ أَبِي ذِئْبٍ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَطَاءٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "سَلُوا اللَّهَ لي الوسيلة، فإنه لم يسألها لي عبد فِي الدُّنْيَا إِلَّا كُنْتُ لَهُ شَهِيدًا -أَوْ شَفِيعًا -يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ" 

وَفِي مُسْنَدِ الْإِمَامِ أَحْمَدَ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ سَعْدٍ أَبِي مُجَاهِدٍ الطَّائِيِّ، عَنْ أبي المدله، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قُلْنَا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، حَدِّثْنَا عَنِ الْجَنَّةِ، مَا بِنَاؤُهَا؟ قَالَ: "لَبِنَةُ ذَهَبٍ، وَلَبِنَةُ فِضَّةٍ، وَمِلَاطُهَا الْمِسْكُ، وَحَصْبَاؤُهَا اللُّؤْلُؤُ وَالْيَاقُوتُ، وَتُرَابُهَا الزَّعْفَرَانُ، مَنْ يَدْخُلُهَا يَنْعَمُ لَا يَبْأَسُ، وَيَخْلُدُ لَا يَمُوتُ، لَا تَبْلَى ثِيَابُهُ وَلَا يَفْنَى شَبَابُهُ" 

وروي عن ابن عمر مرفوعا، نحوه وَعِنْدَ التِّرْمِذِيِّ مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ النُّعْمَانِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، عَنْ عَلِيٍّ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ فِي الْجَنَّةِ لغُرفا يُرَى ظُهُورُهَا مِنْ بُطُونِهَا، وَبُطُونُهَا مِنْ ظُهُورِهَا". فَقَامَ أَعْرَابِيٌّ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، لِمَنْ هِيَ؟ فَقَالَ: "لِمَنْ طَيَّبَ الْكَلَامَ، وَأَطْعَمَ الطَّعَامَ، وَأَدَامَ الصِّيَامَ، وَصَلَّى بِاللَّيْلِ وَالنَّاسُ نِيَامٌ" 

ثُمَّ قَالَ: حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ.

وَرَوَاهُ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو وَأَبِي مَالِكٍ الْأَشْعَرِيِّ، كُلٌّ مِنْهُمَا عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، بِنَحْوِهِ وَكُلٌّ مِنَ الْإِسْنَادَيْنِ جَيِّدٌ حَسَنٌ، وَعِنْدَهُ أَنَّ السَّائِلَ هُوَ "أَبُو مَالِكٍ"، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَعَنْ أُسَامَةَ بْنِ زَيْدٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَلَا هَلْ مُشَمِّر إِلَى الْجَنَّةِ؟ فَإِنَّ الْجَنَّةَ لَا خَطَر لَهَا، هِيَ -وَرَبِّ الْكَعْبَةِ -نُورٌ يَتَلَأْلَأُ وَرَيْحَانَةٌ تَهْتَزّ، وَقَصْرٌ مَشيدٌ، وَنَهْرٌ مُطَّرد، وَثَمَرَةٌ نَضِيجة، وَزَوْجَةٌ حَسْنَاءُ جَميلة، وحُلَل كَثِيرَةٌ، وَمَقَامٌ فِي أَبَدٍ، فِي دَارٍ سَلِيمَةٍ، وَفَاكِهَةٍ وَخُضْرَةٍ وَحَبْرَةٍ وَنَعْمَةٍ فِي مَحَلَّةٍ عَالِيَةٍ بَهِيَّةٍ". قَالُوا: نَعَمْ يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، نَحْنُ الْمُشَمِّرُونَ لَهَا، قَالَ: "قُولُوا: إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ". فَقَالَ الْقَوْمُ: إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَاجَهْ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَرِضْوَانٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ أَكْبَرُ﴾ أَيْ: رِضَا اللَّهِ عَنْهُمْ أَكْبَرُ وَأَجَلُّ وَأَعْظَمُ مِمَّا هُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ النَّعِيمِ، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ مَالِكٌ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ يَسَارٍ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ الخُدْري، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، يَقُولُ لِأَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ: يَا أَهْلَ الْجَنَّةِ، فَيَقُولُونَ: لَبَّيْكَ يَا رَبَّنَا وَسَعْدَيْكَ، وَالْخَيْرُ فِي يَدِكَ. فَيَقُولُ: هَلْ رَضِيتُمْ؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: وَمَا لَنَا لَا نَرْضَى يَا رَبِّ، وَقَدْ أَعْطَيْتَنَا مَا لَمْ تُعط أَحَدًا مِنْ خَلْقِكَ. فَيَقُولُ: أَلَا أُعْطِيكُمْ أَفْضَلَ مِنْ ذَلِكَ؟ فَيَقُولُونَ: يَا رَبِّ، وَأَيُّ شَيْءٍ أَفْضَلُ مِنْ ذَلِكَ؟ فَيَقُولُ: أُحِلُّ عَلَيْكُمْ رِضْوَانِي فَلَا أَسْخَطُ عَلَيْكُمْ بَعْدَهُ أَبَدًا" أَخْرَجَاهُ مِنْ حَدِيثِ مَالِكٍ 

وَقَالَ أَبُو عَبْدِ اللَّهِ الْحُسَيْنُ بْنُ إِسْمَاعِيلَ الْمَحَامِلِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا الْفَضْلُ الرُّخاميّ، حَدَّثَنَا الفِرْياني، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ، عَنْ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ المُنْكَدِر، عَنْ جَابِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِذَا دَخَلَ أَهْلُ الْجَنَّةِ الْجَنَّةَ قَالَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: هَلْ تَشْتَهُونَ شَيْئًا فَأَزِيدُكُمْ؟ قَالُوا: يَا رَبَّنَا، مَا خَيْرٌ مِمَّا أعطيتنا؟ قال: رضواني أكبر".

وَرَوَاهُ الْبَزَّارُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ الثَّوْرِيِّ وَقَالَ الْحَافِظُ الضِّيَاءُ الْمَقْدِسِيُّ فِي كِتَابِهِ "صِفَةِ الْجَنَّةِ": هَذَا عِنْدِي عَلَى شَرْطِ الصَّحِيحِ، واللَّهُ أعلم.

---

## 9:73-74 — verses 73-74 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty commanded His Messenger ﷺ to struggle against the disbelievers and the hypocrites and to be harsh with them, just as He commanded him to lower his wing to those believers who followed him, and He informed him that the destination of the disbelievers and the hypocrites in the hereafter would be the Fire. It has already been related from the Commander of the Believers, Ali ibn Abi Talib, that he said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was sent with four swords: a sword for the polytheists: {And when the sacred months have passed, then kill the polytheists} [al-Tawbah: 5]; a sword for the disbelievers among the People of the Book: {Fight those who do not believe in Allah nor in the Last Day, and who do not forbid what Allah and His Messenger have forbidden, and who do not follow the religion of truth, from among those who were given the Book, until they pay the jizyah (tribute tax) willingly while being humbled} [al-Tawbah: 29]; a sword for the hypocrites: {Strive against the disbelievers and the hypocrites} [al-Tawbah: 73, al-Tahrim: 9]; and a sword for the rebellious factions: {Then fight the one that transgresses until it returns to the command of Allah} [al-Hujurat: 9].

This implies that they are to be fought with swords if they openly display hypocrisy, and this is the view chosen by Ibn Jarir.

Ibn Mas'ud said regarding His statement, the Almighty: {Strive against the disbelievers and the hypocrites}, "With his hand, and if he is not able, then with his tongue, and if he is not able, then with his heart, and if he is not able, then let him frown in his face."

Ibn Abbas said: Allah, the Almighty, commanded him to strive against the disbelievers with the sword, and against the hypocrites with the tongue, and removed gentleness from him regarding them.

Al-Dahhak said: Strive against the disbelievers with the sword, and be harsh with the hypocrites through speech, and that is the striving against them. The same is reported from Muqatil and al-Rabi'.

Al-Hasan and Qatadah said: Striving against them means establishing the prescribed legal punishments (hudud) upon them.

It may be said that there is no contradiction between these statements, for sometimes he would take them to task by this means and sometimes by that, according to circumstances. And Allah knows best.

Regarding His statement: {They swear by Allah that they did not say it, but they had certainly said the word of disbelief and disbelieved after their (outward) submission (Islam)}, Qatadah said: it was revealed concerning Abdullah ibn Ubayy. This was because two men had fought, a man from Juhaynah and a man from the Ansar, and the Juhani man overcame the Ansari man. So Abdullah said to the Ansar: "Will you not help your brother? By Allah, our case and the case of Muhammad is only as the poet said: 'Fatten your dog and it will eat you.'" And he said: {If we return to Madinah, the mightier will surely expel from it the meaner} [al-Munafiqun: 8]. A man among the Muslims reported this to the Prophet ﷺ, so he sent for him and asked him, and he began to swear by Allah that he had not said it. So Allah revealed this verse concerning him.

Isma'il ibn Ibrahim ibn Uqbah related from his uncle Musa ibn Uqbah, who said: Abdullah ibn al-Fadl told us that he heard Anas ibn Malik, may Allah be pleased with him, say: I grieved over those of my people who were struck at al-Harrah. So Zayd ibn Arqam wrote to me, having heard of the intensity of my grief, mentioning that he had heard the Messenger of Allah ﷺ say: "O Allah, forgive the Ansar and the sons of the Ansar," (Ibn al-Fadl was uncertain whether it included "the sons of the sons of the Ansar" as well). Ibn al-Fadl said: Someone who was with Anas asked him about Zayd ibn Arqam, and he said: He is the one to whom the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said, "Allah has fulfilled what his ear heard as true." That was when he heard a man among the hypocrites say, while the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was delivering a sermon: "If this man is truthful, then we are worse than donkeys." Zayd ibn Arqam said: "By Allah, he is indeed truthful, and you are worse than a donkey." Then that was reported to the Messenger of Allah, and the speaker denied it, so Allah revealed this verse confirming Zayd, meaning His statement: {They swear by Allah that they did not say it} to the end of the verse.

This was related by al-Bukhari in his Sahih, from Isma'il ibn Abi Uways, from Isma'il ibn Ibrahim ibn Uqbah, up to the statement "this is the one for whom Allah fulfilled what his ear heard as true." What comes after this may be from the words of Musa ibn Uqbah himself. It was also related by Muhammad ibn Fulayh from Musa ibn Uqbah with his chain, and then he said: "Ibn Shihab said," and he mentioned what follows from Musa, from Ibn Shihab.

The well known account of this story is that it took place during the expedition against Banu al-Mustaliq, so perhaps the narrator erred in mentioning this particular verse, intending to mention another one but mentioning this instead. And Allah knows best.

[Marginal note]

Al-Umawi said in his Maghazi: Muhammad ibn Ishaq told us, from al-Zuhri, from Abd al-Rahman ibn Abdullah ibn Ka'b ibn Malik, from his grandfather, who said: When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ arrived, my people took me aside and said: "You are a poet, so if you wish to excuse yourself to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ with some pretext, do so, for it would then be a sin for which you could seek Allah's forgiveness." And he mentioned the hadith at length, until he said: Among those who stayed behind from among the hypocrites, and concerning whom the Qur'an was revealed, among those who had been with the Prophet ﷺ, was al-Julas ibn Suwayd ibn al-Samit. He was married to the mother of Umayr ibn Sa'd, and Umayr was under his guardianship. When the Qur'an was revealed and Allah mentioned them with what He revealed concerning the hypocrites, al-Julas said: "By Allah, if this man is truthful in what he says, then we are worse than donkeys." Umayr ibn Sa'd heard this and said: "By Allah, O Julas, you are the most beloved of people to me, and the best of them to me in terms of good treatment, and the dearest to me such that nothing distressing should reach you. Yet you have said a statement such that if I mention it, it will surely disgrace you, and if I conceal it, it will surely destroy me, and one of the two is easier for me than the other." So he went to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and told him what al-Julas had said. When this reached al-Julas, he went out to the Prophet ﷺ and swore by Allah that he had not said what Umayr ibn Sa'd had said, and that Umayr had lied against him. So Allah, mighty and majestic, revealed concerning him: {They swear by Allah that they did not say it, but they had certainly said the word of disbelief and disbelieved after their (outward) submission (Islam)} to the end of the verse. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ then confronted him with it. They claim that al-Julas repented, and his repentance was good, and he withdrew from his hypocrisy in a good manner. This account comes as an inserted (mudraj, interpolated) addition connected to the hadith, and it seems, Allah knows best, to be from the words of Ibn Ishaq himself, not from the words of Ka'b ibn Malik.

Urwah ibn al-Zubayr said: This verse was revealed concerning al-Julas ibn Suwayd ibn al-Samit. He and his wife's son Mus'ab came from Quba, and al-Julas said: "If what Muhammad has brought is true, then we are worse than these donkeys of ours that we are riding." Mus'ab said: "By Allah, O enemy of Allah, I will surely inform the Messenger of Allah ﷺ of what you have said." So I came to the Prophet ﷺ, and I feared that either the Qur'an would be revealed concerning me, or some calamity would strike me, or that I would be implicated in his sin. So I said: "O Messenger of Allah, al-Julas and I came from Quba, and he said such and such, and were it not for my fear of being implicated in a sin or of some calamity striking me, I would not have told you." He said: He then called al-Julas and said: "O Julas, did you say what Mus'ab said?" He swore that he had not, so Allah revealed: {They swear by Allah that they did not say it, but they had certainly said the word of disbelief and disbelieved after their (outward) submission (Islam)} to the end of the verse.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: The one who made that statement, as it has reached me, was al-Julas ibn Suwayd ibn al-Samit. A man who was under his guardianship, called Umayr ibn Sa'id, reported it against him. He denied it and swore by Allah that he had not said it. But when the Qur'an was revealed concerning him, he repented and withdrew from his hypocrisy, and his repentance was good, as it has reached me.

The imam Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir said: [chain] from Ibn Abbas, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ was sitting in the shade of a tree and said: "A man will come to you who looks at you with the eyes of Satan, so when he comes, do not speak to him." Before long, a blue eyed man appeared, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ called him and said: "Why do you and your companions curse me?" The man went off and brought his companions, and they swore by Allah that they had not said it, until he overlooked it from them. Then Allah, mighty and majestic, revealed: {They swear by Allah that they did not say it}.

The verse.

This is clear from what the Hafiz Abu Bakr al-Bayhaqi related in his book "Dala'il al-Nubuwwah" from the hadith of Muhammad ibn Ishaq, from al-A'mash, from Amr ibn Murrah, from [Abu] al-Bakhtari, from Hudhayfah ibn al-Yaman, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: I was holding the halter of the she-camel of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, leading it, while Ammar was driving it from behind, or I was driving it and Ammar was leading it, until when we were at the mountain pass, I suddenly saw twelve riders who had blocked it there. He said: I alerted the Messenger of Allah ﷺ to them, so he shouted at them and they turned away fleeing. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to us: "Did you recognize the people?" We said: No, O Messenger of Allah, they were veiled, but we recognized the mounts. He said: "These are the hypocrites until the Day of Resurrection. Do you know what they intended?" We said: No. He said: "They intended to crowd the Messenger of Allah at the mountain pass and throw him from it." We said: O Messenger of Allah, will you not send word to their clans so that each people sends you the head of their man? He said: "I do not want the Arabs to say among themselves that Muhammad fought with a people until, when Allah gave him victory through them, he turned against them and killed them." Then he said: "O Allah, strike them with the dubaylah (internal boil/abscess)." We said: O Messenger of Allah, what is the dubaylah? He said: "A flame of fire that falls upon the nerve that hangs the heart of one of them, and he perishes."

Imam Ahmad, may Allah have mercy on him, said: Yazid told us, al-Walid ibn Abdullah ibn Jumay' informed us, from Abu al-Tufayl, who said: When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was returning from the expedition of Tabuk, he ordered a caller who called out: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ has taken the mountain pass, so let no one else take it. While the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was being led by Hudhayfah and driven by Ammar, a group of veiled men came on their mounts and closed in on Ammar as he was driving the Messenger of Allah's mount. Ammar, may Allah be pleased with him, began striking the faces of their mounts. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to Hudhayfah: "Enough, enough," until the Messenger of Allah ﷺ descended. When he had descended, he dismounted and Ammar returned. He said: "O Ammar, did you recognize the people?" He said: I recognized most of the mounts, but the people were veiled. He said: "Do you know what they intended?" He said: Allah and His Messenger know best. He said: "They intended to startle the mount of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ so that they might throw him down." He said: Ammar then whispered to a man among the companions of the Prophet ﷺ and said: I ask you by Allah, how many do you know were the companions of the mountain pass? He said: Fourteen. He said: If you were one of them, then they were fifteen. He said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ excused three of them, who said: By Allah, we did not hear the caller of the Messenger of Allah, and we did not know what the people intended. Ammar said: I bear witness that the remaining twelve are at war with Allah and His Messenger in this worldly life and on the Day when the witnesses will stand.

Likewise Ibn Lahi'ah related, from Abu al-Aswad, from Urwah ibn al-Zubayr, something similar to this, and that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ ordered the people to walk in the bottom of the valley, while he himself, along with Hudhayfah and Ammar, climbed the mountain pass. These base men followed them, veiled, intending to take the pass as well. Allah informed the Messenger of Allah ﷺ of their intention, so he ordered Hudhayfah, who turned back to them and struck the faces of their mounts. They were startled and turned back disgraced. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ informed Hudhayfah and Ammar of their names and of what they had intended in the way of assassinating him ﷺ, and he ordered the two of them to keep it secret from the rest.

Likewise Yunus ibn Bukayr related from Ibn Ishaq, except that he named a group of them. Allah knows best.

This is also recounted in the Mu'jam of al-Tabarani, as al-Bayhaqi said. What Muslim related bears witness to the authenticity of this account:

[chain] Zuhayr ibn Harb told us, Abu Ahmad al-Kufi told us, al-Walid ibn Jumay' told us, Abu al-Tufayl told us, who said: Between a man from the people of the mountain pass and Hudhayfah there occurred some of what occurs between people. He said: I ask you by Allah, how many were the companions of the mountain pass? The people said to him: Tell him, since he has asked you. He said: We were told they were fourteen. If you were one of them, then the people were fifteen. And I bear witness by Allah that twelve of them are at war with Allah and His Messenger in this worldly life and on the Day when the witnesses will stand, and he excused three who said: We did not hear the caller of the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, nor did we know what the people intended. He had been at a lava plain and had walked on, and had said: "The water is scarce, so let no one precede me to it," but he found a group who had already preceded him to it, so he cursed them that day.

And what Muslim also related, from the hadith of Qatadah, from Abu Nadrah, from Qays ibn Abbad, from Ammar ibn Yasir, who said: Hudhayfah informed me, from the Prophet ﷺ, that he said: "Among my companions are twelve hypocrites who will not enter Paradise and will not smell its fragrance until the camel passes through the eye of the needle. Eight of them, the dubaylah will suffice for you against them: a flame of fire that appears between their shoulder blades until it emerges from their chests."

For this reason Hudhayfah was called "the man of the secret which no one else knows," meaning, regarding the identification of a group of hypocrites, these being them, whom the Messenger of Allah ﷺ informed him of and no one else. Allah knows best. Al-Tabarani, in the section on the transmissions of Hudhayfah, gave a chapter naming the companions of the mountain pass, then related from Ali ibn Abd al-Aziz, from al-Zubayr ibn Bakkar, that he said: They were Mu'attib ibn Qushayr, Wadi'ah ibn Thabit, Jadd ibn Abdullah ibn Nabtal ibn al-Harith of Banu Amr ibn Awf, al-Harith ibn Yazid al-Ta'i, Aws ibn Qayzi, al-Harith ibn Suwayd, Sa'd ibn Zurarah, Qays ibn Fahd, Suwayd and Da'is of Banu al-Hubuli, Qays ibn Amr ibn Sahl, Zayd ibn al-Lasit, and Sulalah ibn al-Himam, the latter two being from Banu Qaynuqa who outwardly professed Islam.

His statement: {And they found nothing to resent except that Allah and His Messenger had enriched them out of His bounty}, means: the Messenger has no fault in their eyes except that Allah enriched them by his blessing and by the good fortune of his mission. Had good fortune been complete for them, Allah would have guided them to what he brought, just as he, peace be upon him, said to the Ansar: "Did I not find you astray, and Allah guided you through me? And you were scattered, and Allah united you through me? And you were destitute, and Allah enriched you through me?" Every time he said something, they would say: Allah and His Messenger have bestowed the greater favor.

This form of expression is used where there is no real fault, as Allah says: {And they resented them for nothing except that they believed in Allah, the Mighty, the Praiseworthy} [al-Buruj: 8], and as he, peace be upon him, said: "Ibn Jamil resents nothing except that he was poor and Allah enriched him."

Then Allah, Blessed and Exalted, called them to repentance, saying: {If they repent, it will be better for them, but if they turn away, Allah will punish them with a painful punishment in this world and the next}, meaning: if they persist in their way, {Allah will punish them with a painful punishment in this world}, that is, through killing and worry and distress, {and the next}, that is, through punishment, disgrace, humiliation, and abasement. {And they will have no protector or helper on earth}, meaning: they have no one to bring them good fortune, nor to aid them, nor to secure any good for them, nor to repel any harm from them.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

أَمَرَ تَعَالَى رَسُولَهُ ﷺ بِجِهَادِ الْكُفَّارِ وَالْمُنَافِقِينَ وَالْغِلْظَةِ عَلَيْهِمْ، كَمَا أَمَرَهُ بِأَنْ يَخْفِضَ جَنَاحَهُ لِمَنِ اتَّبَعَهُ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَأَخْبَرَهُ أَنَّ مَصِيرَ الْكُفَّارِ وَالْمُنَافِقِينَ إِلَى النَّارِ فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ. وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ عَنْ أَمِيرِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَلِيِّ بْنِ أَبِي طَالِبٍ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: بَعَثَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِأَرْبَعَةِ أَسْيَافٍ، سَيْفٍ لِلْمُشْرِكِينَ: ﴿فَإِذَا انْسَلَخَ الأشْهُرُ الْحُرُمُ فَاقْتُلُوا الْمُشْرِكِينَ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ:٥] وَسَيْفٍ لِلْكُفَّارِ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ: ﴿قَاتِلُوا الَّذِينَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَلا بِالْيَوْمِ الآخِرِ وَلا يُحَرِّمُونَ مَا حَرَّمَ اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ وَلا يَدِينُونَ دِينَ الْحَقِّ مِنَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ حَتَّى يُعْطُوا الْجِزْيَةَ عَنْ يَدٍ وَهُمْ صَاغِرُونَ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ:٢٩] وَسَيْفٍ لِلْمُنَافِقِينَ: ﴿جَاهِدِ الْكُفَّارَ وَالْمُنَافِقِينَ﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ:٧٣، التَّحْرِيمِ:٩] وَسَيْفٍ لِلْبُغَاةِ: ﴿فَقَاتِلُوا الَّتِي تَبْغِي حَتَّى تَفِيءَ إِلَى أَمْرِ اللَّهِ﴾ [الْحُجُرَاتِ:٩]

وَهَذَا يَقْتَضِي أَنَّهُمْ يُجَاهَدُونَ بِالسُّيُوفِ إِذَا أَظْهَرُوا النِّفَاقَ، وَهُوَ اخْتِيَارُ ابْنِ جَرِيرٍ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿جَاهِدِ الْكُفَّارَ وَالْمُنَافِقِينَ﴾ قَالَ: بِيَدِهِ، [فَإِنْ لَمْ يَسْتَطِعْ فَبِلِسَانِهِ فَإِنْ لَمْ يَسْتَطِعْ فَبِقَلْبِهِ] فَإِنْ لَمْ يَسْتَطِعْ فَلْيَكْفَهِرَّ فِي وَجْهِهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: أَمَرَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى بِجِهَادِ الْكُفَّارِ بِالسَّيْفِ، وَالْمُنَافِقِينَ بِاللِّسَانِ، وَأَذْهَبَ الرِّفْقَ عَنْهُمْ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ: جَاهِدِ الْكُفَّارَ بِالسَّيْفِ، وَاغْلُظْ عَلَى الْمُنَافِقِينَ بِالْكَلَامِ، وَهُوَ مُجَاهَدَتُهُمْ. وَعَنْ مُقَاتِلٍ، وَالرَّبِيعِ مِثْلُهُ.
