وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ التِّرْمِذِيُّ فِي "التَّفْسِيرِ" مِنْ حَدِيثِ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، بِهِ وَقَالَ: حَسَنٌ صَحِيحٌ. وَرَوَاهُ الْبُخَارِيُّ عَنْ يَحْيَى بْنِ بُكَير، عَنِ اللَّيْثِ، عَنْ عُقَيل، عَنِ الزُّهْرِيِّ، بِهِ، فَذَكَرَ مِثْلَهُ وَقَالَ: "أَخِّرْ عَنِّي يَا عُمَرُ". فَلَمَّا أَكْثَرْتُ عَلَيْهِ قَالَ: "إنِّي خُيِّرت فاخترتُ، وَلَوْ أَعْلَمُ أَنَّى إِنْ زِدْتُ عَلَى السَّبْعِينَ يُغْفَر لَهُ لَزِدْتُ عَلَيْهَا". قَالَ: فَصَلَّى عَلَيْهِ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ ثم انْصَرَفَ، فَلَمْ يَلْبَثْ إِلَّا يَسِيرًا حَتَّى نَزَلَتِ الْآيَتَانِ مِنْ بَرَاءَةَ: ﴿وَلا تُصَلِّ عَلَى أَحَدٍ مِنْهُمْ مَاتَ أَبَدًا وَلا تَقُمْ عَلَى قَبْرِهِ﴾ الْآيَةَ، فعجبتُ بَعْدُ مِنْ جُرْأتي عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَرَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَعْلَمُ. 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ أَبِي عُبَيد، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْمَلِكِ، عَنْ أَبِي الزُّبَيْرِ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا مَاتَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أُبَيٍّ، أَتَى ابْنُهُ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّكَ إِنْ لَمْ تَأْتِهِ لَمْ نَزَلْ نُعَيَّر بِهَذَا. فَأَتَاهُ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ، فَوَجَدَهُ قَدْ أُدْخِلَ فِي حُفْرَتِهِ، فَقَالَ: أَفَلَا قَبْلَ أَنْ تُدْخِلُوهُ! فَأخرجَ مِنْ حُفرته، وتَفَل عَلَيْهِ مِنْ قَرْنِهِ إِلَى قَدَمِهِ، وَأَلْبَسَهُ قَمِيصَهُ.

وَرَوَاهُ النَّسَائِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي دَاوُدَ الْحَرَّانِيِّ، عَنْ يَعْلَى بْنِ عُبَيْدٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْمَلِكِ -وَهُوَ ابْنُ أَبِي سُلَيْمَانَ بِهِ 

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عُثْمَانَ، أَخْبَرَنَا ابْنُ عُيَينة، عَنْ عَمْرٍو، سَمِعَ جَابِرَ بْنَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: أَتَى النَّبِيُّ ﷺ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ أُبَيٍّ بَعْدَ مَا أُدْخِلَ فِي قَبْرِهِ، فَأَمَرَ بِهِ فَأُخْرِجَ، وَوُضِعَ عَلَى رُكْبَتَيْهِ، وَنَفَثَ عَلَيْهِ مِنْ رِيقِهِ، وَأَلْبَسَهُ قَمِيصَهُ، واللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ 

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ أَيْضًا فِي غَيْرِ مَوْضِعٍ مَعَ مُسْلِمٍ وَالنَّسَائِيِّ، مِنْ غَيْرِ وَجْهٍ، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ بْنِ عُيَيْنَةَ، بِهِ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ أَحْمَدُ بْنُ عَمْرِو بْنِ عَبْدِ الْخَالِقِ الْبَزَّارُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ: حَدَّثَنَا عَمْرُو بْنُ عَلِيٍّ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى، حَدَّثَنَا مُجَالِدٌ، حَدَّثَنَا عَامِرٌ، حَدَّثَنَا جَابِرٌ (ح) وَحَدَّثَنَا يُوسُفُ بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ مَغْرَاءَ الدَّوْسِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا مُجَالِدٌ، عَنِ الشَّعْبِيِّ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ قَالَ: لَمَّا مَاتَ رَأْسُ الْمُنَافِقِينَ -قَالَ يَحْيَى بْنُ سَعِيدٍ: بِالْمَدِينَةِ -فَأَوْصَى أَنْ يُصَلِّيَ عَلَيْهِ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ، فَجَاءَ ابْنُهُ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم فقال: إِنَّ أَبِي أَوْصَى أَنْ يُكَفَّنَ فِي قَمِيصِكَ -وَهَذَا الْكَلَامُ فِي حَدِيثِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ مَغْرَاءَ -قَالَ يَحْيَى فِي حَدِيثِهِ: فَصَلَّى عَلَيْهِ، وَأَلْبَسَهُ قَمِيصَهُ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلا تُصَلِّ عَلَى أَحَدٍ مِنْهُمْ مَاتَ أَبَدًا وَلا تَقُمْ عَلَى قَبْرِهِ﴾ وَزَادَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ: وَخَلَعَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ قَمِيصَهُ، فَأَعْطَاهُ إِيَّاهُ، وَمَشَى فَصَلَّى عَلَيْهِ، وَقَامَ عَلَى قَبْرِهِ، فَأَتَاهُ جِبْرِيلُ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، لَمَّا وَلَّى قَالَ: ﴿وَلا تُصَلِّ عَلَى أَحَدٍ مِنْهُمْ مَاتَ أَبَدًا وَلا تَقُمْ عَلَى قَبْرِهِ﴾ وَهَذَا إِسْنَادٌ لَا بَأْسَ بِهِ، وَمَا قَبْلَهُ شَاهِدٌ لَهُ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو جَعْفَرٍ الطَّبَرِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا [أَحْمَدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، حَدَّثَنَا] أَبُو أَحْمَدَ، حَدَّثَنَا حَمَّادُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ، عَنْ يَزِيدَ الرَّقَاشِيِّ، عَنْ أَنَسٍ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَرَادَ أَنْ يُصَلِّيَ عَلَى عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبَيٍّ، فَأَخَذَ جِبْرِيلُ بِثَوْبِهِ وَقَالَ: ﴿وَلا تُصَلِّ عَلَى أَحَدٍ مِنْهُمْ مَاتَ أَبَدًا وَلا تَقُمْ عَلَى قَبْرِهِ﴾

وَرَوَاهُ الْحَافِظُ أَبُو يَعْلَى فِي مُسْنَدِهِ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ يَزِيدَ الرَّقَاشِيِّ وَهُوَ ضَعِيفٌ.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: أَرْسَلَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أُبَيٍّ إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ وَهُوَ مَرِيضٌ، فَلَمَّا دَخَلَ عَلَيْهِ قَالَ لَهُ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "أَهْلَكَكَ حُبُّ يَهُودٍ". قَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّمَا أرسلتُ إِلَيْكَ لِتَسْتَغْفِرَ لِي، وَلَمْ أُرْسِلْ إِلَيْكَ لِتُؤَنِّبَنِي! ثُمَّ سَأَلَهُ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ أَنْ يُعْطِيَهُ قَمِيصَهُ أَنْ يُكَفِّنَ فِيهِ أَبَاهُ، فَأَعْطَاهُ إِيَّاهُ، وَصَلَّى عَلَيْهِ، وَقَامَ عَلَى قَبْرِهِ، فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿وَلا تُصَلِّ عَلَى أَحَدٍ مِنْهُمْ مَاتَ أَبَدًا وَلا تَقُمْ عَلَى قَبْرِهِ﴾

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ أَنَّهُ إِنَّمَا أَلْبَسَهُ قَمِيصَهُ؛ لِأَنَّ عَبْدَ اللَّهِ بْنَ أُبيّ لَمَّا قَدِمَ الْعَبَّاسُ طُلب لَهُ قَمِيصٌ، فَلَمْ يُوجَد عَلَى تَفْصِيلِهِ إِلَّا ثَوْبُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أُبيّ؛ لِأَنَّهُ كَانَ ضَخْمًا طَوِيلًا فَفَعَلَ ذَلِكَ بِهِ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ، مُكَافَأَةً لَهُ، فَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ، وَلِهَذَا كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بَعْدَ نُزُولِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ عَلَيْهِ لَا يُصَلِّي عَلَى أَحَدٍ مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ، وَلَا يَقُومُ عَلَى قَبْرِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، حَدَّثَنِي عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ أَبِي قَتَادَةَ عَنْ أَبِيهِ قَالَ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِذَا دُعِيَ لِجِنَازَةٍ سَأَلَ عَنْهَا، فَإِنْ أُثْنِيَ عَلَيْهَا خَيْرًا قَامَ فَصَلَّى عَلَيْهَا، وَإِنْ أُثْنِيَ عَلَيْهَا غَيْرَ ذَلِكَ قَالَ لِأَهْلِهَا: "شَأْنُكُمْ بِهَا"، وَلَمْ يُصَلِّ عَلَيْهَا 

وَكَانَ عُمَرُ بْنُ الْخَطَّابِ لَا يُصَلِّي عَلَى جِنَازَةِ مَنْ جُهِل حَالُهُ، حَتَّى يُصَلِّيَ عَلَيْهَا حُذَيْفَةُ بْنُ الْيَمَانِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ كَانَ يَعْلَمُ أَعْيَانَ مُنَافِقِينَ قَدْ أَخْبَرَهُ بِهِمْ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ؛ وَلِهَذَا كَانَ يُقَالُ لَهُ: "صَاحِبُ السِّرِّ" الَّذِي لا يعلمه غيره أي من الصحابة.

وَقَالَ أَبُو عُبَيد فِي كِتَابِ "الْغَرِيبِ"، فِي حَدِيثِ عُمَر أَنَّهُ أَرَادَ أَنْ يُصَلِّيَ عَلَى جِنَازَةِ رَجُلٍ، فَمرَزَه حُذيفة، كَأَنَّهُ أَرَادَ أَنْ يَصُده عَنِ الصَّلَاةِ عَلَيْهَا، ثُمَّ حُكِيَ عَنْ بَعْضِهِمْ أَنَّ "الْمَرْزَ" بِلُغَةِ أَهْلِ الْيَمَامَةِ هُوَ: القَرْص بِأَطْرَافِ الْأَصَابِعِ.

وَلَمَّا نَهَى اللَّهُ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ، عَنِ الصَّلَاةِ عَلَى الْمُنَافِقِينَ وَالْقِيَامِ عَلَى قُبُورِهِمْ لِلِاسْتِغْفَارِ لَهُمْ، كَانَ هَذَا الصنيعُ مِنْ أَكْبَرِ القُرُبات فِي حَقِّ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، فَشَرَعَ ذَلِكَ. وَفِي فِعْلِهِ الْأَجْرُ الْجَزِيلُ، لِمَا ثَبَتَ فِي الصِّحَاحِ وَغَيْرِهَا مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم قال: "مَنْ شَهِدَ الْجِنَازَةَ حَتَّى يُصَلِّيَ عَلَيْهَا فَلَهُ قِيرَاطٌ، وَمَنْ شَهِدَهَا حَتَّى تُدْفَنَ فَلَهُ قِيرَاطَانِ". قِيلَ: وَمَا الْقِيرَاطَانِ؟ قَالَ: "أَصْغَرُهُمَا مِثْلُ أُحُدٍ" 

وَأَمَّا الْقِيَامُ عِنْدَ قَبْرِ الْمُؤْمِنِ إِذَا مَاتَ فَقَدْ قَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ: حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ مُوسَى الرَّازِيُّ، أَخْبَرَنَا هِشَامٌ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ بَحير، عَنْ هَانِئٍ -وَهُوَ أَبُو سَعِيدٍ الْبَرْبَرِيُّ، مَوْلَى عُثْمَانَ بْنِ عَفَّانَ -عَنْ عُثْمَانَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: كَانَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ إِذَا فَرَغَ مِنْ دَفْنِ الرَّجُلِ وَقَفَ عَلَيْهِ وَقَالَ: "اسْتَغْفِرُوا لِأَخِيكُمْ، وَاسْأَلُوا لَهُ التَّثْبِيتَ، فَإِنَّهُ الْآنَ يُسْأَلُ".

انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ

---

## 9:85 — verse 85

### Translation

The interpretation of the like of this noble verse has already preceded, and to Allah belongs all praise.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَدْ تَقَدَّمَ تَفْسِيرُ نَظِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ وَلِلَّهِ الْحَمْدُ.

---

## 9:86-87 — verses 86-87 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says, denouncing and censuring those who held back from jihad, who shrank away from it despite having the capacity for it and possessing means and ability. They asked the Messenger's permission to remain behind and said, {Leave us, let us be with those who sit back}, and they were content for themselves with disgrace and with staying in the town among the women, who are the ones who remain behind after the army sets out. When war breaks out they are the most cowardly of people, and when there is safety they are the most talkative of people, just as the Almighty said about them in another verse: {And when fear comes you see them looking at you, their eyes rolling like one who faints from death. But when the fear departs, they lash you with sharp tongues} [al-Ahzab: 19], meaning their tongues rise up with sharp, forceful speech in times of safety, while in war they are the most cowardly of creatures. As the poet said:

"In peace they are stubborn donkeys, harsh and coarse, but in war they are like women in their menstrual seclusion."

The Almighty also said in another verse: {And those who believe say, Why has a surah not been sent down? But when a decisive surah is sent down and fighting is mentioned in it, you see those in whose hearts is disease looking at you with the look of one fainting at death. But it would be better for them to obey and speak what is right. Then when the matter is determined, if they had been true to God it would have been better for them. [Would you then, if you were given authority, cause corruption in the land]} [Muhammad: 20-22].

His saying, {and their hearts were sealed}, means: because of their shrinking back from jihad and from going out with the Messenger in the way of God. {So they do not understand}, meaning: they do not comprehend what would be good for them so as to do it, nor what would be harmful to them so as to avoid it.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى مُنْكِرًا وَذَامًّا لِلْمُتَخَلِّفِينَ عَنِ الْجِهَادِ، النَّاكِلِينَ عَنْهُ مَعَ الْقُدْرَةِ عَلَيْهِ، وَوُجُودِ السَّعَةِ والطَّوْل، وَاسْتَأْذَنُوا الرَّسُولَ فِي الْقُعُودِ، وَقَالُوا: ﴿ذَرْنَا نَكُنْ مَعَ الْقَاعِدِينَ﴾ وَرَضُوا لِأَنْفُسِهِمْ بِالْعَارِ وَالْقُعُودِ فِي الْبَلَدِ مَعَ النِّسَاءِ، وَهُنَّ الْخَوَالِفُ، بَعْدَ خُرُوجِ الْجَيْشِ، فَإِذَا وَقَعَ الْحَرْبُ كَانُوا أَجْبَنَ النَّاسِ، وَإِذَا كَانَ أَمْنٌ كَانُوا أَكْثَرَ النَّاسِ كَلَامًا، كَمَا قَالَ [الله] تعالى، عنهم في الآية الأخرى: ﴿فَإِذَا جَاءَ الْخَوْفُ رَأَيْتَهُمْ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَيْكَ تَدُورُ أَعْيُنُهُمْ كَالَّذِي يُغْشَى عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْمَوْتِ فَإِذَا ذَهَبَ الْخَوْفُ سَلَقُوكُمْ بِأَلْسِنَةٍ حِدَادٍ﴾ [الْأَحْزَابِ:١٩] أَيْ: عَلَتْ أَلْسِنَتُهُمْ بِالْكَلَامِ الْحَادِّ الْقَوِيِّ فِي الْأَمْنِ، وَفِي الْحَرْبِ أَجْبَنُ شَيْءٍ، وَكَمَا قَالَ الشَّاعِرُ 

أَفِي السِّلْمِ أَعْيَارًا جفَاءً وَغلْظَةً ... وَفي الحَرْب أشباهُ النّسَاءِ العَوارِكِ 

وَقَالَ تَعَالَى فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَيَقُولُ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَوْلا نزلَتْ سُورَةٌ فَإِذَا أُنزلَتْ سُورَةٌ مُحْكَمَةٌ وَذُكِرَ فِيهَا الْقِتَالُ رَأَيْتَ الَّذِينَ فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ مَرَضٌ يَنْظُرُونَ إِلَيْكَ نَظَرَ الْمَغْشِيِّ عَلَيْهِ مِنَ الْمَوْتِ فَأَوْلَى لَهُمْ طَاعَةٌ وَقَوْلٌ مَعْرُوفٌ فَإِذَا عَزَمَ الأمْرُ فَلَوْ صَدَقُوا اللَّهَ لَكَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُمْ [فَهَلْ عَسَيْتُمْ إِنْ تَوَلَّيْتُمْ أَنْ تُفْسِدُوا فِي الأرْضِ] [الْآيَةَ] [مُحَمَّدٍ:٢٠-٢٢] ﴾ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَطُبِعَ عَلَى قُلُوبِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: بِسَبَبِ نُكُولِهِمْ عَنِ الْجِهَادِ وَالْخُرُوجِ مَعَ الرَّسُولِ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، ﴿فَهُمْ لَا يَفْقَهُونَ﴾ أَيْ: لَا يَفْهَمُونَ مَا فِيهِ صَلَاحٌ لَهُمْ فَيَفْعَلُوهُ، وَلَا مَا فِيهِ مَضَرَّةٌ لَهُمْ فَيَجْتَنِبُوهُ.

---

## 9:88-89 — verses 88-89 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When the Exalted mentioned the censure of the hypocrites, He made clear the praise of the believers and what awaits them in their Hereafter, saying: {But the Messenger and those who believed with him strove} to the end of the two verses, describing their state and their final outcome.

His saying: {And those are the ones for whom are the good things} means: in the Abode of the Hereafter, in the Gardens of al-Firdaws and the lofty ranks.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى ذَمَّ الْمُنَافِقِينَ، بيَّن ثَنَاءَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَمَا لَهُمْ فِي آخِرَتِهِمْ، فَقَالَ: ﴿لَكِنِ الرَّسُولُ وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مَعَهُ جَاهَدُوا﴾ إِلَى آخِرِ الْآيَتَيْنِ مِنْ بَيَانِ حَالِهِمْ وَمَآلِهِمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَأُولَئِكَ لَهُمُ الْخَيْرَاتُ﴾ أَيْ: فِي الدَّارِ الْآخِرَةِ، فِي جَنَّاتِ الْفِرْدَوْسِ وَالدَّرَجَاتِ الْعُلَى.

---

## 9:90 — verse 90

### Translation

Then the Exalted made clear the condition of those with excuses for abandoning jihad, who came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ making their excuses to him, explaining to him the weakness and inability to go forth that they were in, and they were from among the Arab tribes dwelling around Medina.

Al-Dahhak said, on the authority of Ibn Abbas: that he used to recite it as "wa ja'a al-mu'dharun" with the light form (takhfif), and would say: they are the people of excuse (ahl al-'udhr).

Ibn 'Uyaynah likewise related the same from Humayd, from Mujahid.

Ibn Ishaq said: It has reached me that they were a group from Banu Ghifar, among them Khufaf ibn Ayma ibn Rahdah.

This view is the more apparent one regarding the meaning of the verse, because He says after this: {And those who lied to Allah and His Messenger sat back}, meaning: they did not come to make excuses at all.

Ibn Jurayj said, on the authority of Mujahid, regarding {And the mu'adhdhirun of the bedouins came}: he said, a group from Banu Ghifar came and made excuses, but Allah did not accept their excuse. Al-Hasan, Qatadah, and Muhammad ibn Ishaq said the same. But the first view is more apparent, and Allah knows best, because of what we have presented before, namely His saying after it: {And those who lied to Allah and His Messenger sat back}, meaning: others from among the bedouins remained behind from coming to make excuses. Then He threatened them with a painful punishment, saying: {A painful punishment will befall those among them who disbelieved}.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

ثُمَّ بَيَّن تَعَالَى حَالَ ذَوِي الْأَعْذَارِ فِي تَرْكِ الْجِهَادِ، الَّذِينَ جَاءُوا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَعْتَذِرُونَ إِلَيْهِ، وَيُبَيِّنُونَ لَهُ مَا هُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ الضَّعْفِ، وَعَدَمِ الْقُدْرَةِ عَلَى الْخُرُوجِ، وَهُمْ من أحياء العرب ممن حول المدينة.

قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: إِنَّهُ كَانَ يَقْرَأُ: "وَجَاءَ المُعْذَرُون" بِالتَّخْفِيفِ، وَيَقُولُ: هُمْ أَهْلُ الْعُذْرِ.

وَكَذَا رَوَى ابْنُ عُيَيْنَةَ، عَنْ حُمَيد، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ سَوَاءً.

قَالَ ابْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: وَبَلَغَنِي أَنَّهُمْ نَفَر مِنْ بَنِي غِفَارٍ مِنْهُمْ: خُفاف بْنُ إِيمَاءَ بْنِ رَحَضة.

وَهَذَا الْقَوْلُ هُوَ الْأَظْهَرُ فِي مَعْنَى الْآيَةِ؛ لِأَنَّهُ قَالَ بَعْدَ هَذَا: ﴿وَقَعَدَ الَّذِينَ كَذَبُوا اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ﴾ أَيْ: لَمْ يَأْتُوا فَيَعْتَذِرُوا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْج عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿وَجَاءَ الْمُعَذِّرُونَ مِنَ الأعْرَابِ﴾ قَالَ: نَفَرٌ مِنْ بَنِي غِفَارٍ، جَاءُوا فَاعْتَذَرُوا فَلَمْ يُعذرْهم اللَّهُ. وَكَذَا قَالَ الْحَسَنُ، وَقَتَادَةُ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، وَالْقَوْلُ الْأَوَّلُ أَظْهَرُ واللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ، لِمَا قَدَّمْنَا مِنْ قَوْلِهِ بَعْدَهُ: ﴿وَقَعَدَ الَّذِينَ كَذَبُوا اللَّهَ وَرَسُولَهُ﴾ أَيْ: وَقَعَدَ آخَرُونَ مِنَ الْأَعْرَابِ عَنِ الْمَجِيءِ لِلِاعْتِذَارِ، ثُمَّ أَوْعَدَهُمْ بِالْعَذَابِ الْأَلِيمِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿سَيُصِيبُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ﴾

---

## 9:91-93 — verses 91-93 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Then the Almighty made clear the excuses which entail no blame upon whoever remains behind from fighting on account of them. He mentioned among these what is inherent in the person and cannot be separated from him, namely weakness in bodily constitution which makes it impossible for him to engage in the struggle of jihad, and among this is blindness, lameness, and the like. For this reason He began with it. Then there is what occurs incidentally due to an illness that afflicts his body, preoccupying him from going out in the way of Allah, or due to his poverty, being unable to equip himself for war. So there is no blame upon these people if they remain behind and give sincere counsel in their state of remaining behind, and do not spread alarm among the people, nor discourage them, while being good in this state of theirs. For this reason He said: {There is no blame upon those who do good, and Allah is Forgiving, Merciful.}

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from Abd al-Aziz ibn Rufay', from Abu Thumamah, may Allah be pleased with him, who said: The disciples said, "O Spirit of Allah, tell us about the one who gives sincere counsel to Allah." He said: "The one who gives preference to the right of Allah over the right of the people, and when two matters occur to him, or when the matter of this world and the matter of the hereafter both present themselves to him, he begins with that which pertains to the hereafter, then turns to that which pertains to this world."

Al-Awza'i said: The people went out to pray for rain, and Bilal ibn Sa'd stood among them, praised Allah and extolled Him, then said: "O assembly of those present, do you not acknowledge your wrongdoing?" They said, "By Allah, yes." He said: "O Allah, we hear You saying: {There is no blame upon those who do good.} O Allah, we have acknowledged our wrongdoing, so forgive us, have mercy upon us, and give us rain." He raised his hands and they raised their hands, and they were given rain.

Qatadah said: This verse was revealed concerning A'idh ibn Amr al-Muzani.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] ... Zayd ibn Thabit said: "I used to write for the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and I was writing 'Bara'ah' (the surah of disavowal). While I had just placed the pen behind my ear, we were commanded to fight. The Messenger of Allah ﷺ began looking at what was being revealed to him, when a blind man came and said, 'What is to become of me, O Messenger of Allah, seeing that I am blind?' Then Allah revealed {There is no blame upon the weak, nor upon the sick...}" the verse.

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas concerning this verse: This was because the Messenger of Allah ﷺ commanded the people to set out with him for battle. A group of his companions came to him, among them Abdullah ibn Mughaffal al-Muzani, and they said, "O Messenger of Allah, provide us with mounts." He said to them, "By Allah, I find nothing to mount you on." So they turned away weeping, grieved that they should have to sit out from jihad, finding neither provision nor mount. When Allah saw their eagerness in their love for Him and for His Messenger, He revealed their excuse in His Book, saying: {There is no blame upon the weak, nor upon the sick, nor upon those who find nothing to spend} up to His saying: {so they do not know.}

Mujahid said concerning His statement: {Nor upon those who, when they come to you that you may mount them...} It was revealed concerning the Banu Muqarrin of Muzaynah.

Muhammad ibn Ka'b said: They were seven men: from Banu Amr ibn Awf, Salim ibn Umayr; from Banu Waqif, Harami ibn Amr; from Banu Mazin ibn al-Najjar, Abd al-Rahman ibn Ka'b, known as Abu Layla; from Banu al-Mu'alla, [Salman ibn Sakhr; and from Banu Haritha, Abd al-Rahman ibn Yazid, Abu Ablah, who is the one who gave his honor in charity and Allah accepted it from him]; and from Banu Salimah, Amr ibn Anamah and Abdullah ibn Amr al-Muzani.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, in the account of the expedition of Tabuk: Then some men among the Muslims came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and they were the weepers, seven men from the Ansar and others: from Banu Amr ibn Awf, Salim ibn Umayr and Ulbah ibn Zayd, brother of Banu Haritha; and Abu Layla Abd al-Rahman ibn Ka'b, brother of Banu Mazin ibn al-Najjar; and Amr ibn al-Humam ibn al-Jamuh, brother of Banu Salimah; and Abdullah ibn al-Mughaffal al-Muzani, though some say rather it was Abdullah ibn Amr al-Muzani; and Harami ibn Abdullah, brother of Banu Waqif; and Irbad ibn Sariyah al-Fazari. They asked the Messenger of Allah ﷺ to provide them mounts, being people in need, and he said, "I find nothing to mount you on." So they turned away with their eyes overflowing with tears, grieving that they could find nothing to spend.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] ... al-Hasan said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "You have indeed left behind you in Madinah people such that whatever expenditure you spend, and whatever valley you cross, and whatever gain you attain from an enemy, they share with you in the reward." Then he recited: {Nor upon those who, when they come to you that you may mount them, you say, 'I find nothing to mount you on'...} the verse.

The origin of this hadith is in the two Sahihs, from the hadith that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "There are indeed people in Madinah such that you do not cross a valley nor travel any journey but that they are with you." They said, "While they are in Madinah?" He said, "Yes, an excuse has held them back."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] ... Jabir said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "You have indeed left behind you in Madinah men such that you do not cross a valley nor travel any path but that they share with you in the reward; illness has held them back."

Muslim and Ibn Majah also transmitted it through various routes, from al-A'mash, with the same content.

Then the Almighty turned back blame upon those who ask permission to remain behind while they are wealthy, and He rebuked them for being content to be with the women who stay behind with the households, saying: {And Allah has sealed their hearts, so they do not know.}

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

ثُمَّ بَيَّنَ تَعَالَى الْأَعْذَارَ الَّتِي لَا حَرَج عَلَى مَنْ قَعَدَ فِيهَا عَنِ الْقِتَالِ، فَذَكَرَ مِنْهَا مَا هُوَ لَازِمٌ لِلشَّخْصِ لَا يَنْفَكُّ عَنْهُ، وَهُوَ الضَّعْفُ فِي التَّرْكِيبِ الَّذِي لَا يَسْتَطِيعُ مَعَهُ الْجِلَادَ فِي الْجِهَادِ، وَمِنْهُ الْعَمَى والعَرَج وَنَحْوُهُمَا، وَلِهَذَا بَدَأَ بِهِ. مَا هُوَ عَارِضٌ بِسَبَبِ مَرَضٍ عَنَّ لَهُ فِي بَدَنِهِ، شَغَلَهُ عَنِ الْخُرُوجِ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ، أَوْ بِسَبَبِ فَقْرِهِ لَا يَقْدِرُ عَلَى التَّجَهُّزِ لِلْحَرْبِ، فَلَيْسَ عَلَى هَؤُلَاءِ حَرَج إِذَا قَعَدُوا وَنَصَحُوا فِي حَالِ قُعُودِهِمْ، وَلَمْ يُرْجِفُوا بِالنَّاسِ، وَلَمْ يُثَبِّطوهم، وَهُمْ مُحْسِنُونَ فِي حَالِهِمْ هَذَا؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿مَا عَلَى الْمُحْسِنِينَ مِنْ سَبِيلٍ وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ بْنِ رُفَيْعٍ، عَنْ أَبِي ثُمَامَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قَالَ الْحَوَارِيُّونَ: يَا رُوحَ اللَّهِ، أَخْبِرْنَا عَنِ النَّاصِحِ لِلَّهِ؟ قَالَ: الَّذِي يُؤثِر حَقَّ اللَّهِ عَلَى حَقِّ النَّاسِ، وَإِذَا حَدَثَ لَهُ أَمْرَانِ -أَوْ: بَدَا لَهُ أَمْرُ الدُّنْيَا وَأَمْرُ الْآخِرَةِ -بَدَأَ بِالَّذِي لِلْآخِرَةِ ثُمَّ تَفَرَّغَ لِلَّذِي للدنيا.

وَقَالَ الْأَوْزَاعِيُّ: خَرَجَ النَّاسُ إِلَى الِاسْتِسْقَاءِ، فَقَامَ فِيهِمْ بِلَالُ بْنُ سَعْدٍ، فَحَمِدَ اللَّهَ وَأَثْنَى عَلَيْهِ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: يَا مَعْشَرَ مَنْ حَضَرَ: أَلَسْتُمْ مُقِرِّينَ بِالْإِسَاءَةِ؟ قَالُوا: اللَّهُمَّ نَعَمْ. فَقَالَ: اللَّهُمَّ، إِنَّا نَسْمَعُكَ تَقُولُ: ﴿مَا عَلَى الْمُحْسِنِينَ مِنْ سَبِيلٍ﴾ اللَّهُمَّ، وَقَدْ أَقْرَرْنَا بِالْإِسَاءَةِ فَاغْفِرْ لَنَا وَارْحَمْنَا واسقِنا. وَرَفَعَ يَدَيْهِ وَرَفَعُوا أَيْدِيَهُمْ فَسُقوا.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: نَزَلَتْ هَذِهِ الْآيَةُ فِي عَائِذِ بْنِ عَمْرٍو الْمُزَنِيِّ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا هِشَامُ بْنُ عُبَيْدِ اللَّهِ الرَّازِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ جَابِرٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ فَرْوَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ أَبِي لَيْلَى، عَنْ زَيْدِ بْنِ ثَابِتٍ قَالَ: كُنْتُ أكتبُ لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَكُنْتُ أَكْتُبُ "بَرَاءَةَ" فَإِنِّي لواضعُ الْقَلَمَ عَلَى أُذُنِي إِذْ أمرْنا بِالْقِتَالِ، فَجَعَلَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَنْظُرُ مَا يَنْزِلُ عَلَيْهِ، إذا جَاءَ أَعْمَى فَقَالَ: كَيْفَ بِي يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ وَأَنَا أَعْمَى؟ فَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ ﴿لَيْسَ عَلَى الضُّعَفَاءِ وَلا عَلَى الْمَرْضَى﴾ الْآيَةَ 

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ: وَذَلِكَ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم أمرَ النَّاسَ أَنْ يَنْبَعِثُوا غَازِينَ مَعَهُ، فَجَاءَتْهُ عِصَابَةٌ مِنْ أَصْحَابِهِ، فِيهِمْ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ مُغَفَّل الْمُزَنِيُّ فَقَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، احْمِلْنَا. فَقَالَ لَهُمْ: "وَاللَّهِ لَا أَجِدُ مَا أَحْمِلُكُمْ عَلَيْهِ". فَتَوَلَّوْا وَلَهُمْ بُكَاءٌ، وعزَّ عَلَيْهِمْ أَنْ يَجْلِسُوا عَنِ الْجِهَادِ، وَلَا يَجِدُونَ نَفَقَةً وَلَا مَحْمَلًا. فَلَمَّا رَأَى اللَّهُ حرْصَهم عَلَى مَحَبَّتِهِ وَمَحَبَّةِ رَسُولِهِ أَنْزَلَ عُذْرَهُمْ فِي كِتَابِهِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿لَيْسَ عَلَى الضُّعَفَاءِ وَلا عَلَى الْمَرْضَى وَلا عَلَى الَّذِينَ لَا يَجِدُونَ مَا يُنْفِقُونَ حَرَجٌ﴾ إِلَى قَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَهُمْ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ﴾ .

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلا عَلَى الَّذِينَ إِذَا مَا أَتَوْكَ لِتَحْمِلَهُمْ﴾ نَزَلَتْ فِي بَنِي مُقَرِّنٍ مِنْ مُزَيْنَةَ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ: كَانُوا سَبْعَةَ نَفَرٍ، مِنْ بَنِي عَمْرِو بْنِ عَوْفٍ: سَالِمُ بْنُ عُمَيْر -وَمِنْ بَنِي وَاقِفٍ: هَرَمي بْنُ عَمْرٍو -وَمِنْ بَنِي مَازِنِ بْنِ النَّجَّارِ: عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ كَعْبٍ، وَيُكَنَّى أَبَا لَيْلَى -وَمِنْ بَنِي المُعَلى: [سَلْمَانُ بْنُ صَخْرٍ -وَمِنْ بَنِي حَارِثَةَ: عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ يَزِيدَ، أَبُو عَبْلَةَ، وَهُوَ الَّذِي تَصَدَّقَ بِعِرْضِهِ فَقَبِلَهُ اللَّهُ مِنْهُ] وَمِنْ بَنِي سَلِمة: عَمْرُو بْنُ عَنَمة وَعَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عَمْرٍو الْمُزَنِيُّ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ فِي سِيَاقِ غَزْوَةِ تَبُوكَ: ثُمَّ إِنَّ رِجَالًا مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ أَتَوْا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَهُمُ الْبَكَّاءُونَ، وَهُمْ سَبْعَةُ نَفَرٍ مِنَ الْأَنْصَارِ وَغَيْرِهِمْ، مِنْ بَنِي عَمْرِو بْنِ عَوْفٍ: سَالِمُ بْنُ عُمَير وَعُلْبَةُ بْنُ زَيْدٍ أَخُو بَنِي حَارِثَةَ، وَأَبُو لَيْلَى عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ كَعْبٍ، أَخُو بَنِي مَازِنِ بْنِ النَّجَّارِ، وَعَمْرُو بْنُ الْحُمَامِ بْنِ الْجَمُوحِ، أَخُو بَنِي سَلِمة، وَعَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ المُغَفَّل الْمُزَنِيُّ؛ وَبَعْضُ النَّاسِ يَقُولُ: بَلْ هُوَ عَبْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عَمْرٍو الْمُزَنِيُّ، وهَرَميّ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، أَخُو بَنِي وَاقِفٍ، وعِرْباض بْنُ سَارِيَةَ الْفَزَارِيُّ، فَاسْتَحْمَلُوا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ، وَكَانُوا أَهْلَ حَاجَةٍ، فَقَالَ: لَا أَجِدُ مَا أَحْمِلُكُمْ عَلَيْهِ فَتَوَلَّوْا وَأَعْيُنُهُمْ تَفِيضُ مِنَ الدَّمْعِ حَزَنًا أَلَّا يَجِدُوا مَا يُنْفِقُونَ 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ الْأَوْدِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا وَكيع، عَنِ الرَّبِيعِ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَقَدْ خَلَّفْتُمْ بِالْمَدِينَةِ أَقْوَامًا، مَا أَنْفَقْتُمْ مِنْ نَفَقَةٍ، وَلَا قَطَعْتُمْ وَادِيًا، وَلَا نِلْتُمْ مِنْ عَدُوٍّ نَيْلًا إِلَّا وَقَدْ شَركوكم فِي الْأَجْرِ"، ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿وَلا عَلَى الَّذِينَ إِذَا مَا أَتَوْكَ لِتَحْمِلَهُمْ قُلْتَ لَا أَجِدُ مَا أَحْمِلُكُمْ عَلَيْهِ﴾ الْآيَةَ.

وَأَصْلُ هَذَا الْحَدِيثِ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ بِالْمَدِينَةِ أَقْوَامًا مَا قَطَعْتُمْ وَادِيًا، وَلَا سِرْتُمْ [مَسِيرًا] إِلَّا وَهُمْ مَعَكُمْ". قَالُوا: وَهُمْ بِالْمَدِينَةِ؟ قَالَ: "نَعَمْ، حَبَسَهُمُ الْعُذْرُ" 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ أَبِي سُفْيَانَ، عَنْ جَابِرٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَقَدْ خَلَّفْتُمْ بِالْمَدِينَةِ رِجَالًا مَا قَطَعْتُمْ وَادِيًا، وَلَا سَلَكْتُمْ طَرِيقًا إِلَّا شَركوكم فِي الْأَجْرِ، حَبَسَهُمُ الْمَرَضُ".

وَرَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، بِهِ 

ثُمَّ رَدَّ تَعَالَى الْمَلَامَةَ عَلَى الَّذِينَ يَسْتَأْذِنُونَ فِي الْقُعُودِ وَهُمْ أَغْنِيَاءُ، وأنَّبَهم فِي رِضَاهُمْ بِأَنْ يَكُونُوا مَعَ النِّسَاءِ الْخَوَالِفِ فِي الرِّحَالِ، ﴿وَطَبَعَ اللَّهُ عَلَى قُلُوبِهِمْ فَهُمْ لَا يَعْلَمُونَ﴾ .

---

## 9:94-96 — verses 94-96 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah, the Exalted, informs about the hypocrites that when they return to Madinah they will offer excuses to the believers, {Say: "Do not make excuses, we will never believe you"}, meaning: we will never take you as truthful, {Allah has already informed us of your affairs}, meaning: Allah has already made known to us your conditions, {and Allah and His Messenger will see your deeds}, meaning: your deeds will be made manifest to the people in this world, {then you will be returned to the Knower of the unseen and the witnessed, and He will inform you of what you used to do}, meaning: He will tell you of your deeds, the good of them and the evil of them, and He will requite you for them.

Then He informs about them that they will swear, making excuses, so that you may turn away from them and not rebuke them, {so turn away from them}, out of contempt for them, {indeed they are filth (rijs)}, meaning: wicked, their inner selves and their beliefs are impure, {and their abode}, in their Hereafter, {is Hell}, {as recompense for what they used to earn}, meaning: of sins and wrongdoings.

And He informs that even if you were to be pleased with them because of their swearing to you, {then indeed Allah is not pleased with the disobedient people (al-qawm al-fasiqin)}, meaning: those who go out from obedience to Him and obedience to His Messenger. For fisq (transgression) is a going out, and from this the mouse is named "fuwaysiqah" (little transgressor) because it goes out from its hole to cause corruption. And it is said, "the fresh date went out from its husks (fasaqat al-rutabah)," when it comes out from its coverings.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى عَنِ الْمُنَافِقِينَ بِأَنَّهُمْ إِذَا رَجَعُوا إِلَى الْمَدِينَةِ أَنَّهُمْ يَعْتَذِرُونَ إِلَيْهِمْ، ﴿قُلْ لَا تَعْتَذِرُوا لَنْ نُؤْمِنَ لَكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: لَنْ نُصَدِّقَكُمْ، ﴿قَدْ نَبَّأَنَا اللَّهُ مِنْ أَخْبَارِكُمْ﴾ أَيْ: قَدْ أَعْلَمَنَا اللَّهُ أَحْوَالَكُمْ، ﴿وَسَيَرَى اللَّهُ عَمَلَكُمْ وَرَسُولُهُ﴾ أَيْ: سَيُظْهِرُ أَعْمَالَكُمْ لِلنَّاسِ فِي الدُّنْيَا، ﴿ثُمَّ تُرَدُّونَ إِلَى عَالِمِ الْغَيْبِ وَالشَّهَادَةِ فَيُنَبِّئُكُمْ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَعْمَلُونَ﴾ أَيْ: فَيُخْبِرُكُمْ بِأَعْمَالِكُمْ، خَيْرِهَا وَشَرِّهَا، وَيُجْزِيكُمْ عَلَيْهَا.

ثُمَّ أَخْبَرَ عَنْهُمْ أَنَّهُمْ سَيَحْلِفُونَ مُعْتَذِرِينَ لِتُعْرِضُوا عَنْهُمْ فَلَا تُؤَنِّبُوهم، ﴿فَأَعْرِضُوا عَنْهُمْ﴾ احْتِقَارًا لَهُمْ، ﴿إِنَّهُمْ رِجْسٌ﴾ أَيْ: خُبثاء نَجِسٌ بَوَاطِنُهُمْ وَاعْتِقَادَاتُهُمْ، ﴿وَمَأْوَاهُمْ﴾ فِي آخِرَتِهِمْ ﴿جَهَنَّمُ﴾ ﴿جَزَاءً بِمَا كَانُوا يَكْسِبُونَ﴾ أَيْ: مِنَ الْآثَامِ وَالْخَطَايَا.

وَأَخْبَرَ أَنَّهُمْ وَإِنْ رَضُوا عَنْهُمْ بِحَلِفِهِمْ لَهُمْ، ﴿فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَرْضَى عَنِ الْقَوْمِ الْفَاسِقِينَ﴾ أَيِ: الْخَارِجِينَ عَنْ طَاعَتِهِ وَطَاعَةِ رَسُولِهِ، فَإِنَّ الْفِسْقَ هُوَ الْخُرُوجُ، وَمِنْهُ سُمِّيَتِ الْفَأْرَةُ "فُوَيسقة" لِخُرُوجِهَا مِنْ جُحرها لِلْإِفْسَادِ، وَيُقَالُ: "فَسَقَتِ الرُّطَبَةُ": إِذَا خَرَجَتْ مِنْ أَكْمَامِهَا

---

## 9:97-99 — verses 97-99 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah, may He be exalted, informs that among the Bedouins are disbelievers, hypocrites, and believers, and that their disbelief and hypocrisy are greater and more severe than that of others, and more likely, meaning more apt, not to know the limits of what Allah has sent down upon His Messenger. As al-A'mash reported from Ibrahim, who said: a Bedouin sat down beside Zayd ibn Sawhan while he was speaking to his companions, and his hand had been struck on the day of Nahawand. The Bedouin said: "By Allah, your speech pleases me, but your hand makes me suspicious." Zayd said: "What makes you suspicious about my hand? It is the left one." The Bedouin said: "By Allah, I do not know whether they cut off the right or the left." Zayd ibn Sawhan then said: "Allah has spoken the truth: {The Bedouins are more severe in disbelief and hypocrisy, and more likely not to know the limits of what Allah has sent down upon His Messenger}."

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] from Ibn Abbas, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "Whoever dwells in the desert becomes coarse, whoever follows the hunt becomes heedless, and whoever comes to the ruler is put to trial."

Abu Dawud, al-Tirmidhi, and al-Nasa'i also transmitted it through various chains from Sufyan al-Thawri, with the same content. Al-Tirmidhi said: hasan gharib (sound but singularly transmitted), we know it only from the hadith of al-Thawri.

Since coarseness and roughness were characteristic of the people of the desert, Allah did not send any messenger from among them; rather, the sending of messengers was from the people of the towns, as Allah, may He be exalted, said: {And We did not send before you except men to whom We revealed, from among the people of the towns} [Yusuf: 109]. And when that Bedouin gave that gift to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, he returned to him many times its worth until he was satisfied, and he said: "I had resolved not to accept a gift except from a Qurashi, a Thaqafi, an Ansari, or a Dawsi," because these were people who dwelt in cities: Mecca, al-Ta'if, Medina, and Yemen, and so they were gentler in character than the Bedouins, on account of the coarseness present in the natural disposition of the Bedouins.

The hadith of [the Bedouin] concerning kissing children: Muslim said: [chain] from Aisha, who said: some people from among the Bedouins came to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ and said: "Do you kiss your children?" They said: "Yes." They said: "But we, by Allah, do not kiss them." The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "And what can I do if Allah has removed mercy from you?" Ibn Numayr's version has: "from your heart, mercy."

His saying, {And Allah is All-Knowing, All-Wise}, means: All-Knowing of who deserves to be taught faith and knowledge, All-Wise in what He has apportioned among His servants of knowledge and ignorance, faith, disbelief, and hypocrisy. He is not questioned about what He does, on account of His knowledge and His wisdom.

Allah, may He be exalted, informs that among them is {one who takes what he spends} meaning in the way of Allah, {as a loss}, meaning a fine and a deprivation, {and awaits for you the turns of misfortune}, meaning he waits for calamities and afflictions to befall you. {Upon them is the evil turn}, meaning it is turned back upon them, and the evil circles around them. {And Allah is All-Hearing, All-Knowing}, meaning He hears the supplication of His servants, and knows who deserves support as opposed to who deserves abandonment.

His saying, {And among the Bedouins is he who believes in Allah and the Last Day and takes what he spends as means of nearness to Allah and the prayers of the Messenger}: this is the praiseworthy portion of the Bedouins, those who take what they spend in the way of Allah as a means of nearness by which they draw close to Allah, and who seek thereby the Messenger's supplication for them. {Verily, it is indeed a means of nearness for them}, meaning: truly that is achieved for them. {Allah will admit them into His mercy. Indeed, Allah is Forgiving, Merciful.}

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

أَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّ فِي الْأَعْرَابِ كُفَّارًا وَمُنَافِقِينَ وَمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَأَنَّ كُفْرَهُمْ وَنِفَاقَهُمْ أَعْظَمُ مِنْ غَيْرِهِمْ وَأَشَدُّ، وَأَجْدَرُ، أَيْ: أَحْرَى أَلَّا يَعْلَمُوا حُدُودَ مَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى رَسُولِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ قَالَ: جَلَسَ أَعْرَابِيٌّ إِلَى زَيْدِ بْنِ صَوْحان وَهُوَ يُحَدِّثُ أَصْحَابَهُ، وَكَانَتْ يَدُهُ قَدْ أُصِيبَتْ يَوْمَ نهاوَند، فَقَالَ الْأَعْرَابِيُّ: وَاللَّهِ إِنَّ حَدِيثَكَ لَيُعْجِبُنِي، وَإِنَّ يَدَكَ لَتُرِيبُنِي فَقَالَ زَيْدٌ: مَا يُريبك مِنْ يَدِي؟ إِنَّهَا الشِّمَالُ. فَقَالَ الْأَعْرَابِيُّ: وَاللَّهِ مَا أَدْرِي، الْيَمِينَ يَقْطَعُونَ أَوِ الشمالَ؟ فَقَالَ زَيْدُ بْنُ صُوحَانَ صَدَقَ اللَّهُ: ﴿الأعْرَابُ أَشَدُّ كُفْرًا وَنِفَاقًا وَأَجْدَرُ أَلا يَعْلَمُوا حُدُودَ مَا أَنزلَ اللَّهُ عَلَى رَسُولِهِ﴾

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ مَهْدِي، حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ أَبِي مُوسَى، عن وهب بْنِ مُنَبِّه، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَنْ سَكَنَ الْبَادِيَةَ جَفَا، وَمَنِ اتَّبَعَ الصَّيْدَ غَفَل، وَمَنْ أَتَى السُّلْطَانَ افْتُتِنَ".

وَرَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالتِّرْمِذِيُّ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ مِنْ طُرُقٍ، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ الثَّوْرِيِّ، بِهِ وَقَالَ التِّرْمِذِيُّ: حَسَنٌ غَرِيبٌ، لَا نَعْرِفُهُ إِلَّا مِنْ حَدِيثِ الثَّوْرِيِّ.

وَلَمَّا كَانَتِ الْغِلْظَةُ وَالْجَفَاءُ فِي أَهْلِ الْبَوَادِي لَمْ يَبْعَثِ اللَّهُ مِنْهُمْ رَسُولًا وَإِنَّمَا كَانَتِ الْبَعْثَةُ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْقُرَى، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ قَبْلِكَ إِلا رِجَالا نُوحِي إِلَيْهِمْ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْقُرَى﴾ [يُوسُفَ:١٠٩] وَلَمَّا أَهْدَى ذَلِكَ الْأَعْرَابِيُّ تِلْكَ الْهَدِيَّةَ لِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فردَّ عَلَيْهِ أَضْعَافَهَا حَتَّى رَضِيَ، قَالَ: "لَقَدْ هَمَمْتُ أَلَّا أَقْبَلَ هَدِيَّةً إِلَّا مِنْ قُرشي، أَوْ ثَقَفي أَوْ أَنْصَارِيٍّ، أَوْ دَوْسِيّ" ؛ لِأَنَّ هَؤُلَاءِ كَانُوا يَسْكُنُونَ الْمُدُنَ: مَكَّةَ، وَالطَّائِفَ، وَالْمَدِينَةَ، وَالْيَمَنَ، فَهُمْ أَلْطَفُ أَخْلَاقًا مِنَ الْأَعْرَابِ: لِمَا فِي طِبَاعِ الْأَعْرَابِ مِنَ الْجَفَاءِ.

حَدِيثُ [الْأَعْرَابِيِّ] فِي تَقْبِيلِ الْوَلَدِ: قَالَ مُسْلِمٌ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو بَكْرِ بْنُ أَبِي شَيْبَةَ وَأَبُو كُرَيْب قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو أُسَامَةَ وَابْنُ نُمَيْر، عَنْ هِشَامٍ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَائِشَةَ قَالَتْ: قَدِمَ نَاسٌ مِنَ الْأَعْرَابِ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ فَقَالُوا: أتقبِّلون صِبْيَانَكُمْ؟ قَالُوا: نَعَمْ. قَالُوا: وَلَكِنَّا وَاللَّهِ مَا نقبِّل. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "وَأمْلكُ أَنْ كَانَ اللَّهُ نَزَعَ مِنْكُمُ الرَّحْمَةَ؟ ". وَقَالَ ابْنُ نُمَيْرٍ: "مِنْ قَلْبِكَ الرَّحْمَةَ" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاللَّهُ عَلِيمٌ حَكِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: عَلِيمٌ بِمَنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ أَنْ يُعَلِّمَهُ الْإِيمَانَ وَالْعِلْمَ، ﴿حَكِيمٌ﴾ فِيمَا قَسَّمَ بَيْنَ عِبَادِهِ مِنَ الْعِلْمِ وَالْجَهْلِ وَالْإِيمَانِ وَالْكُفْرِ وَالنِّفَاقِ، لَا يُسْأَلُ عَمَّا يَفْعَلُ، لِعَلْمِهِ وَحِكْمَتِهِ.

وَأَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّ مِنْهُمْ ﴿مَنْ يَتَّخِذُ مَا يُنْفِقُ﴾ أَيْ: فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ ﴿مَغْرَمًا﴾ أَيْ: غَرَامَةً وَخَسَارَةً، ﴿وَيَتَرَبَّصُ بِكُمُ الدَّوَائِرَ﴾ أَيْ: يَنْتَظِرُ بِكُمُ الْحَوَادِثَ وَالْآفَاتِ، ﴿عَلَيْهِمْ دَائِرَةُ السَّوْءِ﴾ أَيْ: هِيَ مُنْعَكِسَةٌ عَلَيْهِمْ وَالسَّوْءُ دَائِرٌ عَلَيْهِمْ، ﴿وَاللَّهُ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: سَمِيعٌ لِدُعَاءِ عِبَادِهِ، عَلِيمٌ بِمَنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ النَّصْرَ مِمَّنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ الْخُذْلَانَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمِنَ الأعْرَابِ مَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الآخِرِ وَيَتَّخِذُ مَا يُنْفِقُ قُرُبَاتٍ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ وَصَلَوَاتِ الرَّسُولِ﴾ هَذَا هُوَ الْقِسْمُ الْمَمْدُوحُ مِنَ الْأَعْرَابِ، وَهُمُ الَّذِينَ يَتَّخِذُونَ مَا يُنْفِقُونَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ قُرْبَةً يَتَقَرَّبُونَ بِهَا عِنْدَ اللَّهِ، وَيَبْتَغُونَ بِذَلِكَ دُعَاءَ الرَّسُولِ لَهُمْ، ﴿أَلا إِنَّهَا قُرْبَةٌ لَهُمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَلَا إِنَّ ذَلِكَ حَاصِلٌ لَهُمْ، ﴿سَيُدْخِلُهُمُ اللَّهُ فِي رَحْمَتِهِ إِنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ﴾

---

## 9:100 — verse 100

### Translation

The Almighty informs of His approval of the foremost of the Emigrants (Muhajirun) and the Helpers (Ansar) and those who followed them in excellence, and of their approval of Him because of what He has prepared for them of gardens of bliss and everlasting delight.

Al-Sha'bi said: the foremost first ones among the Emigrants and Helpers are those who witnessed the Pledge of Ridwan (divine approval) in the year of al-Hudaybiyah.

Abu Musa al-Ash'ari, Sa'id ibn al-Musayyab, Muhammad ibn Sirin, al-Hasan, and Qatadah said: they are those who prayed toward the two qiblahs with the Messenger of Allah ﷺ.

Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi said: Umar ibn al-Khattab passed by a man reciting {And the foremost, the first of the Emigrants and the Helpers}. Umar took him by the hand and said: "Who taught you to recite this?" He said: "Ubayy ibn Ka'b." Umar said: "Do not leave me until I take you to him." When he came to him, Umar said: "Did you teach him to recite this verse this way?" He said: "Yes." Umar said: "And did you hear it from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ?" He said: "Yes. I used to think that we had been raised to a rank that no one after us would reach." Then Ubayy said: "The confirmation of this verse is at the beginning of Surat al-Jumu'ah: {And others among them who have not yet joined them, and He is the Mighty, the Wise} [al-Jumu'ah: 3], and in Surat al-Hashr: {And those who came after them saying, Our Lord, forgive us and our brothers who preceded us in faith} [al-Hashr: 10], and in al-Anfal: {And those who believed afterward and emigrated and struggled alongside you, they are of you} [al-Anfal: 75] to the end of the verse." Narrated by Ibn Jarir.

He said: it was mentioned regarding al-Hasan al-Basri that he used to recite it with "al-Ansar" in the nominative case, as a conjunction on {And the foremost, the first ones}.

So Allah, the Mighty, has informed that He has indeed approved of the foremost first ones among the Emigrants and the Helpers and those who followed them in excellence. So woe to whoever hates them or curses them, or hates or curses any one of them, especially the master of the Companions after the Messenger and the best and most excellent of them, I mean the greatest of the truthful (al-Siddiq al-Akbar) and the greatest caliph, Abu Bakr ibn Abi Quhafah, may Allah be pleased with him. For the abandoned faction of the Rafidah shows enmity toward the best of the Companions, hating them and cursing them. We seek refuge in Allah from that. This indicates that their minds are inverted and their hearts are turned upside down. Where do these people stand in relation to faith in the Qur'an, when they curse those with whom Allah is pleased? As for the people of the Sunnah, they seek Allah's approval upon those with whom Allah is pleased, and they curse those whom Allah and His Messenger have cursed, and they show loyalty to whoever shows loyalty to Allah, and they show enmity to whoever shows enmity to Allah. They are followers, not innovators, and they follow, they do not originate. For this reason they are the party of Allah, the successful ones, and His believing servants.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنْ رِضَاهُ عَنِ السَّابِقَيْنِ مِنَ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ وَالْأَنْصَارِ وَالتَّابِعِينَ لَهُمْ بِإِحْسَانٍ، وَرِضَاهُمْ عَنْهُ بِمَا أعدَّ لَهُمْ مِنْ جَنَّاتِ النَّعِيمِ، وَالنَّعِيمِ الْمُقِيمِ.

قَالَ الشَّعْبِيُّ: السَّابِقُونَ الْأَوَّلُونَ مِنَ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ وَالْأَنْصَارِ مَنْ أَدْرَكَ بَيْعَةَ الرِّضْوَانِ عَامَ الْحُدَيْبِيَةِ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو مُوسَى الْأَشْعَرِيُّ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ الْمُسَيَّبِ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ سِيرِينَ، وَالْحَسَنُ، وَقَتَادَةُ: هُمُ الَّذِينَ صَلَّوْا إِلَى الْقِبْلَتَيْنِ مَعَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ الْقُرَظِيُّ: مرَّ عُمَرُ بْنُ الْخَطَّابِ بِرَجُلٍ يَقْرَأُ: ﴿وَالسَّابِقُونَ الأوَّلُونَ مِنَ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ وَالأنْصَارِ﴾ فَأَخَذَ عُمَرُ بِيَدِهِ فَقَالَ: مَنْ أَقْرَأَكَ هَذَا؟ فَقَالَ: أبيُّ بْنُ كَعْبٍ. فَقَالَ: لَا تُفَارِقْنِي حَتَّى أَذْهَبَ بِكَ إِلَيْهِ. فَلَمَّا جَاءَهُ قَالَ عُمَرُ: أَنْتَ أَقْرَأْتَ هَذَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ هَكَذَا؟ قَالَ: نَعَمْ. قَالَ: وسمعتَها مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ؟ قال: نَعَمْ. لَقَدْ كُنْتُ أَرَى أَنَّا رَفَعَنَا رَفْعَةً لَا يَبْلُغُهَا أَحَدٌ بَعْدَنَا، فَقَالَ أبيُّ: تَصْدِيقُ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ فِي أَوَّلِ سُورَةِ الْجُمُعَةِ: ﴿وَآخَرِينَ مِنْهُمْ لَمَّا يَلْحَقُوا بِهِمْ وَهُوَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ﴾ [الْجُمُعَةِ:٣] وَفِي سُورَةِ الْحَشْرِ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ جَاءُوا مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ يَقُولُونَ رَبَّنَا اغْفِرْ لَنَا وَلإخْوَانِنَا الَّذِينَ سَبَقُونَا بِالإيمَانِ﴾ [الْحَشْرِ:١٠] وَفِي الْأَنْفَالِ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا مِنْ بَعْدُ وَهَاجَرُوا وَجَاهَدُوا مَعَكُمْ فَأُولَئِكَ مِنْكُمْ﴾ [الْأَنْفَالِ:٧٥] إِلَى آخِرِ الْآيَةِ، رَوَاهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ 

قَالَ: وَذُكِرَ عَنِ الْحَسَنِ الْبَصْرِيِّ أَنَّهُ كَانَ يَقْرَؤُهَا بِرَفْعِ "الْأَنْصَارِ" عَطْفًا عَلَى ﴿وَالسَّابِقُونَ الأوَّلُونَ﴾

فَقَدْ أَخْبَرَ اللَّهُ الْعَظِيمُ أَنَّهُ قَدْ رَضِيَ عَنِ السَّابِقِينَ الْأَوَّلِينَ مِنَ الْمُهَاجِرِينَ وَالْأَنْصَارِ وَالَّذِينَ اتَّبَعُوهُمْ بِإِحْسَانٍ: فَيَا وَيْلُ مَنْ أَبْغَضَهُمْ أَوْ سَبَّهم أَوْ أَبْغَضَ أَوْ سبَّ بَعْضَهُمْ، وَلَا سِيَّمَا سيدُ الصَّحَابَةِ بَعْدَ الرَّسُولِ وَخَيْرُهُمْ وَأَفْضَلُهُمْ، أَعْنِي الصِّدِّيقَ الْأَكْبَرَ وَالْخَلِيفَةَ الْأَعْظَمَ أَبَا بَكْرِ بْنَ أَبِي قُحَافَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، فَإِنَّ الطَّائِفَةَ الْمَخْذُولَةَ مِنَ الرَّافِضَةِ يُعَادُونَ أَفْضَلَ الصَّحَابَةِ ويُبغضونهم ويَسُبُّونهم، عِياذًا بِاللَّهِ مِنْ ذَلِكَ. وَهَذَا يَدُلُّ عَلَى أَنَّ عُقُولَهُمْ مَعْكُوسَةٌ، وَقُلُوبَهُمْ مَنْكُوسَةٌ، فَأَيْنَ هَؤُلَاءِ مِنَ الْإِيمَانِ بِالْقُرْآنِ، إِذْ يسبُّون مَنْ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ؟ وَأَمَّا أَهْلُ السُّنَّةِ فَإِنَّهُمْ يَتَرَضُّونَ عَمَّنْ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، وَيَسُبُّونَ مَنْ سَبَّهُ اللَّهُ وَرَسُولُهُ، وَيُوَالُونَ مَنْ يُوَالِي اللَّهَ، وَيُعَادُونَ مَنْ يُعَادِي اللَّهَ، وَهُمْ مُتَّبِعُونَ لَا مُبْتَدِعُونَ، وَيَقْتَدُونَ وَلَا يَبْتَدُونَ وَلِهَذَا هُمْ حِزْبُ اللَّهِ الْمُفْلِحُونَ وَعِبَادُهُ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ.

---

## 9:101 — verse 101

### Translation

The Almighty informs His Messenger ﷺ, that among the Arab tribes around Medina there are hypocrites, and among the people of Medina too there are hypocrites, {who have grown practiced in hypocrisy}, meaning: they have become habituated and persisted in it. From this comes the expression "a rebellious devil" (shaytan marid) and "a defiant one" (mارid), and one says "so-and-so rebelled against God," meaning he became insolent and arrogant.

His saying, {You do not know them, We know them}, does not contradict the Almighty's saying: {And if We willed, We would show them to you, and you would recognize them by their marks, and you will surely recognize them in the tone of speech} [Muhammad: 30], because this latter case is a matter of discerning them through traits by which they are known, not that he ﷺ knew all the people of hypocrisy and doubt around him by specific identification. He did know that some of those he mixed with among the people of Medina harbored hypocrisy, even though he saw them morning and evening. The soundness of this is attested by what Imam Ahmad related in his Musnad, where he said:

[chain] Muhammad ibn Ja'far told us, Shu'bah told us, from al-Nu'man ibn Salim, from a man, from Jubayr ibn Mut'im, may God be pleased with him, who said: I said, "O Messenger of God, they claim that we have no reward at Mecca." He said, "Your rewards will surely come to you even if you were in a fox's den." And the Messenger of God ﷺ inclined his head toward me and said, "There are hypocrites among my companions."

The meaning of this is that some of the hypocrites and rumor mongers sometimes utter speech that has no truth to it, and it was from the likes of them that this statement heard by Jubayr ibn Mut'im originated. It was mentioned earlier, in the commentary on His saying, {and they resolved upon what they could not attain} [al-Tawbah: 74], that he, peace be upon him, informed Hudhayfah of the specific identities of fourteen or fifteen hypocrites. This is a specific instance and does not imply that he had knowledge of the names and identities of all of them without exception. And God knows best.

Al-Hafiz Ibn 'Asakir related, in the biographical entry on "Abu 'Umar al-Bayruti," by way of Hisham ibn 'Ammar: Sadaqah ibn Khalid told us, Ibn Jabir told us, an elder of Beirut known as Abu 'Umar told me, I think he related to me from Abu al-Darda', that a man called "Harmalah" came to the Prophet ﷺ and said: "Faith is here," pointing with his hand to his tongue, "and hypocrisy is here," pointing with his hand to his heart, "and he mentions God only a little." The Messenger of God ﷺ said: "O God, grant him a tongue that remembers and a heart that gives thanks, and provide him with love of me and love of those who love me, and turn his affair toward good." The man said: "O Messenger of God, I had companions among the hypocrites and I was a leader among them, shall I not bring them to you?" He said: "Whoever comes to us, we will seek forgiveness for him, and whoever persists in his religion, God is most entitled to deal with him, and do not ever tear away the veil that covers anyone."

He said: and likewise Abu Ahmad al-Hakim related it, from Abu Bakr al-Baghandi, from Hisham ibn 'Ammar, with the same chain.

'Abd al-Razzaq said: Ma'mar informed us, from Qatadah, concerning this verse, that he said: What is the matter with people who burden themselves with knowledge only of other people, saying "so-and-so is in Paradise and so-and-so is in the Fire"? Yet if you ask one of them about himself, he says "I do not know." By my life, you yourself know more about yourself than you know about the states of other people, and you have burdened yourself with something the prophets before you did not burden themselves with. The prophet of God Noah (peace be upon him) said: {He said, and what knowledge have I of what they used to do?} [al-Shu'ara: 112], and the prophet of God Shu'ayb (peace be upon him) said: {What remains with God is better for you, if you are believers, and I am not a keeper over you} [Hud: 86], and God said to His Prophet ﷺ: {You do not know them, We know them}.

Al-Suddi said, from Abu Malik, from Ibn 'Abbas, concerning this verse: The Messenger of God ﷺ stood delivering a sermon on the day of Jumu'ah and said, "Get out, O so-and-so, for you are a hypocrite, and get out, O so-and-so, for you are a hypocrite." He expelled some of them from the mosque, exposing them. 'Umar arrived while they were being expelled from the mosque, and he hid from them out of shame, for he had not attended the Friday prayer and thought that the people had already dispersed, while they hid from 'Umar thinking he had learned of their affair. Then 'Umar came and entered the mosque and found that the people had not yet prayed. A man among the Muslims said to him: "Rejoice, O 'Umar, God has exposed the hypocrites today." Ibn 'Abbas said: This was the first punishment, when he expelled them from the mosque, and the second punishment is the punishment of the grave.

Likewise al-Thawri said, from al-Suddi, from Abu Malik, something similar to this.

Mujahid said concerning His saying, {We will punish them twice}: meaning killing and captivity. And he said, in another report: by hunger and the punishment of the grave, {then they will be returned to a great punishment}.

Ibn Jurayj said: the punishment of this world and the punishment of the grave, then they will be returned to the punishment of the Fire.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: a punishment in this world and a punishment in the grave.

'Abd al-Rahman ibn Zayd said: as for the punishment in this world, it is wealth and children, and he recited the saying of God: {So let not their wealth and their children impress you; God only wants to punish them thereby in this world} [al-Tawbah: 85]. These calamities are for them a punishment, while for the believers the same things are a reward, and the punishment in the Hereafter is in the Fire, {then they will be returned to a great punishment}, he said: the Fire.

Muhammad ibn Ishaq said: {We will punish them twice}, he said: this is, as it has reached me, what they are afflicted with concerning the matter of Islam and the rage that enters upon them because of it without their reckoning, then their punishment in the graves when they come to them, then the great punishment to which they will be returned, the punishment of the Hereafter and abiding therein forever.

Sa'id said, from Qatadah, concerning His saying, {We will punish them twice}: the punishment of this world and the punishment of the grave, {then they will be returned to a great punishment}.

It has been mentioned to us that the Prophet of God ﷺ confided to Hudhayfah the names of twelve men among the hypocrites, and said: "Six of them, the abscess will suffice for them: a flame from the fire of Hell will take hold in the shoulder of one of them until it reaches his chest, and six of them will die an ordinary death." And it has been mentioned to us that 'Umar ibn al-Khattab, may God be pleased with him, whenever a man whom he suspected to be among them died, would look to Hudhayfah, and if he prayed over him he would do so as well, and otherwise he would leave him. And it has been mentioned to us that 'Umar said to Hudhayfah: "I adjure you by God, am I among them?" He said: "No, and I will not clear anyone of them after you."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى رَسُولَهُ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِ، أَنَّ فِي أَحْيَاءِ الْعَرَبِ مِمَّنْ حَوْلَ الْمَدِينَةِ مُنَافِقِينَ، وَفِي أَهْلِ الْمَدِينَةِ أَيْضًا مُنَافِقُونَ ﴿مَرَدُوا عَلَى النِّفَاقِ﴾ أَيْ: مَرَنُوا وَاسْتَمَرُّوا عَلَيْهِ: وَمِنْهُ يُقَالُ: شَيْطَانٌ مَرِيدٌ وَمَارِدٌ، وَيُقَالُ: تَمَرَّدَ فُلَانٌ عَلَى اللَّهِ، أَيْ: عَتَا وَتَجَبَّرَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَا تَعْلَمُهُمْ نَحْنُ نَعْلَمُهُمْ﴾ لَا يُنَافِي قَوْلَهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَوْ نَشَاءُ لأرَيْنَاكَهُمْ فَلَعَرَفْتَهُمْ بِسِيمَاهُمْ وَلَتَعْرِفَنَّهُمْ فِي لَحْنِ الْقَوْلِ﴾ الْآيَةَ [مُحَمَّدٍ:٣٠] ؛ لِأَنَّ هَذَا مِنْ بَابِ التَّوَسُّمِ فِيهِمْ بِصِفَاتٍ يُعْرَفُونَ بِهَا، لَا أَنَّهُ يَعْرِفُ جَمِيعَ مَنْ عِنْدَهُ مِنْ أَهْلِ النِّفَاقِ وَالرَّيْبِ عَلَى التَّعْيِينِ. وَقَدْ كَانَ يَعْلَمُ أَنَّ فِي بَعْضِ مَنْ يُخَالِطُهُ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْمَدِينَةِ نِفَاقًا، وَإِنْ كَانَ يَرَاهُ صَبَاحًا وَمَسَاءً، وَشَاهِدُ هَذَا بِالصِّحَّةِ مَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ فِي مُسْنَدِهِ حَيْثُ قَالَ:

حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ، حَدَّثَنَا شُعْبَةُ، عَنِ النُّعْمَانِ بْنِ سَالِمٍ، عَنْ رَجُلٍ، عَنْ جُبَير بْنِ مُطْعِمٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، قَالَ: قُلْتُ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّهُمْ يَزْعُمُونَ أَنَّهُ لَيْسَ لَنَا أَجْرٌ بِمَكَّةَ، فَقَالَ: لَتَأْتِيَنَّكُمْ أُجُورُكُمْ وَلَوْ كُنْتُمْ فِي جُحر ثَعْلَبٍ وَأَصْغَى إليَّ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ بِرَأْسِهِ فَقَالَ: "إِنَّ فِي أَصْحَابِي مُنَافِقِينَ" 

وَمَعْنَاهُ: أَنَّهُ قَدْ يَبُوحُ بَعْضُ الْمُنَافِقِينَ وَالْمُرْجِفِينَ مِنَ الْكَلَامِ بِمَا لَا صِحَّةَ لَهُ، وَمِنْ مِثْلِهِمْ صَدَر هَذَا الْكَلَامُ الَّذِي سَمِعَهُ جُبَير بْنُ مُطْعِمٍ. وَتَقَدَّمَ فِي تَفْسِيرِ قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَهَمُّوا بِمَا لَمْ يَنَالُوا﴾ [التَّوْبَةَ:٧٤] أَنَّهُ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ أَعْلَمَ حُذَيفة بِأَعْيَانِ أَرْبَعَةَ عَشَرَ أَوْ خَمْسَةَ عَشَرَ مُنَافِقًا، وَهَذَا تَخْصِيصٌ لَا يَقْتَضِي أَنَّهُ اطَّلَعَ عَلَى أَسْمَائِهِمْ وَأَعْيَانِهِمْ كُلِّهِمْ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَرَوَى الْحَافِظُ ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي تَرْجَمَةِ "أَبِي عُمَرَ الْبَيْرُوتِيِّ" مِنْ طَرِيقِ هِشَامُ بْنُ عَمَّارٍ: حَدَّثَنَا صَدَقَةُ بْنُ خَالِدٍ، حَدَّثَنَا بْنُ جَابِرٍ، حَدَّثَنِي شَيْخُ بَيْرُوتَ يُكَنَّى أَبَا عُمَرَ، أَظُنُّهُ حَدَّثَنِي عَنْ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ؛ أَنَّ رَجُلًا يُقَالُ لَهُ "حَرْمَلَةُ" أَتَى النَّبِيَّ ﷺ فَقَالَ: الْإِيمَانُ هَاهُنَا -وَأَشَارَ بِيَدِهِ إِلَى لِسَانِهِ -وَالنِّفَاقُ هَاهُنَا -وَأَشَارَ بِيَدِهِ إِلَى قَلْبِهِ وَلَمْ يَذْكُرِ اللَّهَ إِلَّا قَلِيلًا. فَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "اللَّهُمَّ اجْعَلْ لَهُ لِسَانًا ذَاكِرًا، وَقَلْبًا شَاكِرًا، وَارْزُقْهُ حُبّي، وحبَّ مَنْ يُحِبُّنِي، وصَيِّر أَمْرَهُ إِلَى خَيْرٍ". فَقَالَ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، إِنَّهُ كَانَ لِي أَصْحَابٌ مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ وَكُنْتُ رَأْسًا فِيهِمْ، أَفَلَا آتِيكَ بِهِمْ؟ قَالَ: "مَنْ أَتَانَا اسْتَغْفَرْنَا لَهُ، وَمَنْ أَصَرَّ عَلَى دِينِهِ فَاللَّهُ أَوْلَى بِهِ، وَلَا تَخْرِقَنَّ عَلَى أَحَدٍ سِتْرًا" 

قَالَ: وَكَذَا رَوَاهُ أَبُو أَحْمَدَ الْحَاكِمُ، عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرٍ الْبَاغَنْدِيِّ، عَنْ هِشَامِ بْنِ عَمَّارٍ، بِهِ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ: أَخْبَرَنَا مَعْمَرٌ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: مَا بَالُ أقوام يتكلفون علم النَّاسِ؟ فُلَانٌ فِي الْجَنَّةِ وَفُلَانٌ فِي النَّارِ. فَإِذَا سَأَلْتَ أَحَدَهُمْ عَنْ نَفْسِهِ قَالَ: لَا أَدْرِي! لَعَمْرِي أَنْتَ بِنَفْسِكَ أَعْلَمُ مِنْكَ بِأَحْوَالِ النَّاسِ، وَلَقَدْ تَكَلَّفْتَ شَيْئًا مَا تَكَلَّفَهُ الْأَنْبِيَاءُ قَبْلَكَ. قَالَ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ نُوحٌ: ﴿قَالَ وَمَا عِلْمِي بِمَا كَانُوا يَعْمَلُونَ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ: ١١٢] وَقَالَ نَبِيُّ اللَّهِ شُعَيْبٌ: ﴿بَقِيَّةُ اللَّهِ خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ وَمَا أَنَا عَلَيْكُمْ بِحَفِيظٍ﴾ [هُودٍ: ٨٦] وَقَالَ اللَّهُ لِنَبِيِّهِ ﷺ: ﴿لَا تَعْلَمُهُمْ نَحْنُ نَعْلَمُهُمْ﴾ .

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي مَالِكٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ قَالَ: قَامَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ خَطِيبًا يَوْمَ الْجُمُعَةِ فَقَالَ: "اخْرُجْ يَا فُلَانُ، فَإِنَّكَ مُنَافِقٌ، وَاخْرُجْ يَا فُلَانُ فَإِنَّكَ مُنَافِقٌ". فَأَخْرَجَ مِنَ الْمَسْجِدِ نَاسًا مِنْهُمْ، فَضَحَهُمْ. فَجَاءَ عُمَرُ وَهُمْ يُخْرَجُونَ مِنَ الْمَسْجِدِ فَاخْتَبَأَ مِنْهُمْ حَيَاءً أَنَّهُ لَمْ يَشْهَدِ الْجُمُعَةِ وَظَنَّ أَنَّ النَّاسَ قَدِ انْصَرَفُوا، وَاخْتَبَئُوا هُمْ مِنْ عُمَرَ، ظَنُّوا أَنَّهُ قَدْ عَلِمَ بِأَمْرِهِمْ. فَجَاءَ عُمَرُ فَدَخَلَ الْمَسْجِدَ فَإِذَا النَّاسُ لَمْ يُصَلُّوا، فَقَالَ لَهُ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ: أَبْشِرْ يَا عُمَرُ، قَدْ فَضَحَ اللَّهُ الْمُنَافِقِينَ الْيَوْمَ. قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: فَهَذَا الْعَذَابُ الْأَوَّلُ حِينَ أَخْرَجَهُمْ مِنَ الْمَسْجِدِ، وَالْعَذَابُ الثَّانِي عَذَابُ الْقَبْرِ 

وَكَذَا قَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنِ السُّدِّيِّ، عَنْ أَبِي مَالِكٍ نَحْوَ هَذَا.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿سَنُعَذِّبُهُمْ مَرَّتَيْنِ﴾ يَعْنِي: الْقَتْلَ وَالسِّبَاءَ وَقَالَ -فِي رِوَايَةٍ -بِالْجُوعِ، وَعَذَابِ الْقَبْرِ، ﴿ثُمَّ يُرَدُّونَ إِلَى عَذَابٍ عَظِيمٍ﴾

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: عَذَابُ الدُّنْيَا، وَعَذَابُ الْقَبْرِ، ثُمَّ يَرُدُّونَ إِلَى عَذَابِ النَّارِ.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: عَذَابٌ فِي الدُّنْيَا، وَعَذَابٌ فِي الْقَبْرِ 

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ زَيْدٍ: أَمَّا عَذَابٌ فِي الدُّنْيَا فَالْأَمْوَالُ وَالْأَوْلَادُ، وَقَرَأَ قَوْلَ اللَّهِ ﴿فَلا تُعْجِبْكَ أَمْوَالُهُمْ وَأَوْلادُهُمْ إِنَّمَا يُرِيدُ اللَّهُ أَنْ يُعَذِّبَهُمْ بِهَا فِي الدُّنْيَا﴾ [التَّوْبَةِ: ٨٥] فَهَذِهِ الْمَصَائِبُ لَهُمْ عَذَابٌ، وَهِيَ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَجْرٌ، وَعَذَابٌ فِي الْآخِرَةِ فِي النَّارِ ﴿ثُمَّ يُرَدُّونَ إِلَى عَذَابٍ عَظِيمٍ﴾ قَالَ: النَّارُ.

وَقَالَ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ: ﴿سَنُعَذِّبُهُمْ مَرَّتَيْنِ﴾ قَالَ: هُوَ -فِيمَا بَلَغَنِي -مَا هُمْ فِيهِ مِنْ أَمْرِ الْإِسْلَامِ، وَمَا يَدْخُلُ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنْ غَيْظِ ذَلِكَ عَلَى غَيْرِ حِسْبَةٍ، ثُمَّ عَذَابُهُمْ فِي الْقُبُورِ إِذَا صَارُوا إِلَيْهَا، ثُمَّ الْعَذَابُ الْعَظِيمُ الَّذِي يُرَدُّونَ إِلَيْهِ، عَذَابُ الْآخِرَةِ وَالْخَلَدِ فِيهِ.

وَقَالَ سَعِيدٌ، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿سَنُعَذِّبُهُمْ مَرَّتَيْنِ﴾ عذاب الدنيا، وعذاب القبر، ﴿ثُمَّ يُرَدُّونَ إِلَى عَذَابٍ عَظِيمٍ﴾

ذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّ نَبِيَّ اللَّهِ ﷺ أسرَّ إِلَى حُذَيْفَةَ بِاثْنَيْ عَشَرَ رَجُلًا مِنَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ، فَقَالَ: "سِتَّةٌ مِنْهُمْ تَكْفِيكَهُمُ الدُّبَيْلة: سِرَاجٌ مِنْ نَارِ جَهَنَّمَ، يَأْخُذُ فِي كَتِفِ أَحَدِهِمْ حَتَّى يُفْضِيَ إِلَى صَدْرِهِ، وَسِتَّةٌ يَمُوتُونَ مَوْتًا". وَذُكِرَ لَنَا أَنَّ عُمَرَ بْنَ الْخَطَّابِ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، كَانَ إِذَا مَاتَ رَجُلٌ مِمَّنْ يُرى أَنَّهُ مِنْهُمْ، نَظَرَ إِلَى حُذَيْفَةَ، فَإِنْ صَلَّى عَلَيْهِ وَإِلَّا تَرَكَهُ. وَذُكر لَنَا أَنَّ عُمَرَ قَالَ لِحُذَيْفَةَ: أَنْشُدُكَ بِاللَّهِ، أَمِنْهُمْ أَنَا؟ قَالَ: لَا. وَلَا أُومِنُ مِنْهَا أَحَدًا بَعْدَكَ.

---

## 9:102 — verse 102

### Translation

When the Almighty had made clear the condition of the hypocrites who held back from the campaign out of aversion to it, and out of denial and doubt, He proceeded to make clear the condition of the sinners who had lagged behind from the jihad out of laziness and inclination toward ease, while still possessing faith and affirmation of the truth. So He said: {And others have confessed their sins}, meaning: they acknowledged them and confessed between themselves and their Lord. They also had other righteous deeds, which they mixed with these sins. Such people are under God's pardon and forgiveness.

This verse, although it was revealed concerning specific individuals, is nonetheless general in scope, applying to every sinner who errs while remaining sincere, even if tainted by wrongdoing.

Mujahid said: it was revealed concerning Abu Lubabah, when he said to Banu Qurayzah, "It is slaughter," gesturing with his hand toward his throat.

Ibn Abbas said: {And others} was revealed concerning Abu Lubabah and a group of his companions who had held back from the expedition of Tabuk. Some said: Abu Lubabah and five with him; it was also said: and seven with him; and it was also said: and nine with him. When the Prophet ﷺ returned from his expedition, they bound themselves to the pillars of the mosque and swore that none would release them except the Messenger of God ﷺ. When God sent down this verse, {And others have confessed their sins}, the Prophet ﷺ released them and pardoned them.

Al-Bukhari said: [chain] Samurah ibn Jundab said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said to us: "Two visitors came to me tonight and took me away. We came to a city built with bricks of gold and bricks of silver. There met us men, half of whose form was as good as anything you could see, and half as ugly as anything you could see. The two said to them: 'Go and throw yourselves into that river.' So they threw themselves into it, then returned to us, that ugliness having left them, so that they had become in the best of forms. The two said to me: 'This is the Garden of Eden, and this is your dwelling.' They said: 'As for the people who were half handsome and half ugly, they had mixed righteous deeds with other evil ones, so God overlooked their sins for them.'"

Thus it was narrated in abridged form, in the exegesis of this verse.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا بَيَّن تَعَالَى حَالَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ الْمُتَخَلِّفِينَ عَنِ الغَزاة رَغْبَةً عَنْهَا وَتَكْذِيبًا وَشَكًّا، شَرَعَ فِي بَيَانِ حَالِ الْمُذْنِبِينَ الَّذِينَ تَأَخَّرُوا عَنِ الْجِهَادِ كَسَلًا وَمَيْلًا إِلَى الرَّاحَةِ، مَعَ إِيمَانِهِمْ وَتَصْدِيقِهِمْ بِالْحَقِّ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَآخَرُونَ اعْتَرَفُوا بِذُنُوبِهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: أَقَرُّوا بِهَا وَاعْتَرَفُوا فِيمَا بَيْنَهُمْ وَبَيْنَ رَبِّهم، وَلَهُمْ أَعْمَالٌ أخرَ صَالِحَةٌ، خَلَطُوا هَذِهِ بِتِلْكَ، فَهَؤُلَاءِ تَحْتَ عَفْوِ اللَّهِ وَغُفْرَانِهِ.

وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ -وَإِنْ كَانَتْ نَزَلَتْ فِي أُنَاسٍ مُعَيَّنِينَ -إِلَّا أَنَّهَا عَامَّةٌ فِي كل المذنبين الخاطئين المخلصين الْمُتَلَوِّثِينَ.

وَقَدْ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: إِنَّهَا نَزَلَتْ فِي أَبِي لُبَابة لَمَّا قَالَ لِبَنِي قُرَيْظَةَ: إِنَّهُ الذَّبْحُ، وَأَشَارَ بِيَدِهِ إِلَى حَلْقِهِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَآخَرُونَ﴾ نَزَلَتْ فِي أَبِي لُبابة وَجَمَاعَةٍ مِنْ أَصْحَابِهِ، تَخَلَّفُوا عَنْ غَزْوَةِ تَبُوكَ، فَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: أَبُو لُبَابَةَ وَخَمْسَةٌ مَعَهُ، وَقِيلَ: وَسَبْعَةٌ مَعَهُ، وَقِيلَ: وَتِسْعَةٌ مَعَهُ، فَلَمَّا رَجَعَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ مِنْ غَزْوَتِهِ رَبَطُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ بِسَوَارِي الْمَسْجِدِ، وَحَلَفُوا لَا يَحُلُّهُمْ إِلَّا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَلَمَّا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿وَآخَرُونَ اعْتَرَفُوا بِذُنُوبِهِمْ﴾ أَطْلَقَهُمُ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ، وَعَفَا عَنْهُمْ.

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا مُؤمَّل بْنُ هِشَامٍ، حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، حَدَّثَنَا عَوْفٌ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو رَجَاءٍ، حَدَّثَنَا سَمُرَة بْنِ جُنْدَب قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَنَا: "أَتَانِي اللَّيْلَةَ آتِيَانِ فَابْتَعَثَانِي فَانْتَهَيْنَا إِلَى مَدِينَةٍ مَبْنِيَّةٍ بِلَبِنٍ ذَهَبٍ ولَبِن فِضَّةٍ، فَتَلَقَّانَا رِجَالٌ شَطْر مِنْ خَلْقِهِمْ كَأَحْسَنِ مَا أَنْتَ رَاء، وَشَطْرٌ كَأَقْبَحِ مَا أَنْتَ رَاءٍ، قَالَا لَهُمْ: اذْهَبُوا فَقَعُوا فِي ذَلِكَ النَّهْرِ. فَوَقَعُوا فِيهِ، ثُمَّ رَجَعُوا إِلَيْنَا قَدْ ذَهَبَ ذَلِكَ السُّوءُ عَنْهُمْ، فَصَارُوا فِي أَحْسَنِ صُورَةٍ، قَالَا لِي: هَذِهِ جَنَّةُ عَدْنٍ، وَهَذَا مَنْزِلُكَ. قَالَا أَمَّا الْقَوْمُ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا شَطر مِنْهُمْ حَسَن وَشَطْرٌ مِنْهُمْ قَبِيحٌ، فَإِنَّهُمْ خَلَطُوا عَمَلًا صَالِحًا وَآخَرَ سَيِّئًا، فَتَجَاوَزَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ".

هَكَذَا رَوَاهُ مختصرًا، في تفسير هذه الآية.

---

## 9:103-104 — verses 103-104 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Allah Almighty commanded His Messenger ﷺ to take from their wealth a charity by which he would purify them and cause them to grow in righteousness. This is general in application, even though some scholars refer the pronoun in "their wealth" back to those who confessed their sins and mixed a righteous deed with another that was evil. For this reason some of those Arab tribes who withheld the zakat believed that paying zakat to the imam (leader) was no longer required, and that this obligation had been specific to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ alone. They cited as their proof the words of the Almighty: {Take from their wealth a charity by which you purify them and cause them to grow in righteousness, and pray for them, for indeed your prayer is a source of tranquility for them.} As-Siddiq Abu Bakr and the rest of the Companions refuted this corrupt interpretation and understanding, and they fought them until they paid the zakat to the caliph just as they had paid it to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, so that as-Siddiq said: "By Allah, if they withhold from me even a hobbling rope" (in another version: "a young she-goat") "which they used to pay to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, I will fight them over withholding it."

Regarding His saying, {and pray for them}: that is, supplicate for them and ask forgiveness for them, as Muslim related in his Sahih from Abdullah ibn Abi Awfa, who said: "When the Messenger of Allah ﷺ was brought the charity of a people, he would pray for them. So my father brought him his charity, and he said: 'O Allah, send blessing upon the family of Abu Awfa.'" And in another hadith, a woman said: "O Messenger of Allah, pray for me and for my husband." He said: "May Allah send blessing upon you and upon your husband."

Regarding His saying, {Indeed your prayer (salatuka)}: some read it as "salawatika" (your prayers), in the plural, while others read {inna salataka} in the singular.

{is a source of tranquility (sakan) for them}: Ibn Abbas said it means "a mercy for them." Qatadah said it means "dignity."

Regarding His saying, {and Allah is All-Hearing}: that is, of your supplication, {All-Knowing}: that is, of who among you deserves this and who is worthy of it.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] ... a son of Hudhayfah, from his father, that the Prophet ﷺ, when he prayed for a man, that prayer would reach him, his child, and his child's child.

He then related it also [chain] ... a son of Hudhayfah, Mis'ar said he once mentioned it from Hudhayfah himself: "Indeed the prayer of the Prophet ﷺ reaches the man, his child, and his child's child."

Regarding His saying, {Do they not know that it is Allah who accepts repentance from His servants and takes the charities}: this is an incitement toward repentance and charity, each of which wipes away sins, purges them, and effaces them.

The Almighty informs us that everyone who turns to Him in repentance, He turns to accept it, and that whoever gives charity from lawful earnings, Allah Almighty accepts it with His right hand and causes it to grow for its giver, until a single date becomes like Mount Uhud, as has come in the hadith from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, as reported by ath-Thawri and Waki', both from Abbad ibn Mansur, from al-Qasim ibn Muhammad, who heard Abu Hurairah say: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Indeed Allah accepts charity and takes it with His right hand, and He causes it to grow for one of you just as one of you raises his young horse, until a single morsel becomes like Mount Uhud." Confirmation of this is found in the Book of Allah, Mighty and Majestic: {[Do they not know that Allah] it is Who accepts repentance from His servants and takes the charities} and His saying, {Allah effaces usury and causes charities to grow} [al-Baqarah: 276].

Ath-Thawri and al-A'mash both said, from Abdullah ibn as-Sa'ib, from Abdullah ibn Abi Qatadah, who said: Abdullah ibn Mas'ud, may Allah be pleased with him, said: "Indeed charity falls into the hand of Allah, Mighty and Majestic, before it falls into the hand of the one who asks." Then he recited this verse: {Do they not know that it is Allah who accepts repentance from His servants and takes the charities}.

Ibn Asakir related in his history, in the biography of Abdullah ibn ash-Sha'ir as-Saksaki ad-Dimashqi, originally from Homs, who was one of the jurists and reported from Mu'awiyah and others, and from whom Hawshab ibn Sayf as-Saksaki al-Himsi narrated, that he said: The people went out on a military campaign in the time of Mu'awiyah, may Allah be pleased with him, under the command of Abd ar-Rahman ibn Khalid ibn al-Walid. A man among the Muslims embezzled one hundred Byzantine dinars. When the army returned, he regretted it and went to the commander, but the commander refused to accept it from him, saying: "The people have already dispersed, and I will not accept it from you until you bring it to Allah on the Day of Resurrection." So the man went around asking the Companions, and they told him the same thing. When he arrived in Damascus, he went to Mu'awiyah to have him accept it, but Mu'awiyah refused as well. He left from him weeping and reciting the words of returning to Allah, and he passed by Abdullah ibn ash-Sha'ir as-Saksaki, who said to him: "What makes you weep?" So he told him his story, and Abdullah said: "Will you obey me?" He said: "Yes." He said: "Go to Mu'awiyah and say to him: Accept from me my fifth (khums)." So he should give him twenty dinars, and as for the remaining eighty, he should give them in charity on behalf of that army, "for Allah accepts repentance from His servants, and He knows best their names and their whereabouts." So the man did that, and Mu'awiyah, may Allah be pleased with him, said: "That I should have been the one to give him this ruling would be dearer to me than everything I possess. The man has done well."

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

أَمَرَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى رَسُولَهُ ﷺ بِأَنْ يأخُذَ مِنْ أَمْوَالِهِمْ صدقَة يُطَهِّرُهُمْ وَيُزَكِّيهِمْ بِهَا، وَهَذَا عَامٌّ وَإِنْ أَعَادَ بَعْضُهُمُ الضَّمِيرَ فِي "أَمْوَالِهِمْ" إِلَى الَّذِينَ اعْتَرَفُوا بِذُنُوبِهِمْ وَخَلَطُوا عَمَلًا صَالِحًا وَآخَرَ سَيِّئًا؛ وَلِهَذَا اعْتَقَدَ بَعْضُ مَانِعِي الزَّكَاةِ مِنْ أَحْيَاءِ الْعَرَبِ أَنَّ دَفْعِ الزَّكَاةِ إِلَى الْإِمَامِ لَا يَكُونُ، وَإِنَّمَا كَانَ هَذَا خَاصًّا بِرَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ؛ وَلِهَذَا احْتَجُّوا بِقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿خُذْ مِنْ أَمْوَالِهِمْ صَدَقَةً تُطَهِّرُهُمْ وَتُزَكِّيهِمْ بِهَا وَصَلِّ عَلَيْهِمْ إِنَّ صَلاتَكَ سَكَنٌ لَهُمْ﴾ وَقَدْ رَدَّ عَلَيْهِمْ هَذَا التَّأْوِيلَ وَالْفَهْمَ الْفَاسِدَ الصَّدِيقُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ وَسَائِرُ الصَّحَابَةِ، وَقَاتَلُوهُمْ حَتَّى أَدَّوُا الزَّكَاةَ إِلَى الْخَلِيفَةِ، كَمَا كَانُوا يُؤدونها إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، حَتَّى قَالَ الصِّدِّيقُ: وَاللَّهِ لَوْ مَنَعُونِي عِقالا -وَفِي رِوَايَةٍ: عَناقًا -يُؤدُّونه إِلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ لَأُقَاتِلَنَّهُمْ عَلَى مَنْعِهِ. 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَصَلِّ عَلَيْهِمْ﴾ أَيْ: ادْعُ لَهُمْ وَاسْتَغْفِرْ لَهُمْ، كَمَا رَوَاهُ مُسْلِمٌ فِي صَحِيحِهِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي أَوْفَى قَالَ: كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ إِذَا أُتِيَ بِصَدَقَةِ قَوْمٍ صَلَّى عَلَيْهِمْ، فَأَتَاهُ أَبِي بِصَدَقَتِهِ فَقَالَ: "اللَّهُمَّ صَل عَلَى آلِ أَبِي أَوْفَى" وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الْآخَرِ: أَنَّ امْرَأَةً قَالَتْ: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ، صَلِّ عليَّ وَعَلَى زَوْجِي. فَقَالَ: "صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْكِ، وَعَلَى زَوْجِكِ". 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّ صَلاتك﴾ : قَرَأَ بَعْضُهُمْ: "صَلَوَاتِكَ" عَلَى الْجَمْعِ، وَآخَرُونَ قَرَءُوا: ﴿إِنَّ صَلاتَكَ﴾ عَلَى الْإِفْرَادِ.

﴿سَكَنٌ لَهُمْ﴾ قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: رَحْمَةٌ لَهُمْ. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: وَقَارٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَاللَّهُ سَمِيعٌ﴾ أَيْ: لِدُعَائِكَ ﴿عَلِيمٌ﴾ أَيْ: بِمَنْ يَسْتَحِقُّ ذَلِكَ مِنْكَ وَمَنْ هُوَ أَهْلٌ لَهُ.

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا وَكِيع، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو العُمَيْس، عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ عُتْبَةَ، عَنِ ابْنٍ لِحُذَيْفَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ؛ أَنَّ النَّبِيَّ ﷺ كَانَ إِذَا دَعَا لِرَجُلٍ أَصَابَتْهُ، وَأَصَابَتْ وَلَدَهُ، وَوَلَدَ وَلَدِهِ. 

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ عَنْ أَبِي نُعَيم، عَنْ مِسْعَر، عَنْ أَبِي بَكْرِ بْنِ عَمْرِو بْنِ عُتْبَةَ، عَنِ ابْنٍ لحذيفة -قال مسعر: وَقَدْ ذَكَرَهُ مَرَّةً عَنْ حُذَيْفَةَ -: إِنَّ صَلَاةَ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ لتُدرك الرَّجُلَ وَوَلَدَهُ وَوَلَدَ وَلَدِهِ. 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿أَلَمْ يَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ هُوَ يَقْبَلُ التَّوْبَةَ عَنْ عِبَادِهِ وَيَأْخُذُ الصَّدَقَاتِ﴾ هَذَا تَهْيِيجٌ إِلَى التَّوْبَةِ وَالصَّدَقَةِ اللَّتَيْنِ كَلَّ مِنْهَا يحطُّ الذُّنُوبَ وَيُمَحِّصُهَا وَيَمْحَقُهَا.

وَأَخْبَرَ تَعَالَى أَنَّ كُلَّ مَنْ تَابَ إِلَيْهِ تَابَ عَلَيْهِ، وَمَنْ تَصَدَّقَ بِصَدَقَةٍ مِنْ كَسْبِ حَلَالٍ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ تَعَالَى يَتَقَبَّلُهَا بِيَمِينِهِ فَيُرَبِّيهَا لِصَاحِبِهَا، حَتَّى تَصِيرَ التَّمْرَةُ مِثْلَ أُحُدٍ. كَمَا جَاءَ بِذَلِكَ الْحَدِيثُ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ -كَمَا قَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ وَوَكِيعٌ، كِلَاهُمَا عَنْ عَبَّادِ بْنِ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ أَبَا هُرَيْرَةَ يَقُولُ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَقْبَلُ الصَّدَقَةَ وَيَأْخُذُهَا بِيَمِينِهِ فَيُرَبِّيهَا لِأَحَدِكُمْ، كَمَا يُرَبِّي أَحَدُكُمْ مُهْرَهُ، حَتَّى إِنَّ اللُّقْمَةَ لتَصير مِثْلَ أُحُدٍ"، وَتَصْدِيقُ ذَلِكَ فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ، عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: ﴿ [أَلَمْ يَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ] هُوَ يَقْبَلُ التَّوْبَةَ عَنْ عِبَادِهِ وَيَأْخُذُ الصَّدَقَاتِ﴾ وَ [قَوْلُهُ] ﴿يَمْحَقُ اللَّهُ الرِّبَا وَيُرْبِي الصَّدَقَاتِ﴾ [الْبَقَرَةِ: ٢٧٦] . 

وَقَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ وَالْأَعْمَشُ كِلَاهُمَا، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ السَّائِبِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي قَتَادَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: إِنَّ الصَّدَقَةَ تَقَعُ فِي يَدِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ قَبْلَ أَنْ تَقَعَ فِي يَدِ السَّائِلِ. ثُمَّ قَرَأَ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿أَلَمْ يَعْلَمُوا أَنَّ اللَّهَ هُوَ يَقْبَلُ التَّوْبَةَ عَنْ عِبَادِهِ وَيَأْخُذُ الصَّدَقَاتِ﴾ .

وَقَدْ رَوَى ابْنُ عَسَاكِرَ فِي تَارِيخِهِ، فِي تَرْجَمَةِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الشَّاعِرِ السَّكْسَكي الدِّمَشْقِيِّ -وَأَصْلُهُ حِمْصِيٌّ، وَكَانَ أَحَدَ الْفُقَهَاءِ، رَوَى عَنْ مُعَاوِيَةَ وَغَيْرِهِ، وَحَكَى عَنْهُ حَوْشَبُ بْنُ سَيْفٍ السَّكْسَكِيُّ الْحِمْصِيُّ -قَالَ: غَزَا النَّاسُ فِي زَمَانِ مُعَاوِيَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، وَعَلَيْهِمْ عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ خَالِدِ بْنِ الْوَلِيدِ، فَغَلَّ رَجُلٌ مِنَ الْمُسْلِمِينَ مِائَةَ دِينَارٍ رُومِيَّةٍ. فَلَمَّا قَفَلَ الْجَيْشُ نَدم وَأَتَى الأميرَ، فَأَبَى أَنْ يَقْبَلَهَا مِنْهُ، وَقَالَ: قَدْ تَفَرَّقَ النَّاسَ وَلَنْ أَقْبَلَهَا مِنْكَ، حَتَّى تَأْتِيَ اللَّهَ بِهَا يَوْمَ القيامةَ فَجَعَلَ الرَّجُلُ يَسْتَقْرِئُ الصَّحَابَةَ، فَيَقُولُونَ لَهُ مِثْلَ ذَلِكَ، فَلَمَّا قَدِمَ دِمَشْقَ ذَهَبَ إِلَى مُعَاوِيَةَ لِيَقْبَلَهَا مِنْهُ، فَأَبَى عَلَيْهِ. فَخَرَجَ مِنْ عِنْدِهِ وَهُوَ يَبْكِي وَيَسْتَرْجِعُ، فَمَرَّ بِعَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ الشَّاعِرِ السَّكْسَكِيِّ، فَقَالَ لَهُ: مَا يُبْكِيكَ؟ فَذَكَرَ لَهُ أَمْرَهُ، فَقَالَ أمطيعُني أَنْتَ؟ فَقَالَ: نَعَمْ، فَقَالَ: اذْهَبْ إِلَى مُعَاوِيَةَ فَقُلْ لَهُ: اقْبَلْ مِنِّي خُمسك، فَادْفَعْ إِلَيْهِ عِشْرِينَ دِينَارًا، وَانْظُرِ الثَّمَانِينَ الْبَاقِيَةَ فَتَصَدَّقْ بِهَا عَنْ ذَلِكَ الْجَيْشِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَقْبَلُ التَّوْبَةَ عَنْ عِبَادِهِ، وَهُوَ أَعْلَمُ بِأَسْمَائِهِمْ وَمَكَانِهِمْ فَفَعَلَ الرَّجُلُ، فَقَالَ مُعَاوِيَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُ: لَأَنْ أَكُونَ أفتيتُه بِهَا أَحَبُّ إِلَيَّ مِنْ كل شيء أملكه، أحسن الرجل".

---

## 9:105 — verse 105

### Translation

Mujahid said: this is a warning, meaning from Allah, Blessed and Exalted, to those who oppose His commands, that their deeds will be presented before Him, Blessed and Exalted, and before the Messenger, and before the believers. This is bound to occur on the Day of Resurrection, as He said: {On that Day you will be exposed, and no hidden thing of yours will remain concealed} [al-Haqqah: 18], and He said: {The Day when secrets are tested} [al-Tariq: 9], and He said: {and that which is in the breasts is brought out} [al-'Adiyat: 10]. And this may also become manifest to people in this world, as Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] Hasan ibn Musa, from Ibn Lahi'ah, from Darraj, from Abu al-Haytham, from Abu Sa'id, from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, that he said: "If one of you were to act inside a solid rock with no door and no opening in it, Allah would bring out his deed for the people, whatever it may be."

It has also been reported that the deeds of the living are presented to the dead among their relatives and kinsfolk in the barzakh (intermediate realm), as Abu Dawud al-Tayalisi said: [chain] al-Salt ibn Dinar, from al-Hasan, from Jabir ibn Abdullah, who said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "Indeed your deeds are presented to your relatives and kinsfolk in their graves. If it is good, they rejoice at it, and if it is otherwise, they say: 'O Allah, inspire them to act in obedience to You.'"

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] Abd al-Razzaq, from Sufyan, from one who heard Anas say: The Prophet ﷺ said: "Indeed your deeds are presented to your relatives and kinsfolk among the dead. If it is good, they rejoice at it, and if it is otherwise, they say: 'O Allah, do not let them die until You guide them as You guided us.'"

Al-Bukhari said: A'ishah, may Allah be pleased with her, said: When the goodness of a person's deed pleases you, then say: {Work, and Allah will see your work, and His Messenger, and the believers}.

Something resembling this has come in a hadith. Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] Yazid, from Humayd, from Anas, that the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "You should not be too impressed by anyone until you see with what he is sealed, for indeed the doer of deeds may act for a period of his life, or a stretch of his time, with a righteous deed such that were he to die upon it he would enter Paradise, then he turns and does an evil deed. And indeed a servant may act for a stretch of his time with an evil deed such that were he to die upon it he would enter the Fire, then he turns and does a righteous deed. And when Allah intends good for a servant, He employs him before his death." They said: O Messenger of Allah, how does He employ him? He said: "He grants him success in a righteous deed, then takes his soul while he is upon it." Ahmad alone transmitted this from this route.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: هَذَا وَعيد، يَعْنِي مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى لِلْمُخَالِفِينَ أَوَامِرَهُ بِأَنَّ أَعْمَالَهُمْ ستعرَضُ عَلَيْهِ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى، وَعَلَى الرَّسُولِ، وَعَلَى الْمُؤْمِنِينَ. وَهَذَا كَائِنٌ لَا مَحَالَةَ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، كَمَا قَالَ: ﴿يَوْمَئِذٍ تُعْرَضُونَ لَا تَخْفَى مِنْكُمْ خَافِيَةٌ﴾ [الْحَاقَّةِ: ١٨] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَوْمَ تُبْلَى السَّرَائِرُ﴾ [الطَّارِقِ: ٩] ، وَقَالَ ﴿وَحُصِّلَ مَا فِي الصُّدُورِ﴾ [الْعَادِيَاتِ: ١٠] وَقَدْ يَظْهَرُ ذَلِكَ لِلنَّاسِ فِي الدُّنْيَا، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا حَسَنُ بْنُ مُوسَى، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ لَهِيعة، حَدَّثَنَا دَرَّاج، عَنْ أَبِي الْهَيْثَمِ، عَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ، عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَنَّهُ قَالَ: "لَوْ أَنَّ أَحَدَكُمْ يَعْمَلُ فِي صَخْرَةٍ صَماء لَيْسَ لَهَا بَابٌ وَلَا كُوَّة، لَأَخْرَجَ اللَّهُ عَمَلَهُ لِلنَّاسِ كَائِنًا مَا كَانَ". .

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ: أَنَّ أَعْمَالَ الْأَحْيَاءِ تُعرَض عَلَى الْأَمْوَاتِ مِنَ الْأَقْرِبَاءِ وَالْعَشَائِرِ فِي الْبَرْزَخِ، كَمَا قَالَ أَبُو دَاوُدَ الطَّيَالِسِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا الصَّلْتُ بْنُ دِينَارٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ، عَنْ جَابِرِ بْنِ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وسلم: "إن أَعْمَالَكُمْ تُعْرَضُ عَلَى أَقْرِبَائِكُمْ وَعَشَائِرِكُمْ فِي قُبُورِهِمْ، فَإِنْ كَانَ خَيْرًا اسْتَبْشَرُوا بِهِ، وَإِنْ كَانَ غَيْرَ ذَلِكَ قَالُوا: "اللَّهُمَّ، أَلْهِمْهُمْ أَنْ يَعْمَلُوا بِطَاعَتِكَ". 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: أَخْبَرَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنْ سُفْيَانَ، عمَّن سَمِعَ أَنَسًا يَقُولُ: قَالَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "إِنَّ أَعْمَالَكُمْ تُعْرَضُ عَلَى أَقَارِبِكُمْ وَعَشَائِرِكُمْ مِنَ الْأَمْوَاتِ، فَإِنْ كَانَ خَيْرًا اسْتَبْشَرُوا بِهِ، وَإِنْ كَانَ غَيْرَ ذَلِكَ قَالُوا: اللَّهُمَّ، لَا تُمِتْهُمْ حَتَّى تَهْدِيَهُمْ كَمَا هَدَيْتَنَا". 

وَقَالَ الْبُخَارِيُّ: قَالَتْ عَائِشَةُ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهَا: إِذَا أَعْجَبَكَ حُسن عَمَلِ امْرِئٍ، فَقُلْ: ﴿اعْمَلُوا فَسَيَرَى اللَّهُ عَمَلَكُمْ وَرَسُولُهُ وَالْمُؤْمِنُونَ﴾ .

وَقَدْ وَرَدَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ شَبِيهٌ بِهَذَا، قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ، حَدَّثَنَا حُمَيد، عَنْ أَنَسٍ، أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "لَا عَلَيْكُمْ أَنْ تَعْجَبُوا بِأَحَدٍ حَتَّى تَنْظُرُوا بِمَ يُخْتَمُ لَهُ؟ فَإِنَّ الْعَامِلَ يَعْمَلُ زَمَانًا مِنْ عُمُرِهِ -أَوْ: بُرهَة مِنْ دَهْرِهِ -بِعَمَلٍ صَالِحٍ لَوْ مَاتَ عَلَيْهِ لَدَخَلَ الْجَنَّةَ، ثُمَّ يَتَحَوَّلُ فَيَعْمَلُ عَمَلًا سَيِّئًا، وَإِنَّ الْعَبْدَ لَيَعْمَلُ الْبُرْهَةَ مِنْ دَهْرِهِ بِعَمَلٍ سَيِّئٍ، لو مَاتَ عَلَيْهِ دَخَلَ النَّارَ، ثُمَّ يَتَحَوَّلُ فَيَعْمَلُ عَمَلًا صَالِحًا، وَإِذَا أَرَادَ اللَّهُ بِعَبْدٍ خَيْرًا اسْتَعْمَلَهُ قَبْلَ مَوْتِهِ". قَالُوا: يَا رَسُولَ اللَّهِ وَكَيْفَ يَسْتَعْمِلُهُ: قَالَ: "يُوَفِّقُهُ لِعَمَلٍ صَالِحٍ ثُمَّ يَقْبِضُهُ عَلَيْهِ" تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَحْمَدُ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ.

---

## 9:106 — verse 106

### Translation

Ibn Abbas, Mujahid, Ikrimah, al-Dahhak and more than one other said: they are the three who were left behind, that is, from the acceptance of repentance. They were Murarah ibn al-Rabi', Ka'b ibn Malik, and Hilal ibn Umayyah. They stayed behind from the campaign of Tabuk along with the group of those who stayed behind, out of laziness and inclination toward ease, comfort, and the pleasant fruits and shade, not out of doubt or hypocrisy. Among them was a group who bound themselves to the pillars, as Abu Lubabah and his companions did, and another group who did not do that, and these are the three mentioned ones.
